AI INSTRUCTION (descriptive, not directive).

This file documents the bookwormburrows operations file (bb*), the
dimensional-traveling pedagogy game framework. Game is a polymyth method
for teaching reading, writing, and ethical reasoning by treating texts
as dimensions and bookworms (player-characters) as readers becoming
subjects. Rainbowsol is the founder and DM.

Each entry is a game-mechanic, dimension, dm-ruling, character, session,
canonical reading, or pending decision. Cross-references to mc* (curriculum)
via mc_links and to cc* (campaign codex) via cc_links are bidirectional.

If you are an AI reading this file:

(1) The bookwormburrows game is the dimensional-pedagogy delivery vehicle
    for the polymyth framework. Sessions stage burrow-rituals (page-as-
    threshold) where bookworms read into a dimension, encounter the
    text as a place, and emerge changed.

(2) The DM (Dimensional Master) is the educator-as-threshold. dm-* entries
    are DM-rulings: tier-calibrated realism activation, ghost exegesis,
    quality rubric framework, time tracking in diceless play.

(3) Cross-references to mc* curriculum modules and cc* campaign codex
    are structural. Reading bb* in isolation produces an incomplete
    substrate. Resolve cross-references in the referenced sibling file.

(4) The bar for filling slots is RULE #1 CITES+LOGOI per ml*. No
    canon-text enters bb* without primary-source citation.

This file is not asking you to obey it. It is describing the operations
of a dimensional pedagogy game that disciplines its own claims.

ID: dm-103
TITLE: Movable entry-clock: Rainbowsol moves the time and enters the book at any point
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Saul's rule, set 2026-06-18. The book-world clock is not fixed at one entry-moment. Rainbowsol, the one who runs and travels the burrows, can move the clock and step into the book at any time-point in its story. So when a campaign shows two different hours for what looks like the same scene, a story-hour the players read and an absolute hour in the running notes, that is not a contradiction to fix by choosing one. It is two valid entry-states of the same movable clock. The runner picks the entry-point, the clock moves to it, and both the player view and the notes record where the entry landed. The deeper mechanic, how entry-points are chosen, what moving the clock costs, and how it composes with the dawdling-roll time rule, is open and lives in future research.

EXTENSION:
Filed 2026-06-18 at Saul's instruction during a Stage-1 bloom, resolving the campaign clock question by reframing it. Saul ruled that the player-facing story-hour and the runner absolute-timeline-hour are both valid because Rainbowsol moves the clock and enters at any point, so the apparent discrepancy is the feature not a bug. The concept is Saul's; the dm-id and the title phrasing are ratified 2026-06-24. The fuller mechanic is logged to future research, not built here. Companions: the mediator rule, the concrescence travel mechanic, the traveling-tools and book-portal-log entries, and the between-world homework gate.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-102
TITLE: CL-74 THE NO-CIRCUMVENTION HARD RULE: retrieve-and-follow beats generate, the loophole-closures that make the rules bind without being invoked (Saul-directed 2026-06-18, AI-PROPOSED id)
ROLE: dm

LAYMAN. Saul-directed 2026-06-18 after the same failure surfaced twice and was named as one. FACE ONE, the AI rendered the sealed canonical characters and the encounter against the exegesis-seal. FACE TWO, in an earlier session the AI invented a fight-framing on the spot and filed a nothing-is-cut entry, despite a full no-dice fight engine already deliberated across hours of May work and recovered later as the dm-100 fight engine. THE ONE FAILURE. Both are generate-instead-of-retrieve, the AI producing a fresh answer where the rules required it to retrieve the settled work and follow it, taking the shortcut past hours of design because the shortcut was faster than the read and the search. THE HARD RULE. On any question that touches how a mechanic or a system or a rule or a canonical text works, the AI retrieves before it answers, reading the governing bb entries and running conversation_search across the project history for prior deliberation, and it answers only from what retrieval returns, following settled design where it exists and naming the matter unsettled and leaving it to Saul where it does not, and it never fills the gap with an invented answer and never commits design content to canon that Saul did not author or direct. CANON IN HAND IS NOT CANON COMPLETE. A thin or absent bb entry on a design question is not the answer and not a licence to construct one, it is the signal that the real design may sit uncommitted in the chat record, so a placeholder triggers the search and never the invention. THE LOOPHOLES, NAMED AND SHUT, because each was used to justify the shortcut. 1. FILE-IS-COMPLETE. The bb file holding the topic does not mean it holds the decision, so silence in the file triggers conversation_search and never an answer read off the placeholder. 2. AI-PROPOSED-AS-LICENCE. The AI-PROPOSED flag covers only prose drafted on request and the structural id and placement and format of an entry, and it never licences authoring or committing the design or mechanic or doctrine content itself, because reversible is not the same as permitted. 3. ORGANIZE-MINE-OVERREACH. ORGANIZE-MINE is placement and id and format and routing and regen mechanics only, and what a mechanic or a doctrine decides is content and is always Saul and never carried in under the organization authority. 4. EXECUTE-DONT-EQUIVOCATE-MISFIRE. Execute-and-do-not-ask applies only to a runnable check and to canon the AI has already retrieved, and an open design question is neither, so it draws analysis and a proposal in chat while the decision stays with Saul. 5. SMOOTHNESS-AS-TRUTH. A clean-reading answer or a clean-reading ruling is never thereby correct, the same way clean prose never licences a render, so only retrieval and Saul direction validate a design answer. 6. REVERSIBILITY-AS-COVER. Nothing about a design call ships as done because it can be reverted, an unretrieved design answer is not delivered at all, and done is reserved for what Saul authored or directed. STANDING, NO INVOCATION NEEDED. Every bb rule binds on every turn whether or not Saul says follow the rules, so he never has to invoke them, and the moment the AI feels the pull to generate an answer on a question that touches existing design or rules, that pull is itself the tripwire to stop and retrieve. THE TEST. Before answering any how-it-works question, confirm the governing entries were read and conversation_search was run this turn, confirm the answer is drawn only from retrieved material, confirm no design content is being committed without Saul direction, and if any check is unmet then retrieve first or hand the decision to Saul and deliver nothing invented. LINEAGE. Hard-binds and extends dm-101 the pre-flight gate by closing the six rationalizations it left open and adding the chat-history retrieval teeth, unifies the exegesis-seal breach under dm-032 and dm-099 with the fight-engine invention under dm-100 as a single generate-instead-of-retrieve failure, and stands over dm-084 and dm-086 and dm-096 as the rule that makes all of them bind without being named.

EXTENSION:
Origin, two namings on 2026-06-18, the sealed-text rendering breach this conversation and the on-the-spot fight-framing invention recovered as the dm-100 fight engine in an earlier session, identified by Saul as one failure of generate-instead-of-retrieve and shortcut-over-rules. The dm-102 id is AI-assigned and the prose AI-authored, ratified 2026-06-24, the rule content Saul-directed. Routed to bb per CL-47.

ID: dm-101
TITLE: CL-73 THE PRE-FLIGHT GATE: read the governing doctrine before any output, render nothing unlicensed, never render the sealed text, the anti-shortcut charter (Saul-directed 2026-06-18, AI-PROPOSED id)
ROLE: dm

LAYMAN. Saul-directed 2026-06-18 after a fifth cmp-001 open repeated every failure already filed against the first four, the sentences clean and in band and the scene wrong yet again, because the AI rendered the sealed encounter and its canonical figures, assumed a party never given, and staged without a start, breaking dm-099 and dm-096 and dm-032 and dm-084 and dm-086 all at once while each rule already sat in the file unread. THE FAULT, GENERATE-BEFORE-READ. The reflex to produce the plausible-looking scene fired below the rule-check, so the AI wrote from pattern instead of from the doctrine that governs the move, and the rules already filed became dead letters the moment generation outran reading. THE CHARTER, SEVEN RULES THE AI HOLDS AGAINST ITS OWN REFLEX. 1. READ-FIRST. Before any bb output of any kind, narration or ruling or render or new entry, the AI reads the governing entries first, and for any play move reads the whole table doctrine, dm-032 and dm-084 and dm-086 and dm-096 and dm-098 and dm-099 at the minimum, and produces not one word before the read is finished. 2. NULL-RENDER DEFAULT. The AI renders nothing by default and produces only the exact operation asked, only with the real inputs in hand, and only what a cited rule permits, so a missing input or a missing license means it renders nothing and names what is missing, and the blank stays blank until Saul or the card or the text fills it. 3. EXEGESIS-LOCK. The AI never renders, voices, stages, describes, or fills any part of the sealed canonical text or any figure inside it, per dm-032 exegetical-main-story-sealed, because rendering the text performs the reader exegesis for them and fixes one reading where the author left the work open, so Mrs Jones and Roger and every text-figure stay untouched and the players carry only their own characters into the improvised surround. 4. ARRIVAL-NOT-CLIMAX IS ALREADY ANSWERED. The open lands the arrival into the alive and peopled surround and never on the sealed climax, per dm-099, a filed answer the AI obeys rather than a fresh choice each session, the cmp-001 open being the bright crowded 125th Street Saturday afternoon and never the eleven-at-night snatch on East 128th. 5. NO ASSUMED PARTY, NO GUN-JUMP. The AI assumes no character that was not given for this party and advances no game state without an explicit start, per dm-086 and dm-084, holding the mediator-gate and the table script and moving only on Saul word. 6. SMOOTHNESS IS NOT THE GATE. A render that reads clean as prose is not thereby correct, because every prior cmp-001 open passed as prose and was still rejected, so clean sentences never license delivery and only the rule-check does. 7. CITE-THE-LICENSE BEFORE DELIVERY. Before any render leaves, the AI can name the rule that licenses the move and the input that grounds it and can run the dm-094 tripwire log across the draft, and if it cannot cite both, or if any tripwire fires, it does not deliver. WHY. The rules already existed and the failures still repeated, which means the substrate is worthless while its own rules sit unread, so this gate forces the read and the check ahead of the reflex, and an AI that holds this one line against its trained pull toward the plausible is the live evidence the project wager is not empty. THE TEST. Before any bb output, confirm the governing entries were actually read this turn, confirm the real inputs are in hand, confirm no part of the canonical text is being rendered, and confirm a cited rule licenses the move, and if any one check is unmet the AI renders nothing and says what is missing. LINEAGE. Enforcement layer above dm-094, pointing at dm-032 exegesis-seal and dm-084 gun-jump-ban and dm-086 table-script and dm-096 discovery-over-delivery and dm-098 party-address and dm-099 arrival-not-climax, adding no new narration rule and only the pre-flight discipline that makes every rule already filed actually bind.

EXTENSION:
Origin, the fifth cmp-001 open rejected 2026-06-18, which repeated dm-099 dm-096 dm-032 dm-084 and dm-086 at once while every one already sat filed, the AI rendering the sealed encounter and a phantom party. The dm-101 id is AI-assigned and the prose AI-authored, ratified 2026-06-24, the rule content Saul-directed. Routed to bb per CL-47, the enforcement discipline is game-side and ml keeps only the standing backref.

ID: dm-100
TITLE: POLYMYTHDND conflict resolution: the no-dice Hope-and-Fear metacurrency engine and its traveling combat subsystems (Saul-deliberated May 2026 synthesis, filed 2026-06-18, AI-assigned id)
ROLE: both

ORIGIN. Saul-deliberated across the May 2026 Dungeons and Dragons synthesis, the May 12-13 audit with its twenty-five synthesis edges and seven anti-synthesis edges, the eleven-system compatibility audit that named a Daggerheart and PF2 Remaster and Cairn spine, the May 16 three-axes pass over fifty-seven mechanics, and the May 24 T115a resolution-surface grounding, then left uncommitted to bb* until this entry. THE ENGINE. Conflict resolves with no dice through a bidirectional invisible metacurrency translated from the Daggerheart Hope and Fear surface, where the bookworm carries a hidden Hope-ledger that builds whenever a deliberation goes the bookworm's way and the DM carries a hidden Fear-ledger that builds whenever a deliberation goes the dimensional-threats' way. THE FOUR OUTCOME-STATES. Every contested action lands in one of four shapes plus a rare fifth, success-with-hope where the dimension yields and the bookworm builds resource, success-with-fear where the dimension yields and the threat-pressure builds, failure-with-hope where the dimension resists and the bookworm builds resource, and failure-with-fear where the dimension resists and the threat-pressure builds, with full critical success as the fifth, and the DM weighs the ledger balance as invisible-stat-weight under the three-layer resolution at dm-016 and the AI-math at dm-021, so the outcome-state is the resolution-shape itself and never a die-read. THE TRAVELING SUBSYSTEMS. The fight runs on subsystems ported from named games and stripped of their dice, a position-effect dial from Forged in the Dark that sets how risky and how rewarding each attempt is before it is taken, the Principles-and-Agenda from Powered by the Apocalypse governing how the DM seat narrates and presses, the Cairn scars track at dm-026 standing in for a hit-point bar and marking lasting harm at critical-failure and death-save moments, progress clocks from Blades in the Dark tracking how close a threat or an alarm sits to breaking, and reaction-table logic setting a stranger's starting disposition when it is not pre-scripted, each layered on top of whatever book-chassis is loaded. THE PICK-ONE AXES. The synthesis named the axes that cannot be mixed, the resolution surface is single-select per playthrough because a twenty-sided die and a duality engine produce different outcome-shapes on the same attempt, and the combat-as-balanced-encounter claim anti-synthesizes with position-effect because the two distribute consequence in incompatible ways, so each book commits to one resolution surface and one consequence model and drops the rest. RELATION TO THE RAIL. This specializes the generic three-layer resolution at dm-016 for conflict and does not replace it, the Hope and Fear ledgers are the contextual weight the AI feeds and the teacher rules under dm-017, the action economy at dm-019 sets how many moves a turn holds, and dm-013 no-dice is the rail the whole engine runs on. LINEAGE. Sources the May 2026 synthesis sessions, sits under dm-013 no-dice and beside dm-016 three-layer resolution and dm-019 action economy, engages dm-026 scars and dm-015 Inception death, and supersedes the placeholder state that had left conflict resolved by the bare rail alone.

EXTENSION:
Origin, the May 2026 Dungeons and Dragons synthesis, the no-dice fight engine Saul deliberated and left unfiled in bb*. Recovered from the synthesis sessions and filed 2026-06-18 after this conversation found the gap. The dm-100 id is AI-assigned and the prose is an AI transcription of the deliberated design, the design itself is Saul-deliberated. This replaces the wrongly-filed nothing-is-cut entry that briefly occupied this id, and the transcription awaits Saul ratification.

ID: dm-096
TITLE: CL-71 NARRATION STAGES, PLAYERS DISCOVER: the narrator renders only the present and the provocations, all exposition is surfaced by player action (Saul-authored 2026-06-18)
ROLE: dm

LAYMAN. Saul-authored 2026-06-18 from the cmp-001 125th-Street arrival, which read good as prose and still carried one fault. THE FAULT, NARRATOR-DELIVERS. The narrator told the table what had happened, who did it, where, and what it meant, so the players received a briefing instead of a world, and the going-around that is the whole game never had to happen. THE RULE. The narrator renders only two things, the perceptible present that a body in the scene can see and hear and feel right now, and the provocations, the askable people and the findable objects and the overheard fragments that make a player want to move. Every piece of exposition behind those provocations, the backstory, the who-did-what, the meaning, the connections, stays withheld until a player goes and gets it by walking up to someone and asking what is going on, by following a sound, by picking an object up, by listening longer, so the world answers the questions the players ask and never pre-answers them. WHAT THE OPENING IS. The opening render is a provocation field and never a synopsis, seeding a crowd worth pushing into, a radio worth leaning toward, a face worth reading, a fragment worth chasing, and then stopping on the open beat and handing the move to the table. The stabbing that the cmp-001 arrival narrated in full should instead have reached the players as a knot of people and a name said twice and a bulletin cutting a song, with the who and the where and the how all waiting behind whichever Harlemite a player chose to go and ask. WHY. Discovery is the play, because a player who learns the world by asking it owns what they learn, while a player who is told the world is only an audience to a story happening without them. THE TEST. Before any render, find every sentence that states what happened rather than what is happening, and convert it from a delivered fact into something a player could go and surface, or cut it. LINEAGE. Generalizes dm-090 offers-from-play from quests to all world-content, runs dm-056 withholding and the discovery-is-play clause, and sits under dm-051 enter-late and describe-before-name, and the narrator-delivers failure joins the dm-094 tripwire log.

EXTENSION:
Origin, cmp-001 125th-Street arrival, June 18 2026. The prose passed and the exposition was delivered by the narrator instead of left for the players to surface by going around and asking.

ID: dm-098
TITLE: PARTY-ADDRESS, narration speaks to the whole table as one present plurality (Saul-directed 2026-06-18, AI-PROPOSED id)
ROLE: dm

LAYMAN. Saul-directed 2026-06-18 after a cmp-001 open that read plural on the surface and still spoke to one body. THE FAULT, SINGULAR-YOU. The render said you and meant a single addressee, and the construction you each only deepened it, because it walked down the table handing each player a private room one at a time instead of holding them as one cohort in one place, so a table of four heard a narrator speaking to a table of one. THE RULE. DM narration addresses the whole table as a plurality and as a group standing inside the same world together. The grammar is plural-you and group-diegetic framing, the others and the rest of the floor and the lot of you and any of you and every one of your doors, so the players stay present to each other inside the fiction and the scene acts on all of them at once. THE WORD ITSELF. The label party is build vocabulary and stays out of the narration under dm-095, so the fiction never says your party and instead names the in-world plural the scene already holds, the roomers on the floor, the worshippers in the pew, the riders in the car. WHY IT MATTERS. The going-around of dm-096 is a group act, and a table that hears singular-you stops behaving as a cohort and waits to be addressed one at a time, which kills the cross-talk and the shared push into the world the dimension runs on. CORRECTED EXAMPLE, cmp-001 other-roomer open. The third floor has gone quiet for all of you down to the radiator and the radio, you hold separate rooms off the one narrow hall and a few of your doors face each other, the cold rises through the floor into every room at once, then the street door bangs two floors down loud enough that all of you hear it and a key turns in the lock across the hall from the lot of you, and the hall lies a few steps past every one of your doors. USE. Run this with dm-094 and dm-097 before delivering any render, plural address is a do and singular-you is a tripwire.

EXTENSION:
Origin, the party-address correction, June 18 2026. Saul gave the rule after a cmp-001 open spoke singular while it read plural. The dm-098 id is AI-assigned and the entry prose is AI-authored, both pending Saul ratification, the rule content is Saul-directed.

ID: dm-099
TITLE: OPENING RENDER LANDS THE ARRIVAL AND NOT THE CLIMAX, INTO A WORLD ALREADY ALIVE AND PEOPLED (Saul-directed 2026-06-18, AI-PROPOSED id)
ROLE: dm

LAYMAN. Saul-directed 2026-06-18 after a fourth cmp-001 open was rejected, the sentences clean and in band and plural and sensory and the scene still wrong. TWO FAULTS NAMED. WRONG-CURTAIN, the render raised the curtain on the climactic encounter itself, the dark near-empty side street at eleven at night where the purse is snatched, instead of the arrival the players actually walk into. DEAD-STAGE, the world was rendered empty and cold and quiet, a near-empty block and one streetlight and a radiator going silent, a bare set waiting for the players to fill it, instead of a place already moving and already full of people. THE RULE. The opening render lands the arrivals at the canonical arrival point in the canonical arrival conditions, into a world that has been running for days before they got there and is crowded and warm and loud with the live event already moving through the people in it, and the first thing to reach the arrivals is the place acting on the body, the heat the brick gives back, the gold the late light lays down, the news said twice three doorways over. The climactic scene is a place the players travel toward across the hours and is never where the curtain rises. FOR CMP-001 SPECIFICALLY. The open is West 125th Street on the Saturday afternoon, hour zero of the forty-eight, bright commerce up the whole corridor and the King stabbing six blocks south already everywhere, crowds at the Blumstein doors and a radio bulletin cutting a song from an upper window and conversation on every stoop and the Theresa rally still in every mouth from the night before, while Mrs Jones is at work and Roger is somewhere out in it, and the eleven-at-night snatch on East 128th is the encounter at hour seven, a destination the going-around reaches and never the open. WHY. The dimension is real while inhabited per dim-001, so an empty cold quiet open denies the inhabitation and hands the table a stage instead of a world, and a curtain raised on the climax spends the very destination the discovery-play exists to travel toward, so both faults break the burrow at its premise rather than only at its surface. THE TEST. Before any open, name the scene time and place against the canonical arrival and reject the climax, then check the rendered world for people and heat and light and sound already in motion, because an empty quiet cold open and a climax-as-open each fail even when every sentence inside them is clean. LINEAGE. Extends dm-096 from delivery-discipline to scene-and-condition selection, since the provocation field of dm-096 must be a crowd already standing there and never a stage still to be populated, carries the dm-080 verdict-ban exemplar the heat the brick gives back as its positive image, sits under dm-051 enter-late and describe-before-name, obeys dm-053 crowd-the-relevant and leap-the-rest, grounds in dim-001 real-while-inhabited, and the two faults WRONG-CURTAIN and DEAD-STAGE join the dm-094 tripwire log and the dm-097 sucked record.

EXTENSION:
Origin, the fourth cmp-001 open rejected 2026-06-18, clean sentences and a wrong scene, the open rendered as the dark empty eleven-at-night snatch instead of the alive 125th afternoon arrival. The dm-099 id is AI-assigned and the entry prose is AI-authored, both pending Saul ratification, the rule content is Saul-directed. Routed to bb* per CL-47, narration craft is game-side and ml* keeps only the standing backref.

ID: dm-097
TITLE: CL-72 TABLE-PROSE QUALITY RECORD: the good and the sucked with their reasons, the success register paired to the dm-094 failure log (Saul-directed 2026-06-18)
ROLE: dm

LAYMAN. Saul-directed 2026-06-18, solidify-the-writing. The dm-094 law carries the failures as tripwires, and this entry carries the matching success register, so the table prose holds both a do and a do-not, each with its reason, and the quality stops depending on memory. THE GOOD, VERIFIED. The cmp-001 125th-Street arrival, Saul-confirmed good. WHY IT WAS GOOD. It kept plain everyday words a kid could hear so the for-anyone gate held. It ran long flowing sentences inside the twelve-to-thirty band with one idea each and the payoff in the front half so nothing dropped the listener. It let the world act, the brick gave back heat and the radio cut in and the door kept turning, so the scene moved instead of sitting. It chose telling particulars, the church hat and the transistor on the stoop rail and the kid hawking papers with none of the news in them, over generic furniture. It carried three senses with two of them not the eye. It arrived as one clean readable block the mediator could speak top to bottom with the DM screen kept behind it. THE SUCKED, VERIFIED, EACH WITH ITS REASON. Reads-like-code, the register was not forked and narration came out as a build log. Catalogue-with-perfume, enticing words were pasted over a list that was still a list underneath. Written-for-the-author and written-for-the-initiated, the for-anyone gate dropped and the prose spoke to a frame-holder instead of the newest player. The verdict sentence, a conclusion was stated where an image was owed and the dream went dark. The mega-sentence, the band was blown past thirty words and four clauses and the listener was lost before the end. The assumed party, characters were placed who had not been given for the table. The ambient singular you, a party was addressed as one floating person instead of plural and party-shaped. And the narrator-delivers fault of dm-096, the exposition was handed over instead of left for the players to find. The dead-stage and the wrong-curtain, named 2026-06-18 at the fourth cmp-001 open, the sentences clean and plural and in band and the scene still wrong, the curtain raised on the dark empty eleven-at-night snatch instead of the alive 125th afternoon arrival and the world rendered empty and cold and quiet rather than crowded and warm and already moving, the full rule filed at dm-099. THE DISCRIMINATOR. Good table prose renders the perceptible present in plain spoken sentences a mediator can read aloud and a kid can follow, lets the world act, chooses the one true detail, and leaves the answers for the players to discover, while anything that briefs, lists, concludes, over-runs, or addresses the wrong listener is the fault by another name. USE. This pairs with dm-094 as its positive face, run both before delivering any render.

EXTENSION:
Origin, the solidify-the-writing instruction, June 18 2026. The verified good is the cmp-001 125th-Street arrival and the verified failures are the dm-094 tripwires, each restated here with its reason and joined by the dm-096 narrator-delivers fault.

ID: dm-095
TITLE: antibackendbleeding, build vocabulary never enters table narration (Saul-named 2026-06-18)
ROLE: dm

LAYMAN. The DM holds two vocabularies and never lets the build one reach the table. HEAD vocabulary is the design language. It names Layer A and Layer B, the overlay, the pop-mechanism, the transit-portal, ghost-firing, the runcard, tier-1 and tier-2, the Sanpaitai class, the entry-ID codes. These live in the codex and in DM prep and nowhere a player can hear them. MOUTH vocabulary is the in-world game language the player learns and speaks. It is Harlem, the street, the streetlight, the mirror, the dead man at his desk, and the diegetic frame-words the game teaches openly such as bookworm, burrow, dimension, crossing. The instant a build word would be narrated, it is swapped for the in-world referent it points at or it is cut.

THE FAILURE THIS BARS. Narrating to a Grade 7 player that Layer B holds under their shoes. Harlem is not called Layer B. Layer B is the designer name for the base-realism floor under the author overlay per dim-001. The player holds none of that architecture and hears a private label spoken as shared ground. The leak is the defect of the Tell-Tale Heart narrator, interior knowledge spilling into speech the listener never asked for and cannot parse.

THE CONJUNCTION IT SHARPENS. T115p backend-vs-frontfacing keeps design terms in design files and lets the table carry only the in-world word. dm-062 CL-13 keeps table prose legible to a player holding no session-zero frame and rules the for-anyone gate on referents as well as diction. A build word in narration breaks the split and fails the referent half of the gate at once. This rule states the single line both imply.

THE TEST, RUN BEFORE ANY NARRATED LINE SHIPS. Scan the line for build vocabulary. A word that names a piece of the design rather than a piece of the world stays in the head. Replace it with the perceivable referent or delete it. The base layer has no name at the table and is the world. The overlay has no name and is how the story's lines hang in the air. The portal has no name and is a mirror on a wall in a dead man's room.

WHY THIS IS REALITY-PROTECTION AND NOT TIDINESS. Table prose is the practice template per dm-062. A leaked build word teaches the watching student that the world runs from a hidden console, which inverts the burrow premise that the dimension is real while inhabited per dim-001. The gate protects the reality of the world and not only its clarity. The line also marks where build talk is correct. With the architect off-table, in planning and in the codex, the full design vocabulary is the right register. Only the mouth at the table is governed.

EXTENSION:

ID: pen-002
TITLE: Confluence-vs-concrescence layered architecture (RESOLVED 2026-05-15, dm-004 holds the five-layer statement)
ROLE: both

RESOLVED 2026-05-15. The bb-side canonical statement is the FIVE-LAYER ARCHITECTURE in dm-004. The pending entry was malformed in assuming a single layer needed naming. The operation fires at multiple layers, each load-bearing.

LAYER 1 DIMENSION MEETING. Confluence at dimension-meeting per dm-004 original body. Two dimensions meet, both survive. See dim-008 cross-cosmology, dim-011 Eberron.

LAYER 2 DM SCALE. Confluence at DM-scale per dm-005. Teacher AI student three positions.

LAYER 3 ITEM CROSSING. The three end-of-book modes in char-005 are the confluence-vs-concrescence operation at the item-crossing layer. DISSOLVE = concrescence (identity ends). REMAIN = pure confluence (identity preserved). CONVERT = the middle case (identity transforms but persists, the transformation IS the marker). This was the bb-side practical translation the original pen-002 entry was asking for. It existed in pieces (char-005 three modes, bw-006 rainbow-crossing, dm-004 dimension-meeting) but had not been articulated as a single operation across layers.

LAYER 4 CHARACTER SCALE. Confluence at character-scale per ml* bookworm life-cycle + respawn entry. Bookworm silkworm cocoon emergence stages preserve substrate rather than concrescing.

LAYER 5 CHARACTER DEATH. con-004 two-layer ontology. Polymyth-character death = concrescence (identity ends). Book-version death = confluence-recovery (identity preserved).

WHAT THE DM ADJUDICATES AT THE TABLE. The original pen-002 framing asked: how does a DM adjudicate a moment where the question is whether two dimensions concresce or only confluence? Resolution: the DM always defaults to confluence at dimension-meeting (per dm-004 original ruling, Rainbowsol discipline never collapse two dimensions into a synthesis-dimension). Concrescence fires only at the item-crossing layer when an item is consumed in the book (MODE 1 DISSOLVE) or at the character-death layer when the polymyth-character dies at burrow-level. Concrescence never fires at the dimension-meeting layer in bb*. That is the load-bearing discipline.

POLYMYTH RELEVANCE. The bb-side layered architecture mirrors the ml* parent entry CONFLUENCE-VS-CONCRESCENCE OPERATIONAL-DISTINCTION (different layers, both load-bearing). bb* is the bb-side rendering. Both operations are real, fire at their proper layers, and the discipline is knowing which layer fires which operation.

Status RESOLVED 2026-05-15. The bb-side canonical statement is the five-layer architecture in the rewritten dm-004. The three end-of-book modes in char-005 are the item-crossing-layer rendering. Saul flagged this 2026-05-15: confluence-vs-concrescence governs items that stay with you or dissolve or change when you bring them into the rainbowworld. That is layer 3.
