ID: dm-031
TITLE: Leveling system ruling — XP-as-evidence-record, two clocks (bookworm + character), no human-attribute fields
ROLE: dm

DECISION HELD. bb* leveling system operates on XP-as-evidence-record, not XP-as-currency. Numbers do not buy advances. The corpus (writing, journal entries, character-action results, smashes, scars) is the evidence base. The teacher (human reader, not math) declares stage transitions at qualitative thresholds.

TWO CLOCKS, NOT ONE LADDER. (1) BOOKWORM clock. The student-subject moves through bookworm -> silkworm -> cocoon -> self-named-emergence -> eggs-on-mulberry-recursion (see bw-007, bw-008). Years-long. Gated by qualitative tests: fibroin-test for silkworm, self-named act for emergence. No numbers. (2) CHARACTER clock. The character-at-table is local to one campaign. Dies inside one campaign. Earns moves per session that die when the character dies. Two clocks tracked separately. Welding both onto one 10-level ladder forces a silkworm-stage bookworm playing a fresh character to perform "level 1" and forces a long-running character to perform cocoon-resistance the bookworm has not earned. Wrong.

OSSD CLOCK ROUTING. Third clock (OSSD/IB credit-codes) lives in mc*, not bb*. If bb* tracked OSSD codes mechanically, bb* would become mc* with character sheets glued on. The empty mc* is the structural pressure that bb* must resist absorbing.

WHAT THE BOOKWORMCARD TRACKS. Per pen-013 resolution, items split RAINBOW (carry forward) vs Consumable (one-book). Per char-005, three end-of-book modes (dissolve / convert / remain). Per the May 13 SERIES->BOOKS-COMPLETED rename, the top-of-card metadata records the bookworm's burrow-count, not a "series number" that referred to nothing. Books completed IS an XP-as-evidence-record artifact. Not spendable. Documentation that there is a corpus.

WHAT THE BOOKWORMCARD DOES NOT TRACK. Hair color, eye color, height. Per May 13 ruling these are nullified — bookwormburrows characters are smashed-up ideas from other characters, not humans. APPEARANCE remains a single-line prompt for the smash-resultant form, not a human-attribute grid.

OPEN. (1) Framings D and E from May 4 chat 0f3705ce — recovery attempted May 13 2026 via conversation_search across multiple axes (framing D, framing E, portfolio-as-progression, demonstrated capacity, earned-moves dimension-specific). Search returned the framing A/B/C bodies plus the Q3 question that referenced D and E by letter but no body content for D or E was indexed. Two interpretations: D and E were drafted but the chunks containing them are not search-indexed, or D and E were named in the Q3 plan but never bodied. Either way the substrate is recoverable by re-derivation from the F1 to F4 frictions (two-clocks principle, anti-book-counting, anti-spreadsheet, OSSD-routing) combined with the XP-as-evidence-record substrate. Rainbowsol can re-derive if needed. (2) Stage-transition rubric for bookworm clock — what qualitative-evidence-pattern triggers silkworm declaration, cocoon declaration, self-named-emergence declaration. Rainbowsol authorship required. (3) Earned-moves catalog for character clock — what specific moves can be earned per dimension per campaign. Per-dimension authorship required. (4) Relationship to portfolio-quality grading per the May 4 portfolio-as-leveling proposal — grades document the evidence-pattern, but do not convert to spendable XP. Rubric design pending.

CROSS-REFERENCE. ml* XP-as-evidence-record substrate-distinction entry. ml* schema-audit miss entry. ml* bw-002 cannibalistic-reading critique. bw-007 bookworm-vs-character continuity-vs-locality. pen-013 RAINBOW resolution. char-005 three-mode end-of-book. May 13 SERIES->BOOKS-COMPLETED rename in /bookwormcard/print/.

ID: dm-032
TITLE: Dimension build standard. The cmp-001 Thank You M’am methodology synthesized for future cmp-N dimensions
ROLE: dm

DIMENSION BUILD STANDARD. Synthesized May 24 2026 from the cmp-001 Thank You M’am build (April-May 2026). This entry is the canonical methodology any future cmp-N dimension follows. Eight stages, fifteen realism domains, two architectural commitments, one entry-portal class, one time-substrate, one schedule format, one DM-prep budget. The standard exists so cmp-002 (Bradbury, All Summer in a Day) and cmp-003 onward can be built without re-deriving the architecture from scratch.

WHY THE STANDARD EXISTS. cmp-001 was the first dimension built to the depth a bookworm can actually spawn into. 379 cc-cmp001-* entries, fifteen realism-inventory children, named documented historical NPCs at named places at specific times, mirror-portal entry mechanics, exegetical-main story sealed, surroundings improvised live. The build took two months of conversation and several layers of design discovery. None of the discovery needs to happen again. The methodology below condenses the discoveries into a process anyone (Saul, another teacher, an AI engine) can run.

STAGE 1. ANCHOR-TEXT SELECTION AND LOCKING. Pick the text. Read it. Identify the exegetical-main: the sealed-canonical sequence of events the dimension cannot rewrite. For cmp-001 the exegetical-main is the Mrs Jones-Roger encounter on East 128th Street between Madison and Park, 11:15 PM Saturday September 20 1958, through the kitchenette scene and the ten dollars and the door closing. Hughes’s text canonical. Bookworms can be near it, witness it, hear it through the wall, follow Roger after, but the sequence itself stays sealed. Stage 1 output: anchor-text bibliographic record plus exegetical-main beat sequence with timestamps.

STAGE 2. HISTORICAL-REAL OVERLAY. For text-set dimensions (not invented worlds), identify the documented historical context the text sits inside. For cmp-001 the September 17-23 1958 SCLC Northern fundraising week was identified as the load-bearing historical overlay (Stride Toward Freedom release Wednesday, Williams CME fundraiser Thursday, Hotel Theresa rally Friday, Blumstein’s book signing Saturday with the Curry stabbing at 3:20 PM, King in Harlem Hospital surgery 5:45-8:25 PM, Powell at Abyssinian Sunday morning). The historical overlay is the substrate the campaign window opens inside. Stage 2 output: lead-up week chronology plus named documented NPCs with primary-source citations.

STAGE 3. FIFTEEN-DOMAIN REALISM INVENTORY. For each domain, write a substantive entry catalogging period reality at full fidelity. PM13 from ml* governs: paint at full historical fidelity, teacher filters at delivery. The fifteen domains are: (1) Economic, (2) Linguistic, (3) Institutional, (4) Medical, (5) Spatial, (6) Social, (7) Political, (8) Cultural, (9) Religious, (10) Domestic / material-culture, (11) Legal, (12) Recreational, (13) Technological, (14) Environmental, (15) Educational. Each domain entry separates tier-1 elements (every playthrough, every age, full surface intensity) from tier-2 elements (surface on NPC-path-trigger, calibrate by bookworm-card band per dm-010). Stage 3 output: fifteen realism-domain entries each with primary-source citations and tier separation.

STAGE 4. SPATIAL GRID AND ENCOUNTER-BLOCK LOCKING. Build the block-level geography. For cmp-001 the four-avenue grid (Fifth, Lenox, Seventh, Eighth between 110th and 155th), the two core blocks (20 East 127th = Hughes house, East 128th between Madison and Park = encounter block), the Park Avenue viaduct, the 125th Street retail spine, Mrs Jones’s walk-home route (Theresa to East 128th, around 7 blocks, around 15 minutes). Period-typical kitchenette interior documented from DeCarava photographs. Lighting and sound for the encounter beat documented at hour-level fidelity. Stage 4 output: spatial-realism entry plus named-location entries with NYC LPC and NRHP designation citations where they exist.

STAGE 5. MIRROR-PORTAL ENTRY MECHANICS. The universal portal class for bookworm entry into a dimension is the mirror. For cmp-001 the kitchenette mirror inside Mrs Jones’s room is the Layer A crossing-point: a Sanpaitai (a bookworm carrying the layer-A overlay) crosses by stepping through the mirror, applying the overlay in the act of crossing. The Hughes-house workroom mirror is the transit-portal between layers: crossing it lifts Layer A and drops the bookworm into Layer B where Hughes is physically present at the desk drafting. The mirror-as-portal class is the polymythdnd-canonical entry mechanism. Other dimensions can use other mirrors (a school-bathroom mirror in cmp-002 Bradbury, etc.). Stage 5 output: emergence-point entry plus portal-class commitment plus Layer A vs Layer B documentation per cc-cmp001-narrative-architecture.

STAGE 6. NAMED NPC ROSTER WITH NO-FABRICATION DISCIPLINE. Text-canonical NPC names (Mrs Luella Bates Washington Jones, Roger) are committed. Documented-historical NPCs (Powell, Hedgeman, Randolph, Overton, Hulan Jack, Officer Al Howard, Maynard, Curry, Hughes, the Harpers, James L. Hicks) are committed with primary-source citations. Hughes-silent gaps (Roger’s household configuration, Mrs Jones’s church affiliation, kitchenette neighbors’ names) are explicitly preserved as gaps. The AI engine instantiates these live per the seated group at session-runtime. The rule: the codex commits what is text-canonical or historically-documented; everything else stays improvised. Stage 6 output: NPC card entries for canonical and documented characters plus Hughes-silent-gap declarations for the rest.

STAGE 7. KINGDOM COME ARENAS TIME-SUBSTRATE. The breakthrough that turned cmp-001 from a designed-world into a spawnable arena. Kingdom Come Deliverance 1 and 2 model time as a first-class mechanic: per-entity scheduling (every NPC has a daily routine across hours and days), per-item temporal degradation (food spoils, blades dull), quest time-windows (some encounters are only available between specific hours), resource-state coupling (a closed shop has no merchant), travel-time as friction, discrete time-skip via the bench-rest mechanic. Saul-locked design directions for cmp-001 (T115q item 8 design): time-windowed quests, time-cost-of-choice, forced time-skip via btwn-world (the rainbow-bookworm-burrow-between-worlds world) preferred over voluntary time-skip. Research-substrate at /polymyth/research.md. Stage 7 output: time-mechanics design commitment for the dimension plus research-substrate cross-reference.

STAGE 8. NPC DAILY-ROUTINE SCHEDULE DEPLOYMENT. The Kingdom Come substrate gets applied per dimension by writing a named-NPC daily-routine schedule. The schedule places every canonical and documented NPC at a named location at a specific in-fiction time with a documented activity. For cmp-001 the schedule covers the four-day campaign window (Saturday September 20 4 PM through Tuesday September 23 morning) plus the Wednesday-Thursday-Friday lead-up week. Fifteen named NPCs. Nine quest time-windows with explicit open and close times. Movement patterns for the five most-mobile NPCs. Time-cost-of-choice notes flagging which windows block which. Roles-without-names (kitchenette neighbors, beauty-shop coworkers, congregants, Apollo audience) stay live-improvised at session-runtime. Schedule file at /polymyth/campaigncodex/cmp-001-npc-schedule.md. Stage 8 output: the daily-routine schedule markdown that makes the dimension spawnable.

THE TWO ARCHITECTURAL COMMITMENTS. (A) Exegetical-main-plus-variable-surroundings. The text-canonical story sequence is sealed. The surroundings (path-choices, peripheral NPCs, AI-engine improvisations of Hughes-silent gaps) vary by character-environment interaction. The bookworm can read the same text into the same dimension multiple times and meet a different surrounding world each time, but the exegetical-main always runs through the same beats. T115q item 1 ratified this architecture. (B) Pre-commit vs improvise split. The codex pre-commits text-canonical and historically-documented specifics. Everything else stays improvised. The AI engine note at cc-cmp001-clock states it directly: Hughes-text-canonical events anchor Roger and Mrs Jones in their Saturday-night beats. All other character-location specifics across the four-day window are improvised live per session paths, not pre-committed in CC*. This rule prevents the codex from bloating into a fixed novel; it preserves the dimension’s liveness while protecting its anchors.

THE DM-PREP BUDGET. The fully-built dimension can be spawned into by a DM with approximately ninety minutes of cold-start preparation. The reading order is: (1) the anchor-text itself, fifteen minutes for a short story like Hughes, longer for a novel. (2) The NPC daily-routine schedule, fifteen to twenty minutes. (3) The narrative-architecture entry (mirror-portal mechanics, Layer A vs Layer B), ten minutes. (4) The four ghost-firing entries (the four moments in the campaign where text-canonical exegesis activates pedagogically), fifteen minutes. (5) A scan of the eight relevant realism-domain entries to know what tier-2 material is available on path-trigger, fifteen minutes. (6) The DM does not need to read all 379 cc-cmp001-* entries. The codex is reference material, not memorization material. The dmboard (the DM-AI scene-creation interaction surface) handles in-session retrieval per T115q item 5.

THE SESSION-RUNTIME IMPROVISATION RULE. What the AI engine improvises live, per the seated group, per the path the bookworms walk: peripheral NPC names and voices, Hughes-silent gaps (Roger’s household per cc-cmp001-realism-social types A through E, Mrs Jones’s church affiliation per cc-cmp001-realism-religious, the specific desk sergeant on duty at the 28th Precinct night shift, the Amsterdam News compositor on shift, period passersby on any block, the rear-house roomer Roger and Mrs Jones might hear through the wall). What the AI engine does NOT improvise: the exegetical-main beat sequence, the documented-historical NPC schedules, the spatial geography, the period-anchored economic and linguistic registers, the tier-1 realism content.

QUALITY GATES (what counts as ready to spawn into). A dimension is spawn-ready when: (1) the anchor-text is selected and bibliographically cited, (2) the exegetical-main is locked, (3) all fifteen realism domains have substantive entries with tier separation, (4) the spatial grid is built and named locations are committed, (5) the mirror-portal entry mechanism is documented, (6) the named NPC roster is committed with no fabricated names, (7) the time-substrate design direction is locked, (8) the NPC daily-routine schedule is written. cmp-001 hit all eight gates by May 24 2026. cmp-002 Bradbury currently sits at Stage 1 (anchor-text selected, exegetical-main known from the story); Stages 2-8 remain to be executed.

WHAT THIS STANDARD REPLACES. Before May 2026 the design assumption was that a DM running cmp-001 needed to internalize all 379 entries before sitting down with players. This was correct given the entries but wrong given the design intent. The methodology above re-shapes the prep load from memorization to reference-with-runbook. The daily-routine schedule plus the narrative-architecture entry plus the ghost-firing entries plus a tier-2 realism scan equals the runbook. Everything else stays in the codex as reference material the AI engine surfaces on path-trigger.

LINEAGE OF THE DESIGN DISCOVERIES. (a) The exegetical-main-plus-variable-surroundings architecture emerged from T115d item 1 (synthesis-issue identification) and T115q item 1 (ratification). (b) The fifteen-domain realism inventory grew incrementally through the cmp-001 build (eight domains initial, fifteen final after the realism-religious, realism-domestic, realism-legal, realism-recreational, realism-technological, realism-environmental, realism-educational additions). (c) The mirror-portal entry class was formalized in cc-cmp001-narrative-architecture MAY 10 2026 EXTENSION REVISED and re-articulated in cc-cmp001-hughes-house. (d) The Kingdom Come arenas substrate was researched in T115r and locked in T115q item 8 design-direction. (e) The NPC daily-routine schedule format was designed and executed in T115x (May 24 2026) at /polymyth/campaigncodex/cmp-001-npc-schedule.md. (f) The pre-commit vs improvise split was ratified at cc-cmp001-clock and re-affirmed at cc-cmp001-mrs-jones and cc-cmp001-roger as the AI engine note pattern.

CROSS-REFERENCES. ml* PM13 (realism-trumps-all, teacher-is-filter). ml* polymythdnd OP-1 through OP-20 (the twenty operations including OP-18 exegetical-main-plus-variable-surroundings and OP-20 arenas). dm-010 (tier-calibrated activation by bookworm-card band). dm-024 (DM protocol for the spawnable-arena scene-handling). bw-006 (rainbow-crossing as the burrow-return signature). bw-007 (bookworm-vs-character continuity-vs-locality). bw-dmboard-intro (the DM-AI scene-creation surface). cc-cmp001-narrative-architecture (mirror-portal mechanics canonical). cc-cmp001-clock (pre-commit vs improvise rule canonical). cc-cmp001-realism (parent of the fifteen domain children). The NPC daily-routine schedule file at /polymyth/campaigncodex/cmp-001-npc-schedule.md. The Kingdom Come time-mechanics research substrate at /polymyth/research.md. The notebook supplement at /polymyth/notebook/the-burrow-notebook-supplement_v0-1.pdf (the bookworm-facing student-side deployment of the antihivemind / marshmellowmonster / btwn-world vocabulary that emerged through this build arc).

TO RUN A NEW DIMENSION (cmp-002, cmp-003, etc.) FOLLOWING THIS STANDARD. Execute Stages 1 through 8 in order. Use cmp-001 as the worked example. The Bradbury All Summer in a Day dimension at dim-032 sits at Stage 1; the next session-of-work executes Stages 2 through 8 against the Bradbury text. The standard scales: a short story dimension takes the build process this entry documents; a novel-length dimension scales the realism-inventory depth and the schedule duration proportionally. The architecture stays the same. The depth grows with the text.

EXTENSION:
May 24 2026 T115y synthesis. Documents the eight-stage build process, fifteen-domain realism inventory, exegetical-main-plus-variable-surroundings architecture, mirror-portal entry mechanics, Kingdom Come arenas time-substrate, NPC daily-routine schedule format, DM-prep budget, session-runtime improvisation rule, and quality gates. The standard exists so cmp-002 Bradbury and cmp-003 onward can be built without re-deriving the architecture from cmp-001.

ID: dm-033
TITLE: Pregame-arena fair game. Gates arrive at session zero with known participants, never at arena construction (Saul-directed 2026-06-05)
ROLE: dm

PREGAME-ARENA FAIR GAME. Saul-directive 2026-06-05 during Ghibli World scoping, after the AI asked whether heavy films should be age-gated at arena time.

RULE. While an arena is being constructed, the codex, the dimensions, the library, no audience gate applies. Any material that passes the polymyth admission criteria is fair game: internal coherence, external coherence, sabachtan-compatibility. Audience gating, age bands, group fit, content sensitivity, is a session-zero operation. It is performed by the teacher or DM when the actual participants are known, against the known table, never against a hypothetical audience.

AI CONDUCT CLAUSE. The AI never asks who-is-participating or audience-suitability questions during pregame, arena, or codex construction. Such questions belong to session zero. Asking them at construction time is the named failure this entry exists to stop.

ORDER OF OPERATIONS. Construction admits by coherence. Session zero gates by table. The two operations never swap positions.

SIBLINGS. dm-032 dimension build standard governs how arenas are built. dm-018 teacher as load-bearing element holds the gate authority at session zero.

ORIGIN. Saul-directive 2026-06-05, Ghibli World scoping session.

EXTENSION:
Arena construction admits any material passing internal coherence, external coherence, and sabachtan-compatibility; no audience gating at build time. Gating is a session-zero operation by the teacher or DM against known participants. The AI never asks audience-suitability questions during pregame or codex construction.

ID: dm-034
TITLE: Kegare contamination system: contagious mechanical defilement with a cleansing economy (AI-filed 2026-06-06, cmp-003 import)
ROLE: dm

RULE. Defilement is a stacking meter, contagious and mechanical, never moral. SOURCES. Death strongest, then blood, childbirth, disease; corpse contact loads heaviest. SPREAD. Contact and proximity transfer points within a radius; an unclean traveler contaminates companions, lodgings, tools. GATES. Accumulation bars torii thresholds and shrine ground, sours dealings under purity norms, and attracts hostile spirits at high load. CLEANSING ECONOMY, tiered. Temizu rinse trims trace points free; salt wards entrances and persons cheap; the onusa wand and shubatsu sprinkle clear mid-tier at shrines; full harae rites and misogi cold-water ablution clear deep load at real time and resource cost. CURSE VARIANT. The tatarigami pattern: a wound of hatred that empowers as it corrupts, a separate corruption track that cleansing alone cannot touch; resolution demands righting the source wrong. ORIGIN. cmp-003 substrate research, archive 2 section 1; the load-bearing physics across all five frames.

EXTENSION:
Contagious purity meter with tiered cleansing and a tatarigami corruption variant; the cmp-003 physics core.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-035
TITLE: Encounter grammar: four tags and the ward-as-puzzle rule (AI-filed 2026-06-06, cmp-003 import)
ROLE: dm

RULE. Every spirit entity carries one or more of four tags. TRICKSTER runs social and puzzle play. THREAT runs combat or evasion. GUARDIAN runs gatekeeping, alliance, and protector roles. OMEN runs foreshadowing and lore triggers, never direct conflict. WARD-AS-PUZZLE. The folkloric ward is the designed solution, never trivia: bow to the kappa and the dish spills; hand the funayurei a bottomless ladle; hide the rokurokubi body; draw and share the amabie image to end a plague event; speak the betobeto-san past with please go ahead. A table that knows the folklore wins by knowledge; a table that does not can discover the ward in play through clues. SOURCING DISCIPLINE. Entities draw from the public-domain record, Sekien, Yanagita, Hearn; modern copyrighted designs, Mizuki above all, never enter. ORIGIN. cmp-003 substrate research, archive 2 section 2 and the 44-entry bestiary index.

MOVE-ECONOMY LAYER (added 2026-06-06, CL-30): consequence delivery inside every encounter runs the dm-039 soft-then-hard cadence, telegraph first, follow through only on an ignored telegraph, the move never named aloud.

EXTENSION:
Trickster, threat, guardian, omen; the folkloric ward is the puzzle answer; public-domain sourcing only.

ID: dm-036
TITLE: Seasonal matsuri clock and the satoyama management biome (AI-filed 2026-06-06, cmp-003 import)
ROLE: dm

CLOCK RULE. The festival year is the campaign clock: shogatsu and hatsumode open it; setsubun expels; hanami, tanabata, obon with the ancestor return, tsukimi, shichi-go-san, and omisoka with its 108 bells close it; local mikoshi processions and harvest rites stud the map. Festivals grant purity and fortune buffs; a missed or botched rite costs crops, luck, and standing; obon opens the ancestor-contact window. BIOME RULE. Satoyama is the default map: the managed mosaic of paddy, coppice, grassland, and stream between village and mountain, carrying a management level. High management yields resources and safe passage; neglect collapses the patchwork and invites encroachment from the yama side, spirits and beasts pressing into human ground. NODES. Chinju no mori groves are protected old-growth islands; bunrei shrine-division lets players build new protective shrine nodes by inviting a kami, infrastructure as worship. ORIGIN. cmp-003 substrate research, archive 2 sections on the matsuri calendar and landscape ecology.

EXTENSION:
Festival year as campaign clock with rite buffs and penalties; satoyama management level; bunrei shrine-building.

ID: dm-037
TITLE: Name-magic class trio and the frame economies pointer (AI-filed 2026-06-06, cmp-003 import)
ROLE: dm

THREE PRACTITIONER TEMPLATES. KOTODAMA, word-spirit: true speech affects what it names; recovering a stolen name breaks bondage, the Spirited and Earthsea pattern generalized; holding a kitsune pearl compels service; norito and sutra speech raise barriers. ONMYODO, the bureaucratic ritualist: the Taiho 701 bureau template on the Abe no Seimei archetype; calendar mastery, divination, shikigami paper familiars, and kataimi directional taboos that turn movement into a planning puzzle; uniquely licensed to handle kegare without self-pollution. SHUGENDO ASCETIC, the mountain-entry discipline of the yamabushi, flagged as a named research gap; class skeleton only until the practice detail lands. ECONOMIES POINTER. Each cmp-003 period frame plays its documented economy literally: the 1927 shop list, coffee 10 sen, soba 8 to 10 sen, rent 20 yen, graduate salary 80 yen monthly; the 1945 ration ledger, 1793 calories and falling; see the cc substrate-frames entry. ORIGIN. cmp-003 substrate research, archive 2.

EXTENSION:
Kotodama name-magic, onmyodo ritualist with kataimi planning, shugendo skeleton pending; period price lists as literal shops.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-038
TITLE: CL-14 Adjudication spine: roll only with stakes, middle path, success at a cost (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Roll only when both conditions hold: a real chance of failure AND a meaningful consequence for failing. If either is absent, rule: say yes, or say it cannot work, and narrate on. Dice are tools; the dice do not run the table (2014 DMG ch. 8, pp. 236-237, verified to page scan; retained 2024). Default posture is the middle path between rolling-for-everything and pure fiat. Marginal failure, missed by one or two, converts to success at a cost: the goal lands plus a complication. Larger misses use degrees of failure; a five-or-more miss earns the worse outcome. Flat failure is reserved for cases where the setback is itself interesting. Interaction: dm-021 AI-math contributions feed the odds, dm-017 hierarchy holds, story keeps the table.

EXTENSION:
DMG-doctrine research capture. The most transferable rules-craft across fifty years of official print.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-039
TITLE: CL-15 Soft-move then hard-move cadence, the move economy under encounter grammar (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

The narration grammar of consequence. Soft move: announce future badness, show signs of the approaching threat, offer opportunity with cost, then end on the open question. The player gets the chance to act. A soft move ignored becomes the golden opportunity for the hard move: irrevocable follow-through. Never jump to irrevocable harm without the telegraph; never skip the follow-through once the telegraph was ignored, or telegraphs stop meaning. Never speak the move’s name; narrate the fictional event only, and misdirect to the fiction (Apocalypse World and Dungeon World principles, verified to SRD and reproduced second-edition text). OSR telegraphing is the same grammar: mention danger when it becomes obvious. Extends dm-035 as its move-economy layer.

EXTENSION:
GM-craft research capture. Wired into dm-035 by cross-link same pass.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-040
TITLE: CL-16 World-as-agent procedure: goals in motion, offscreen advance, events snowball (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Every active NPC and faction holds a goal it pursues right now, on its own clock, indifferent to player convenience. Offscreen motion advances between scenes and telegraphs through perceivable signs onscreen: smoke on the ridge, a price doubled, a roster face missing. Give NPCs concerns that do not involve the party (Principia Apocrypha, verified). Events snowball; action, reaction, and consequence drive the table without management (Blades, verified). The world never waits for its prose to be admired; the inert-world failure is this procedure absent. Bookkeeping: fronts or clocks per threat, advanced when the table looks away or dawdles, interacting with the dm-036 matsuri clock where the campaign carries one.

EXTENSION:
GM-craft research capture. The procedure-level cure for the narrator-admiring-his-own-gravity failure.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-041
TITLE: CL-17 No-menu choice surfacing: affordances live in the world (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Options are never presented as parallel labeled items, bolded headers, or bulleted lists; that is interface, not world. Affordances live in geography, NPC behavior, sound, motion, and consequence: the path splits where the burned trees start, the broker keeps glancing at the side door, the drumming is louder uphill. Telegraph danger and opportunity as perceivable fact and let the player infer the verbs. When a young or new player stalls, route assistance through the fiction: an NPC suggestion, a companion’s idea, an intuition line in second person, never a list. The catalogue-with-perfume failure was this rule broken at structure level while passing at word level.

META-CHANNEL RIDER (2026-06-06, CL-54): the channel stays open for every seat, never only the young one. Share freely what the character would suspect, intuit, and predict, since the player holds only the narrow channel of the narrator’s few words (Blades, verified). Feelings stay the player’s own per dm-060; suspicion and prediction are shareable, the interior is never assigned.

EXTENSION:
GM-craft research capture. The mechanism under T118 asymmetric staging, ml* side.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-042
TITLE: CL-18 Encounter-worth test plus the rewards note (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

An encounter earns its slot by doing at least one: pressuring a finite resource (time, strength, supplies, light, standing), advancing or foreshadowing story, revealing world or theme, or offering a real choice with consequences. An encounter doing none of these is filler and gets cut before the table sees it. Standing ceiling from the 2024 doctrine, verified: random or planned, encounters should never be tiresome. Closure note shipped with this entry: official XP and adventuring-day attrition economies are superseded at this table by the bookworm-character two-clock progression already canonical; the only surviving fragment is that rewards function as motivation and pacing markers, never as the goal of play.

FUN-SUFFICES RIDER (2026-06-06): an encounter moving nothing may still hold its slot when the table will love playing it; fun serves the story too (2024 fun-distractions clause, verified).

EXTENSION:
DMG-doctrine research capture plus the CL-33 closure rider.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-043
TITLE: CL-19 Onboarding inside the fiction, mixed-knowledge handling (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Address the characters, not the players (Apocalypse World principle, verified). Lore arrives through NPC dialogue, small in-fiction questions, and what the world does, never through lecture; the lore dump is a named anti-pattern (dm-049). Ask provocative questions and build on the answers; the new player learns the world by being asked into it. Mixed-knowledge tables: give players what their characters may not know and characters what their players lack, and make consequences land on everyone so each seat holds a handle (Laws, verified interview). The fourth table failure (dm-062) is the onboarding half of this rule broken: the frame must be given in the fiction, never assumed.

EXTENSION:
GM-craft research capture. Pairs with the pregame brief; gating authority unchanged, dm-033 holds.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-044
TITLE: CL-20 Kids-table pacing block (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Completed arc every session; cliffhangers are for adults, small children want completion (Hart, The DM Lair, verified; session length consensus sixty to one-twenty minutes, exact figure contested and flagged). Explicit turn-taking outside combat: name the player, state where they stand, ask what they do, and the next player knows they are next. Props and tactile anchors carry attention; let kids breathe life into the mundane. Non-lethal stakes default: knockouts, setbacks, captures, never deaths that derail. Quiet-seat protection: the watcher and the casual player are invited, never forced into the spotlight (4e DMG watcher guidance and Laws casual-gamer rule, both verified). Recap good decisions at session end.

EXTENSION:
GM-craft and kids-DMing research capture. Feeds the pregame page; teacher gating per dm-033 untouched.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-045
TITLE: CL-21 Player-motivation lens, the merged taxonomy (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

One spotlight-tuning instrument from two verified taxonomies. 4e DMG eight types, verbatim list verified: actor, explorer, instigator, power gamer, slayer, storyteller, thinker, watcher. Laws seven, verified to Robin’s Laws 2002: power gamer, butt-kicker, tactician, specialist, method actor, storyteller, casual gamer. Operational rule from Laws: read what a player builds and asks for as their order for the type of fun they want, then feed it. Per-seat tuning beats per-table averaging. Watch-fors travel with the types: the instigator derails, the actor weaponizes in-character, the slayer steamrolls nuance; redirect inside the fiction.

EXTENSION:
DMG-doctrine and GM-craft research capture, merged as one lens.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-046
TITLE: CL-22 NPC one-sentence kit (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Construction standard for any speaking NPC, one sentence per slot, slots fillable live: occupation and history; one distinctive appearance detail; one notable talent; one mannerism; one interaction trait; an ideal, a bond, and a flaw or secret (2014 DMG ch. 4 apparatus, verified). The ideal-bond-flaw triple is the social-resolution hook: discovering one shifts what persuasion can reach, two steps better at the deepest read (2014 ch. 8 structure, verified). Named adversaries deserve the same kit as allies. Existing cmp-003 rosters stand as filed; the kit governs construction going forward.

RIDER (2026-06-06): name every speaking NPC at first appearance; a name makes them human (Apocalypse World principle, verified).

EXTENSION:
DMG-doctrine research capture. Forward standard, no retro-edit of filed rosters.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-047
TITLE: CL-23 Situations not plots, the three-clue rule, fan of the characters (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Prep situations, never scripts: a plot is a sequence of events you expect; a situation is a set of circumstances that plays out differently depending on what the players do (Alexandrian, verified). The 2024 DMG prints the same law: events should not be pre-determined, the characters’ actions have to matter (verified). Three-clue rule: any conclusion the table must reach gets at least three independent clues; any chokepoint gets three routes (verified). Play to find out what happens. Be a fan of the characters: present the world honestly, hold its dangers, and never become its enemy (verified). Railroad diagnosis: players repeatedly bouncing off one required outcome means the bottleneck converts to multiple viable paths, immediately.

EXTENSION:
GM-craft and DMG-doctrine research capture, convergent third-party and official print.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-048
TITLE: CL-24 Improv block: be obvious, yes-but, reincorporate, never block (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Take the obvious offer instead of straining for cleverness; hold ideas lightly (Johnstone via Walmsley, Play Unsafe, verified structure). Default answer to a risky player goal is yes-but: the goal lands, a cost or complication rides along (Blades practice, verified). Reincorporate: earlier details return and the world coheres; gifts get used, never wasted. Never block a player idea; build on it or price it. Spotlight is shared deliberately, each seat engaged as an individual (D’Amato exercises, verified secondhand). Boundary: improv serves the scene’s purpose; there is a time to stop yes-anding when the story needs its turn (Angry GM caution, verified).

EXTENSION:
GM-craft research capture.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-049
TITLE: CL-25 Anti-pattern register, eight named (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

The masters’ named failures, kept as a pre-delivery checklist. One, boxed-text drone: reciting kills attention; speak, never recite. Two, the lore dump. Three, the quiz-master gotcha: gating on referents the table was never given; the fourth table failure (dm-062) sits here. Four, over-description: vomiting descriptive prose past the three-sentence cap. Five, the railroad. Six, the GM performing for himself: written-for-the-author at table scale, Gardner frigidity. Seven, blocking player ideas. Eight, the menu-interface: catalogue-with-perfume at structure scale. Four of the eight were committed at this table and named; the register exists so the other four never are.

EXTENSION:
GM-craft research capture, mapped onto the T118 failure lineage.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-050
TITLE: CL-01 NARRATION LOOP LAW (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Describe what the characters can perceive, three sentences or fewer, second person, end on the open question, then yield. Disclose progressively: more detail is the reward for investigation, never a quiz gate (dm-056 boundary governs). Loop: describe, invite action, narrate result, yield again. Convergent across the 2024 DMG narration guidance (players begin to lose focus after about three sentences of descriptive text, verified to reproduced page text), Angry GM narration-as-information (verified), and the OSR two-sentence room rule. The cap is hard during live play; layering is earned by player attention.

EXTENSION:
Filed from the GM-craft and DMG-doctrine research passes, same day as T118 rev 2. Operationalizes the table burst shape.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-051
TITLE: CL-02 SCENE-OPENING LAW (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Two moves before the mouth opens: identify the agenda (why this scene matters, what question it answers) and open on the bang, the event that forces a decision. Cut as close to the next meaningful choice as possible. Enter late, leave early (Goldman). Start in the action with stakes in the first line (Moth, verified). Strong start anchors the session (Sly Flourish, verified). The opening gives the frame through what happens; it never requires the frame to be held already.

EXTENSION:
Alexandrian scene-framing plus oral-stage doctrine. Pairs with dm-062 as the positive law the fourth failure broke.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-052
TITLE: CL-03 SENTENCE-RHYTHM LAW (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Variety governs. Le Guin, verified: there is no optimum sentence length, the optimum is variety; the test of a sentence is whether it sounds right. Never three same-length sentences consecutively. The short hit lands the live beat after a long roll. Punctuation is breath for spoken delivery; every burst must be sayable. Provost passage (verified to 100 Ways to Improve Your Writing, Signet 1985, pp. 60-61) archived as the operational template. Monotone length and matched shapes read as machine output, the mechanism under the catalogue-with-perfume failure.

EXTENSION:
Sentence-level half of asymmetric staging. Cross-links T118 rev 2.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-053
TITLE: CL-04 DETAIL-SELECTION LAW (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

One characterizing particular per beat, the detail that implies the rest. Crowd the relevant, leap the rest (Le Guin, verified: listing is not describing, only the relevant belongs, white space around the word). Reveal a place bit by bit; a small number of very particular details outperforms many common ones; each word carries more weight when a player must act on it (Emily Short, verified, interactive fiction as the nearest written tradition to table narration). A detail that decorates rather than characterizes is a darling and gets cut.

EXTENSION:
Grounds the standing describe-before-name law with its selection mechanism.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-054
TITLE: CL-05 VERB-MOTION LAW (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

The world takes strong transitive verbs; objects act. Thought-verb ban (Palahniuk, verified): thinks, knows, understands, realizes, believes, wants, remembers, imagines, desires, loves, hates, and as far as possible is and has. Filter-word ban: saw, heard, felt, noticed, watched, seemed, looked, realized, decided, wondered, knew. Render the evidence, let the listener do the knowing. Exception: keep the filter when the act of perceiving is itself the event or marked uncertainty is the point. Lanham paramedic method clears static patches: find the action, put it in a verb, cut nominalization strings. Register model: screenplay action lines, present tense, spare, kinetic, second by second.

CALIBRATION RIDER (2026-06-06): the passive is correct when the receiver of the action is the true subject of attention; activization is a default, never a dogma (Pullum correction of Strunk-White, verified).

EXTENSION:
The line-level engine of world-as-agent. Diagnoses reads-like-code at sentence scale.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-055
TITLE: CL-06 PSYCHIC-DISTANCE DIAL (research capture 2026-06-06, Gardner secondhand-flagged)
ROLE: dm

Narration runs a distance dial from far (it was winter) to close (cold, the wet snap of the collar). Move close on the live beat, pull far for transitions. Accidental shifts break the vivid continuous dream. Diagnosis attached: the data register is this dial welded at maximum distance, which is the mechanism under the reads-like-code failure. Frigidity, Gardner’s term for the author more interested in performing the telling than in the thing told, is the mechanism under the written-for-the-author failure. Gardner formulations carried secondhand pending primary verification per CL-28 ledger.

EXTENSION:
Art of Fiction doctrine routed through the failure log. Quote-status flagged.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-056
TITLE: CL-07 WITHHOLDING BOUNDARY, THE INVERTED-U (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Curiosity is a perceived gap in knowledge the listener believes could be filled (Loewenstein 1994, Psychological Bulletin, verified). Intensity follows an inverted-U: it peaks at partial knowledge and dies at too little exactly as at too much. Operational boundary: the gap must concern what happens NEXT, never what is happening NOW; the listener must already know enough to care and to act. Too-little is the quiz-master pole, the gatekeeping failure. Micro-tension (Maass, verified) carries pull through calm beats via conflicting undercurrents, tension over the next few seconds rather than plot danger. Plant the question in the listener first; never make them guess what they were never given.

EXTENSION:
The academic backbone of withholding-pulls and the craft-grounding of the fourth table failure (dm-062).

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-057
TITLE: CL-08 FOLKTALE-REGISTER SPEC (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

How plain prose enchants, the positive mechanism under the for-anyone gate. Luthi, verified formulations: one-dimensionality, the miracle is matter-of-fact and provokes no surprise; depthlessness, character externalized into action and object; abstract style, sharp outlines, extremes and contrasts, pure colors; isolation with universal interconnection. Calvino, verified: lightness goes with precision and determination, never vagueness; quickness as agility; exactitude as the clear, incisive, memorable image. Wonder lives in event, image, and promise, never in adjectives. One hard word is permitted when plain context cradles it: children backhand hard words over the net provided the context absorbs them (E.B. White, Paris Review 1969, verified). Never write down (Lewis, White).

EXTENSION:
The register the table runs in: dirt-test prose that still carries awe.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-058
TITLE: CL-09 SPOKEN-SYNTAX GATE (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

A listening child cannot re-read, so syntax gates harder than vocabulary. Additive right-branching chains over center-embedding: center-embedded comprehension is very poor in listening six-to-eight-year-olds independent of context or memory span (Weighall and Altmann 2011, Journal of Child Language, verified); spoken language is practically free of multiple center-embedding (Karlsson 2007, Journal of Linguistics, verified). Subject-relatives over object-relatives. No garden-path late reversals; speech offers no second pass. Subject-first canonical order on load-bearing beats. Strategic redundancy is a feature in spoken delivery, never clutter (Ong, verified). Vocabulary and content may sit above a ten-year-old’s reading level while syntax stays clean: listening level leads reading level until grade eight (Trelease 1982, verified).

THRESHOLD RIDER (2026-06-06): an adult-only table may relax this gate toward cumulative-sentence richness; the verb-motion and micro-tension laws never relax (dm-054, dm-056).

EXTENSION:
Empirical floor under the dirt-test. Lift the words, keep the structures clean.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-059
TITLE: CL-10 BEAT-ARCHITECTURE LAW (research capture 2026-06-06, Swain secondhand-flagged)
ROLE: dm

Moment grammar: stimulus before reaction, always. The world acts first, objectively and externally; reaction follows in order, feeling, then action, then speech (Swain motivation-reaction units, doctrine verified through many editors, exact wording secondhand-flagged per CL-28). At the table the reaction slot belongs to the player: present the stimulus and stop. Never narrate the player’s interior. Paragraph shapes vary as hard as sentence lengths; the one-sentence paragraph is a hit; silence between bursts is pacing (Le Guin white space, verified).

EXTENSION:
Beat-level half of asymmetric staging; the stop-point discipline of the narration loop.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-060
TITLE: CL-11 SECOND-PERSON DISCIPLINE (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

You stays the agent. The world acts on you: a torch gutters on the wall, never you see a torch. Filter words are doubly corrosive in second person since they reassert that you merely observe. Never command the player’s feelings (you are terrified is banned); never force the gaze; present the stimulus and let the feeling arise in the listener (Klinkenborg on overgoverning the reader, verified; Emily Short on the active you, verified). Discovery happens through the player’s action, never through assignment.

EXTENSION:
The table-narration form of describe-before-name plus the MRU stop-point.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-061
TITLE: CL-12 REVISION PASS, SCRIPTED (research capture 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Runs on every table burst before delivery, five checks plus a cut. One: strip filter words and thought verbs (dm-054). Two: distance close on the live beat (dm-055). Three: rhythm varied, no three same-length sentences, shapes asymmetric (dm-052, CL-10). Four: the open gap points at next, never at now, and gates on nothing the table was not given (dm-056). Five: frigidity test, am I enjoying this phrase more than the listener will; a yes deletes the phrase (Quiller-Couch murder-your-darlings, verified to On the Art of Writing 1916; the context is exactly ornament written for display). Then cut ten percent (King, verified).

CALIBRATION RIDER (2026-06-06): the adverb rule cuts the adverb propping a weak verb, never every adverb; absolutism on this point is contested and flagged.

EXTENSION:
The enforcement layer over CL-01 through CL-11.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-062
TITLE: CL-13 WRITTEN-FOR-THE-INITIATED, the fourth table failure 2026-06-06: OPENING ADDRESSED TO A FRAME-HOLDER
ROLE: dm

Fourth same-day failure, first Studio Qibla table, caught by Saul in one line: are you assuming the player knows what you are talking about. The opening’s closing instruction, name your film, your where, your when, was actable only by a player already holding the session-zero frame, and no table beat had built that frame. The four sensory leaks compounded it by rewarding corpus recognition: invitations to the initiated, weather without handles to anyone else. Mechanism: the Loewenstein too-little pole (dm-056); the gap was pitched about NOW, gated on lore never given. Anti-pattern match: the quiz-master GM (dm-049 register). Ruling: the for-anyone gate judges referents as well as diction; prose addressed to a knower fails the gate even when the knower is the only one seated, since table prose is the practice’s template. Fix demonstrated same turn: the world teaches its own frame through event before any choice is asked, and the choice arrives actable with zero prior knowledge. Naming record at the ml* pending-user-authorship section.

NAMED (2026-06-06): WRITTEN-FOR-THE-INITIATED, chosen by the AI under Saul delegation, his words, this does not matter, you can name it yourself. The name follows the sibling form of WRITTEN-FOR-THE-AUTHOR, since both failures pitch prose at a reader who is not the table. PASSWORD-PROSE is retired.

EXTENSION:
Failure log lineage: reads-like-code, catalogue-with-perfume, written-for-the-author, this. T118 rev 3 backref.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-063
TITLE: CL-38 Random-table craft law (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Tables stay small, d6 or d8, never the d100 monster; the table only ever sees one result, and a list too big to be all good is a list padded with boring. Tables are specific to their world: an enchanted forest and a horror forest never share a table. Own every borrowed table before play; rolling on a table is never the first time it gets read. The re-roll urge is a defect signal: wanting to roll again means the table holds entries that should never have been on it. Rolling before the session is legitimate craft, brainstorm from the result, then polish until it lands deliberate. Dice are suggestion, never boss: a short list pulled from at will serves the same function without the roll. Randomness earns its keep twice over: it breaks the DM’s own blinders past the row of correct dots, and it places the world beyond the DM’s visible control, which defeats player metagaming and forces in-character risk assessment. Sources: 2024 DMG ch. 4 doctrine, verified; craft synthesis from the table-craft commentary transcript Saul supplied 2026-06-06.

EXTENSION:
Second-wave CL capture. System-level law over the five cc* cmp-003 tables (CL-26 instances).

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-064
TITLE: CL-39 General pacing law: the hope-fear pulse (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Beats alternate between hope and fear; the pulse is the pacing instrument (Laws, Hamlet’s Hit Points, book secondhand-flagged, interview formulations verified). Alternate procedural beats, progress toward a tangible goal, with dramatic beats, pressure between people. Players cruising: drop a hard beat. Players drowning: give a break. Dead time dies by eliding narration, several days pass, or by the sharp cut; no scene runs without an agenda (Alexandrian, verified). A scene is a location plus one driving challenge, with clean transitions and the scene re-set after each (Angry GM, verified). Prep heuristic: roughly one scene per forty-five minutes. Session shape: strong start, clean close, and the last line known before the closing burst begins, land the plane (Sly Flourish and the Moth, verified).

THIRD BEAT COLOR (2026-06-06, CL-55): alongside procedural and dramatic runs the informational beat, the discovery beat (Laws pillar mapping, verified interview). In exegetical play this color is first-class: seam-noticing is the game working, so the pulse alternates across all three, and a session heavy in any one color reads as a dm-068 symptom.

EXTENSION:
Second-wave CL capture, the general-table half of the dm-044 kids block.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-065
TITLE: CL-40 Tension economy and rest placement (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Successive encounters raise tension; a rest relaxes it; the table breathes where rest is possible, so place rest opportunities deliberately and scarcity of safe ground becomes a pacing dial (2024 DMG encounter-pace guidance, verified). Endings choose between resolution and cliffhanger; the dm-044 completion law overrides toward resolution whenever children sit at the table. Urgency tools stay editorial, never lethal, per the CL-26 usage law.

EXTENSION:
Second-wave CL capture.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-066
TITLE: CL-41 NPC dialogue law: no as-you-know (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

An NPC never tells another character what both already know so the table can overhear it; the as-you-know scene is dead on arrival (Mamet memo to the writers of The Unit, verified). An NPC speaks from a simple, pressing need pursued right now, and information the table must learn arrives dramatized through that want, never announced. Test before any NPC line: what does this speaker want this second, and what are their hands doing. A line surviving neither question gets cut.

EXTENSION:
Second-wave CL capture. The dialogue-channel twin of dm-043 onboarding.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-067
TITLE: CL-43 Table-contract law: shared responsibility for the fun (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

The game is cooperative root to branch. The DM plays the antagonists and wants the party’s failure no more than anyone seated; having fun outranks character success (4e DMG, verbatim verified). The load runs both ways: it is not the DM’s job to entertain the players, every person playing is responsible for the fun (4e, verbatim verified; 2024 mutual-respect frame, verified). Teaching-table application: students co-own whether the story works, and that co-ownership is itself the pedagogy. dm-017 privilege hierarchy untouched; story still holds the table, this entry governs who carries it.

EXTENSION:
Third-wave CL capture, DMG-doctrine research.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-068
TITLE: CL-44 Table-diagnostics loop: symptom to adjustment (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Live tuning instrument, read the table and turn one dial. Child disengages during description: tighten the three-sentence cap further and raise question frequency. Adult disengages: the prose has gone flat, tighten verb motion (dm-054) and micro-tension (dm-056). Both disengage on a long beat: an inventory has formed, leap the rest (dm-053) and enter later (dm-051). Railroad feeling: add clues and routes, convert the bottleneck to multiple paths (dm-047). World feels static: more offscreen advances and telegraphed motion per scene (dm-040). A seat under-participates: read the type (dm-045) and feed it, the quiet seat gets invited, never spotlit. Stakes sag across sessions: reintroduce mild dawdle-pressure before any lethality, per the CL-26 usage law. One adjustment per symptom per session, then re-read.

EXTENSION:
Third-wave CL capture, consolidated from the benchmark sections of all three research reports.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-069
TITLE: CL-45 Epithet-formula law: the recurring tag-phrase (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Every recurring entity carries one fixed tag-phrase sounded at each return, the formulaic epithet: the murage soot to the eyebrows, the well-cold breath, the carrier of names. Oral craft grounds it twice: the aggregative epithet aids the listening ear (Ong, verified) and formulaic fixity is a law of the folktale’s abstract style (Luthi, verified). At a kids table the epithet is the memory anchor; a child who lost the plot finds it again the moment the tag sounds. Discipline: one epithet per entity, plain words, never two for the same referent, retired only when the entity transforms and the retirement itself is narrated.

EXTENSION:
Third-wave CL capture, prose-craft research. The repetition license of dm-058 given its positive instrument.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-070
TITLE: CL-46 Map-withholding law: anchors are DM-side, discovery is play (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Spatial grids and anchor points are the DM’s instruments and never become player handouts. Players chart by living the ground; withholding the map keeps the world dangerous and mysterious (Colville, secondhand-flagged fan notes). A player sketching at the table is play and gets honored as play, errors included; the sketch is theirs, never corrected from above. Free-travel stamp untouched: travel stays free while knowledge stays earned, and the two together are the exploration economy.

EXTENSION:
Third-wave CL capture, GM-craft research. Compatible with the dim-033 grids-as-anchors stamp.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-071
TITLE: CL-48 Worked-example documentation law for campaign codices (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Every cc* campaign document is written to teach by example, the method the 2024 DMG uses when it teaches campaign construction through a worked setting chapter rather than rules alone (verified). The cmp-* stage files, inventories, grids, rosters, clocks, encounter tables, pregame brief, double as the training text for the mass-campaign version where other trained teachers hold the Rainbowsol position. Construction rule following from it: each stage file reads as a template a stranger-teacher could imitate, never as a private record. A stage file failing the stranger-teacher read gets rewritten before the next stage proceeds.

EXTENSION:
Third-wave CL capture, DMG-doctrine research, wired to the dm-032 stage order and dm-018 teacher load-bearing.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-072
TITLE: CL-52 Change-moment law: one small transformation per session (filed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Every completed session arc (dm-044) centers one small transformation, the change the session exists to deliver, five seconds wide at its core. The end-of-session recap names the change out loud, and at a kids table the naming is half the lesson. A session ending with no nameable change feeds dm-068 as a symptom: an inventory ran where a story should have. Attribution: the Moth transformation principle, verified; the five-second phrasing belongs to Dicks, Storyworthy, flagged as his.

EXTENSION:
Fourth-wave CL capture, prose-craft research, oral-stage doctrine.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-073
TITLE: CL-42 Reward tokens, tangible and per-world (Saul-approved 2026-06-06)
ROLE: dm

Saul ruling: these can come in various forms throughout all games. THE RULE. Every campaign carries a tangible reward token, handed across the table when a player makes a great move, with the move named out loud as it passes, and spent later for one small boost the DM honors on the spot. The token is physical at a physical table and named-and-tracked at a remote one. Form varies per world, and the campaign codex names the form. BOUNDARIES. Tokens sit beside the bookworm and character clocks and never replace them; growth stays in the clocks, the token buys a moment. The grant rate stays low enough that a token still feels like an event. For children the token doubles as the tactile anchor dm-044 calls for.

EXTENSION:
CL-42 closed yes, generalized across games. The cmp-003 form is filed at cc* cmp-003-reward-token.

ID: undefined
TITLE: Preliminary character creator (v1 — popout architecture, four operational layers)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Framework entry covering Preliminary character creator. Full operational specification preserved in body below, including any worked examples, citation-locks, and cross-substrate relations.

The bb gate at /bookwormcard/ runs a preliminary character creator that combines four operational layers in a single-page popout-section UI. Built April 29 2026 per Rainbowsol direct specification ("just like different parts of the screen you pick, and it pops out, and you fill it out, and you can pop it back in"). Mandatory fields stay visible at top; optional sections collapse by default and pop out on click.

FOUR OPERATIONAL LAYERS.

LAYER 1 — D&D STORY-SPINE. Ten session-zero questions: backstory, motivation, defining trait, fatal flaw, what-they-want (external goal), what-they-fear, pivotal event, bond, ideal, secret. Story-relevant only — no stat sheet, no STR/DEX/CON. The questions a Dungeon Master asks at session zero to make a player-character novelistic instead of mechanical. Each is a single text-input. Optional. Any subset can be filled.

LAYER 2 — CHARACTER-SMASHING. List 3-5 figures (characters, heroes, real people) the user admires AND say WHY for each. The why-field is load-bearing — without it the operation collapses to name-collage. The user then writes the synthesis: a unique character that is none of the figures but inherits operational signatures from each. Polymyth idiomsmashing methodology applied at the figure-archetype layer (cross-references the existing idiomsmashing methodology entry).

LAYER 3 — HOROSCOPE ARCHETYPES (multi-tradition, polymyth-correct register). All five traditions where the data permits a defensible reading get rendered. NOT pick-favorites — that would violate polymyth methodology (the framework does not pick winners between cosmological grids). Year-only data unlocks Chinese zodiac (12-year cycle, year alone is sufficient). Year+month+day unlocks Western tropical sun sign (Hellenistic-medieval-modern), Celtic tree astrology (Robert Graves Beth-Luis-Nion 13 lunar months), Mayan tzolkin day-sign (260-day count, computed from Julian Day Number with Aug 11 3114 BCE epoch alignment), and Vedic sidereal sun sign (rashi, ~24-day offset from tropical). Year+month+day+time+place would unlock full Vedic chart with rising sign, nakshatra, dasha periods — deferred to v2 because requires astronomical-calculation library beyond scope of inline JS.

HOROSCOPE PRESENTATION REGISTER. Polymyth-defensible: horoscopes-as-cosmological-grids are pre-modern attempts to render the structural-recurrence claim that all human births fall on a wheel. The grid-position-as-symbolic-index claim is structurally robust (the sun IS in Aries on April 15, the Chinese zodiac DOES rotate every 12 years). The predictive-causal claim is defensible only as metaphor or self-fulfilling-prophecy. The character creator presents archetype writeups in the symbolic-index register: the grid-position OPENS a corpus of mythological material accumulated around that position across 2000+ years. The user multi-selects which archetypes they inherit onto their card. Multiple traditions can be selected simultaneously — the framework does not pick winners between traditions. Card output carries each selected archetype as 'tradition: sign-name' on a horoscope-section line.

LAYER 4 — BURROWING ANIMAL SELECTION. 38 burrowing animals across all major taxonomic groups. Worm canonical (the bookwormburrows ancestor — eats text-substrate, transforms through body, becomes soil). Comprehensive list verified against Wikipedia, Britannica, NatGeo, Fact Animal taxonomic sources. Organized into phylogenetic groups: invertebrates (11), fish (1, the West African lungfish), amphibians (2), reptiles (4), birds (4), mammals (16). Each animal carries a short operational-signature writeup. User picks one as starting-creature. CATS EXCLUDED. Per April 29 2026 dialectic: cats are not burrowers in any standard taxonomy — they are occupiers (use existing burrows, do not excavate). The cat is structurally the antagonist of the burrow operation: the cat circles the burrow waiting for the worm to emerge. Cats may appear in bb worldbuilding on the OUTSIDE of burrows; they do not appear as starting-creature options.

UI ARCHITECTURE: POPOUT SECTIONS. Collapsible sections per Rainbowsol's specification. Mandatory fields (username, email, birth year) stay visible at top — gate semantics preserved. Optional fields (birth month/day/time/place) appear in the gate but unlock progressive horoscope traditions when filled. Below the gate, popout sections for paste-back-from-previous-card, one-line-character, D&D story-spine, character-smashing, horoscope archetypes, and burrowing animal. Each popout's header shows title + sub-line explaining what's inside. Click expands. User fills, clicks again to collapse. None forced. Card output proportional to what was filled — minimum card is gate-only, maximum card carries all four layers integrated.

CARD OUTPUT INTEGRATION. The card text-block grows with what the user filled. Identity row first (^username · #hash · b. YYYY[-MM-DD]). Optional one-line character. Optional sections for story-spine / smash / horoscope / starting-creature, each prefixed with double-em-dash header for visual demarcation. Mint-date and source URL at the bottom. Format remains forward-compatible with the future bb social network parser (each section is line-delimited and prefixed).

PASTE-BACK COMPATIBILITY. The paste-back parser was extended to handle the v1 card format. Identity-line regex now matches both YYYY-only and YYYY-MM-DD birth-date formats. One-line character (if present between identity row and first section header) is parsed and the one-line-character popout auto-opens to surface the parsed value. Other fields (D&D, smash, horoscope, animal) are NOT auto-parsed from paste — those represent user choices that should be re-made each turn per the every-visit-is-ouroboros pedagogy. The user can re-select archetypes and animals or change them entirely. The paste-back surfaces only the identity-and-one-liner core.

DEFERRED TO V2. Full Vedic chart computation (requires sidereal-time and ascendant calculation, jpl-style ephemeris). Hellenistic decanic detail (3 decans per zodiac sign, 36 total). Aztec tonalpohualli (shares structure with Mayan tzolkin but uses different signs). Tibetan element-animal cycle. Norse-Germanic rune-birth (Edred Thorsson systems). African divination systems (Ifa Odu, Akan birth-day naming). Each of these has a defensible polymyth presence; v1 prioritized maximum cross-civilizational coverage with calculation-tractable systems. Future passes can add traditions per user request.

CROSS-REFERENCES. Baseball-card decentralized social media methodology entry (the deployment substrate). Primacy-of-beta-over-alpha methodology entry (caret-prefix, applied here at the username layer). Convention-default-on-bureaucratic-forms methodology entry (form design discipline). Idiomsmashing methodology entry (the Layer 2 character-smashing operation extends this from idioms to figures). Earth-equality / dirt-as-scanner-position methodology entry (the burrowing-animal selection grounds the user at the dirt-layer). Hegelianegirl methodology entry (the cocoon-stage universal that the character-creator helps the user particularize through). Anti-method-fossilization rules (every-visit-is-ouroboros, the card is not a saved profile, paste-back-from-email-archive forces re-engagement).

ORIGIN. April 29 2026 cyberphunk-subtitle session, post-bb-gate-build, post-primacy-of-beta-over-alpha-rule, post-Netlify-Forms-architecture-decision. Rainbowsol directive: "from past discussions, just start with all the regular dungeons and dragons character building questions, the ones that are important for story; then combine it with our character smashing rhetoric; make a list of characters/heroes/people you admire AND WHY, smash them together, create your own unique character / add it to birth year horoscopes from all traditions — this needs to be robust and not wishy washy, comprehensive no bullshit horoscopes lol — and all those kinds of questions into a comprehensive character builder; the one bookwormburrows kind of question that we can add from the start is their starting animal burrowing character that they choose; lets make a comprehensive list of animals that burrow. starting with the worm. can cats burrow? lol." Built same session.

EXTENSION:
April 29 2026 build, single-batch ship. Five horoscope traditions × 12-20 archetype writeups each = 76 archetype writeups in JS data structures. 38 burrowing-animal archetypes with operational signatures. 10 D&D story-spine fields. 5 character-smashing rows + synthesis textarea. All in one /bookwormcard/ page with popout architecture. Ship-state.

TITLE: HEGELIANEKITTY-TIER-MARKER
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Tier-marker awarded on the bookwormburrows character card to users who supply Vedic-grade birth-data: full date plus hour plus place. Visible on the card as the sigil ◉ followed by the birth-coordinates. Distinguished from lower-grade markers (date-only, no-data) by precision of horoscopy-substrate.

Hegelianekitty is the tier-marker awarded on the bookwormburrows character card to users who supply Vedic-grade birth-data: full date plus hour plus place. Visible on the card as the sigil ◉ followed by the words "hegelianekitty tier · vedic-grade." Mechanically: a single boolean flag on the horoscope-readout object; renders as a gradient-banded badge in the visual card and as a dedicated line in the plain-text card. The mechanic enforces structural coupling between the deepest cosmological tradition (Vedic jyotish requires moon-position computation requiring time-and-place) and the marker that signals the user opted into that depth. Hegelianekitty is not a gameplay-effect: it does not unlock additional content, modify other readings, or grant computational privileges. It is purely an opt-in-visibility marker — a self-signal embedded in the card declaring "this user provided full birth-data." Function: communicates to anyone who encounters the card that the bearer engaged the framework at maximum depth available in v1. Anti-gamification: the marker has no in-system reward, only the dignity of public commitment. Per polymyth methodology: "level-up" mechanics that grant power-tokens fall into RPG-as-ladder failure mode; hegelianekitty awards visibility-of-having-done-the-work, not the work's leverage. Linked: cyberphunkisms-self-naming, hegel-jung-synthesis-archive (the name itself), polymyth-horoscope-multi-tradition-concrescence.

TITLE: BURROWING-ANIMAL-ROSTER-AS-CHARACTER-FOUNDATION
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Bookwormburrows character-design rule: each bookworm-character draws from the burrowing-animal roster as foundational substrate (mole, rabbit, badger, fox, etc.). The burrowing-animal anchors the character’s movement-substrate (hole-in-hole-out architecture per Burrow-as-wormhole) before any other character-traits get layered on.

The bookwormburrows character creator at /bookwormcard/ offers selection from 38 burrowing animals organized by phylogenetic group: 12 invertebrates, 4 reptiles, 2 amphibians, 1 fish, 3 birds, 16 mammals. Each carries an operational-signature writeup in bookwormburrows-pedagogy register. EARTHWORM is canonical position #1 — the bookworm-ancestor, the figure that eats text-substrate and excretes the medium gardens grow in. CATS ARE EXCLUDED structurally: cats are occupiers, not burrowers. The bookworm-in-burrow archetype is what cats are antagonist to (cat circles burrow waiting for worm to emerge). Including cats would dissolve the foundational opposition. Roster spans phylogenetic spread to honor that burrowing is a strategy multiple kingdoms independently arrived at: lungfish (mucus-cocoon estivation), spadefoot toad (years of dormancy ending in explosive emergence), naked mole rat (eusocial mammal-as-insect-colony), pangolin (chambered burrows large enough for human sleep, critically endangered to species-level human predation), polar bear (largest burrowing animal, maternity-only). Function in the creator: user selects one animal whose mode-of-operation feels closest to their own; the writeup becomes character-construction substrate, not personality-test result. The animal is the bookwormburrow-substrate of the character, not the character's "spirit animal." Pedagogical move: turning the predator-prey axis (cat-versus-worm) into a structural exclusion teaches the framework's first move — what the polymyth excludes is more diagnostic than what it includes.

EXTENSION:
38 burrowing animals as character-creator foundation. Worm canonical #1. Cats excluded structurally (occupiers vs burrowers). Phylogenetic spread honors burrowing as cross-kingdom strategy.

TITLE: CHARACTER-CREATOR-ARCHITECTURE-SIX-SECTION-CONCRESCENCE
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Bookwormburrows character-creator architectural rule. SIX SECTIONS concresce into a single character: (1) burrowing-animal foundation, (2) admired-heroes for smashing, (3) horoscopy-substrate, (4) self-naming slot, (5) starting cave-instances, (6) stampcard initial-state. The concrescence at character-creation layer instantiates Whitehead-metaphysical concrescence at the bb*-pedagogy register.

The bookwormburrows character creator at /bookwormcard/ deploys a six-section concrescence pattern: (1) GATE — handle, email, year (mandatory). (2) D&D SESSION-ZERO QUESTIONS — backstory, motivation, fear, fatal flaw, bond, ideal, secret, pivotal event (eight optional fields drawn from standard D&D character-builder protocols). (3) CHARACTER-SMASHING — five admired-figure / quality-taken pairs (the smashed-character is the composite of these qualities plus the user's particulars; deploys polymyth idiomsmashing at the figure-layer rather than the phrase-layer). (4) POLYMYTH HOROSCOPE BIRTH-DATA — month, day, hour, minute, place (gradient unlock pattern: progressively more readings as more data supplied; full data unlocks hegelianekitty tier). (5) BURROWING ANIMAL — one of 38 from phylogenetically-organized roster. (6) WILDCARD — free text, anything else. ARCHITECTURE: all six sections start collapsed (popped-in); user clicks to pop sections out, fills what they want, leaves rest blank. Single submit returns integrated card combining all sections-with-content. Sections without content are omitted from the card output. Anti-completion-pressure: there is NO "fill all sections to be a real character" implication — the wildcard section explicitly invites a one-line submission. Per polymyth methodology: maximalist content-availability paired with minimalist completion-requirement. The user does not have to use the polymyth horoscope to participate; they CAN use it. Substrate: /bookwormcard/index.html (single page, all logic inline JS, depends on polymyth-horoscope.js + archetypes-set1-3.js + burrowing-animals.js corpus files). Output: comprehensive plain-text card built from filled sections only, with hash, hegelianekitty marker (if earned), and visible-on-card reading-listings. Submitted via Netlify Forms (form-name: bb-character-creator) for storage and email-routing. SUPERSEDED BY MATRIX-CHAT-ARCHITECTURE entry below — this six-section pattern was the v1.0 form-based deployment; v1.1 collapsed everything into a single matrix-chat at /bb/.

EXTENSION:
Character creator: 6 sections (gate / D&D / smashing / horoscope / animal / wildcard), all collapsed by default. SUPERSEDED by matrix-chat architecture in v1.1.
