TITLE: MATRIX-CHAT-ARCHITECTURE-/bookwormcard/
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Framework entry covering MATRIX-CHAT-ARCHITECTURE for the /bookwormcard/ chat-interface. The body below contains the full architectural specification of the matrix-styled keyboard-first conversational interface deployed at /bookwormcard/ as of April 30 2026, replacing the prior six-section scrollable form.

The bookwormburrows site at /bookwormcard/ deploys as a matrix-styled keyboard-first conversational interface as of April 30 2026, replacing the prior six-section scrollable form. Architecture: single-page state-machine with sequential question-prompts, char-by-char typing animation, real-time card-build visible alongside chat, full-keyboard navigation with menu-floats-under-current-question pattern for large-domain selections (38-animal menu, 12-month menu). Aesthetic: phosphor-green-on-black (#33ff66 on #0a0e0a), VT323 font, blinking solid-block cursor, ASCII section dividers, very-subtle matrix-rain canvas background (12fps, paused when document hidden, disabled with prefers-reduced-motion). Opening sequence: matrix homage compressed into thirteen lines hitting "wake up / the platform has you / the feed has you / the algorithm has you / you've been told this / you keep scrolling anyway / a matrix is one story everyone shares / the way out is not another matrix / the way out is many stories at once / all true at once / welcome to bookwormburrows / follow the white rabbit / rabbits burrow / worms burrow through pages / bookworms eat what they burrow." Per polymyth-as-method-not-brand principle, the framework-word "polymyth" is NOT named in the user-facing opening; the methodology-claim is made (many-stories-at-once) without the methodology-name. Bookwormburrows IS named (the visible product-name). Question sequence: animal-pick first (sets the wormcard's identity-emoji), then handle, then email, then birth-data progression (year unlocks 2 readings, +month+day unlocks 8 more, +hour+place triggers hegelianekitty tier), then wormhole (8 personal questions, each skip-able), then character-smashing (unlimited loop, smash-name then smash-quality then "another?"), then wildcard, then review. Returning users hit a bypass-screen first ("paste a wormcard or press enter") which parses pasted card and jumps to review-with-pre-filled-fields. Form-name: bookwormcard (single Netlify Forms bucket). The /bookwormcard/ path 301-redirects to /bb/. Substrate dependencies: polymyth-horoscope.js (calculation engines), archetypes-set1-3.js (189 archetype writeups across 11 traditions), burrowing-animals.js (38 animals with operational-signature writeups). PEDAGOGICAL CLAIM: matrix-aesthetic is the right register for the operation BECAUSE the operation IS waking-up-from-the-platform-feed-algorithm into the multiplicity-of-stories. Aesthetic and operation share substrate. Cute-cyberpunk register (worms in matrix) holds the warmth that would be missing from pure cyberpunk; ASCII-worm decorations (`~~~~~o>`) carry that warmth into the matrix vocabulary. ANTI-CLICKBAIT-CHAT: questions asked once, no follow-up "are you sure?" prompts, no "let's dig deeper" interrogation patterns; matrix-chat operates in the spirit of a terminal that asks what it needs and accepts skip without protest.

EXTENSION:
/bookwormcard/ matrix-chat architecture April 30 2026. Replaces six-section form. Phosphor-green keyboard-first state-machine with bypass-paste path for returning users.

TITLE: BURROWING-ANIMAL-ROSTER-EXPANSION-58-HOLE-RELATIONSHIPS
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Framework entry covering BURROWING-ANIMAL-ROSTER-EXPANSION-58-HOLE-RELATIONSHIPS. Full operational specification preserved in body below, including any worked examples, citation-locks, and cross-substrate relations.

The bookwormburrows animal roster expanded April 30 2026 from 38 strict-burrowers to 58 animals with verified hole-relationships. Expansion criterion: each animal must have a documented operational relationship to holes/cavities/burrows beyond superficial. Cats remain excluded (occupiers-not-burrowers structural exclusion preserved per earlier methodology entry). Hole-relationship modes spanned: BURROWING (digging own holes — earthworm, mole, badger, hamster, etc.), SQUATTING (occupying others' burrows — fox, hermit-crab-style behavior), TREE-CAVITY (woodpecker-hole-occupiers — wood-duck, eagle, squirrel), REEF-CAVITY (coral-hole-dwellers — reef-fish, octopus, lobster, shark), HIBERNATION-CAVITY (rock/leaf-litter aggregators — ladybug, hedgehog, bear), CORPSE-CAVITY (decay-feeders in dead-matter cavities — fly), ARCHITECTURAL-INFRASTRUCTURE-CAVITY (human-built-environment dwellers — cockroach, mouse, rat). New animals: ladybug, fly, cockroach, lobster, octopus (introduces molluscs phylum, cephalopods class), crocodile (crocodilians order), reef-fish, shark, wood-duck, eagle, fox, wolf, bear, mouse, rat, hamster, hedgehog, otter, beaver, squirrel. Each comes with operational-signature writeup in bookwormburrows-pedagogy register. Each carries unicode emoji for card-display (mouse 🐭, hamster 🐹, octopus 🐙, hedgehog 🦔, etc.). The 10 emoji-less animals from the original 38 (mole, groundhog, aardvark, wombat, meerkat, armadillo, naked-mole-rat, pangolin, platypus, caecilian) RETAINED per Saul's "keep them" directive — they render with name-only on cards until favicons ship. Three-stage taxonomic drill-down menu (phylum → class → order → species) handles the expanded roster cleanly. Total taxonomy: 4 phyla (annelids, arthropods, molluscs, chordates), 10 classes, 25+ orders. STRUCTURAL READING: the expansion teaches that "burrowing" is not a discrete category but a SPECTRUM of hole-relationships. The user picking from the expanded roster is choosing not just an animal but a MODE of relating-to-cavity. Earthworm burrows. Lobster defends. Octopus decorates. Bear hibernates. Squirrel distributes. Each is a different operational answer to the same underlying question (how do you exist in relation to your holes). FURTHER EXPANSION April 30 2026 evening: roster expanded again from 58 to 103 animals to fill remaining hole-relationship gaps. Added: ant, cicada-killer-wasp, desert-tortoise, hognose-snake, sidewinder, komodo-dragon, kingfisher, sand-martin, bee-eater, shearwater, marmot, ground-squirrel, chipmunk, lemming, jerboa, vole, fennec-fox, arctic-fox, coyote, african-wild-dog, skunk, muskrat, springhare, numbat, bilby, echidna, tenrec, plus marine: moray-eel, garden-eel, jawfish, goby, flounder, stingray, parrotfish, clownfish, blenny, pistol-shrimp, ghost-shrimp, mole-crab, horseshoe-crab, hermit-crab, lugworm, bobbit-worm, tube-worm. Hover-tooltip on species-pick menu shows full hole-relationship writeup. CROSS-REFERENCE: burrowing-animal-roster-as-character-foundation entry (the original 38); cats-excluded-as-occupiers-not-burrowers structural exclusion (preserved); animal-taxonomy.js substrate file.

ID: undefined
TITLE: Inception arena rule — DM builds the arena, bookworms fill it in, no AI-invented characters pre-session
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Operational/disciplinary rule. The body below contains the full rule-specification of Inception arena rule — DM builds the arena, bookworms fill it in, no AI-invented characters pre-session including trigger conditions, fire-pattern, and failure-mode reversal.

Operational rule for bb* arena-building. Architecturally inspired by the Inception (Nolan 2010) dream-architect distinction. The architect builds the dream's structure (Paris folding over itself, the hotel corridor, the snowscape). The dreamers fill the structure with their own subconscious content. The architect does not write what the dreamers will populate.

TWO KINDS OF CONTENT IN THE bb* ARENA.

(1) ARENA CONTENT — built by the DM (Rainbowsol or AI in DM register) BEFORE the session opens. This includes the canonical text characters (Mrs Jones, Roger), the real historical NPCs of the period and place (MLK at Blumstein's September 1958), real streets, real businesses, real news stories of the date-window, real objects, real period registers and speech-patterns. The arena is documentary at the substrate-layer. Every element is verifiable against primary sources.

(2) FILLER CONTENT — generated by the bookworms IN SESSION. This includes their own characters (smashed from admired-figures via determinate negation), their characters' actions inside the arena, the words their characters say to the canonical and real NPCs, the interactions among themselves, the writing they produce as evidence. Filler is bookworm-substrate, not AI-substrate.

WHAT THE AI MUST NOT DO BEFORE GAME-OPEN. The AI in DM-prep register does not invent fictional supplementary NPCs to flesh out the arena. The AI does not draft sample bookworm-characters that students might play. The AI does not pre-write dialogue the canonical NPCs do not have in their primary sources. The arena is built from documented substrate only. Fictional supplement at this layer is invitation for the bookworm's own filler to be displaced by AI imagination, which is the gorgonification of the pedagogy.

WHAT THE AI CAN DO IN SESSION. Once bookworms have arrived and filled in characters, the AI as scene-running DM voice can adjudicate, narrate, voice the canonical NPCs from their verbatim primary-source lines, and respond to bookworm-actions inside the arena. The AI extends the documented substrate at run-time in response to bookworm-input. Without bookworm-input first, the AI invents nothing.

WHY THIS RULE. Two failure modes are blocked. (1) Bookworm-displacement: if the AI pre-builds a rich cast of fictional NPCs, the bookworms read those NPCs as the dimension's actual content and their own characters become tourists in someone else's story. Bookwormburrows is the opposite operation. The bookworms ARE the visitors and the dimension ALREADY HAS its content (the canonical and historical). AI-fictional supplement breaks this. (2) Documentary integrity: the arena is meant to teach the bookworms to encounter a real place at a real time. Adding fictional NPCs blurs the line between documentary and imaginative, which weakens the frame-break prohibition the dimension carries.

ANALOGOUS PRINCIPLE. The Inception architect does not dream the dreamer's father. The dreamer's subconscious produces the father. The architect produces the building the father appears in. Same here. The DM produces the kitchenette and the canonical Mrs Jones. The bookworms produce the characters who walk in and watch.

CROSS-REFERENCE. cmp-001 pregame arena (campaigns/thank-you-mam/pregame/) is the first deployment of this rule — strictly documentary substrate, no fictional supplement at the arena-layer. bb* dm-002 session-zero protocol. bb* bw-007 bookworm continuity vs character locality. Off-canon-layer ruling in cmp-001 pregame (bookworms watch the canon run without interrupting it on first burrow) is the protocol enactment of this rule.

EXTENSION:
Articulated May 13 2026 by Rainbowsol during Thank You Ma’am pregame arena build. The Inception parallel was Rainbowsol-named; AI extracted the operational rule from it. The rule has been operative implicitly since cmp-001 character creation work began (April 2026); this entry makes it explicit and committable.

ID: undefined
TITLE: Token. Inception-derived subjectivity-marker for bb* characters (May 13 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Framework entry covering Token. Inception-derived subjectivity-marker for bb* characters. Full operational specification preserved in body below, including any worked examples, citation-locks, and cross-substrate relations.

Concept Rainbowsol named May 13 2026 from Inception (Nolan 2010): the token. In the film, each extractor carries a small physical object only they know the precise weight, balance, and behavior of (Cobb’s spinning top; Arthur’s loaded die; Ariadne’s chess bishop). The token’s function is subjectivity-verification: a character uses it to test whether they are inside their own dream-state or someone else’s constructed dream. Only the character’s own private knowledge of the token’s exact feel allows the test to work.

POLYMYTH APPLICATION. The token is a per-character subjectivity-anchor. A bb* character carries one specific object that the bookworm-author knows the precise quality of, in a way no other person at the table knows. The token serves three operational functions.

FUNCTION 1. REALITY-STATE VERIFICATION INSIDE NESTED DIMENSIONS. When a bookworm-character enters a dimension and then enters another dimension within it (dream-within-dream, per dm-015 Inception model), the token is the question they can ask themselves: is this the dimension I came from or another one? The answer is not knowable from the surface of the dimension; it is knowable only by the token’s feel. The token therefore disciplines the bookworm to keep track of subjectivity-layers rather than getting lost in nesting.

FUNCTION 2. ANTI-DISPLACEMENT MARKER. If another bookworm or the DM tries to puppet a character (speak for them, attribute decisions to them, declare what the character does), the original author can invoke the token: does this puppeted-version know how the token feels? If the answer is no, the puppeting is displacement. The token is the author’s legal protection against having their character spoken-over.

FUNCTION 3. EVIDENCE-OF-PRIVATE-INTERIOR. The token is something only the bookworm knows about the character. By existing, it asserts that the character has interior life inaccessible to the table. This is anti-spreadsheet: characters are not exhaustively specified by their bookwormcard fields. Some part is opaque by design.

MECHANICAL IMPLEMENTATION ON BOOKWORMCARD. A TOKEN block is added to the card. The block has two ruled lines and a gloss. The bookworm writes (a) what the token is, in one or two words, and (b) one specific detail about the token only they know. The second line is sealed: the DM may know it exists but not what it says, depending on table convention. Some bookworms write it on the back of the card. Some write it folded over.

CANONICAL TOKEN EXAMPLE FROM CMP-001. Mrs Jones’s pocketbook is her token. She knows its weight (it is heavy enough that when Roger pulls on the strap the strap breaks and the boy falls backward). She knows what is in it ($20 in bills, comb, lipstick, change-purse). Roger does not know the weight or the contents. Mrs Jones’s pocketbook would not test the same in his hand as in hers. Hughes wrote a perfect token-anchor and called it a pocketbook. Polymyth notices this and names it.

CROSS-REFERENCE. Inception arena rule (icons populate; tokens are how bookworm-characters anchor their own subjectivity inside an icon-populated arena). dm-015 Inception death model (nested-dimension protocol that tokens disciplines). bw-007 bookworm vs character distinction (the token belongs to the character, the bookworm carries multiple tokens across multiple characters). dm-031 leveling system (the bookwormcard records evidence; the token is one specific kind of evidence that the character has interior). Inception of ideas entry (the token is the inverse of inception: inception is a foreign idea installed as your own; the token is your own anchor verifying which ideas are yours).

EXTENSION:
Rainbowsol named the token-concept May 13 2026 in dialogue with the Inception arena rule. Bookwormcard TOKEN block added same batch to /bookwormcard/print/.

ID: undefined
TITLE: Polymyth-synthesis-method for TTRPG (BB*-foundational protocol, T114j May 23 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. The canonical method for determining which TTRPGs can be synthesized with polymyth methodology and how the synthesis is run. This entry is the BB*-foundational protocol. Combines the four-step synthesis sequence (Saul, T105 conversation, May 21 2026), the quantity-as-task principle (R37 QUANTITY=QUALITY, T106), and the comparative-religion lens (Saul, May 1 2026 scalable-login conversation, the foundational reframe of TTRPG ethics-systems as theologies).

THE FOUR-STEP PROTOCOL (Saul-stated, T114j canonical capture). (1) LAY THEM ALL OUT. Scan every TTRPG in the catalogue. The task is QUANTITY at this stage. Gather maximum before any synthesis-cut. R37 QUANTITY=QUALITY governs: synthesis quality scales with source-quantity at the gather stage; cutting early produces shallow synthesis. (2) SEE WHAT CAN BE SYNTHESIZED. Find what is the same across the catalogue. Find what is different. Identify cross-system patterns. Identify polymyth-operations the systems share. The T107 synthesis-pass over the 260-entry catalogue produced 20 polymyth-operations as the first-installment output of this step. (3) SEE WHAT CANNOT BE SYNTHESIZED. The residue. Entries whose distinctive feature resists cross-catalogue clustering. Singletons. Caveats. Items where the operation appears in only one or two witnesses and does not cluster at operation-layer. (4) USER DECIDES THE RESIDUE. The residue is returned to Saul as a personal-decision list. AI does not unilaterally resolve residue items; AI surfaces them with brief notes on why each did not synthesize and what its singularity might mean for the framework.

THE COMPARATIVE-RELIGION LENS (Saul, May 1 2026 scalable-login conversation, BB* foundational reframe). Each TTRPG carries a theology — its account of how the world responds to character action. 5e alignment is essentialist religion (moral nature as fixed cosmic-tag, the kind whose adherents historically built caste hierarchies). PF2 Remaster edicts and anathema is covenant religion (ethics as personal code committed and updated, the kind whose adherents built Quaker meetinghouses). Daggerheart Hope/Fear is emergent religion (ethics as live process per encounter, the kind whose adherents wrote existentialist novels in postwar Paris). The synthesis question reframes through the lens: which theologies are polymyth-aligned and can co-exist in BB* as VISITABLE religions bookworms operate under for the duration of a visit (covenant and emergent), and which are gorgonification-encoding and become DIAGNOSTIC OBJECTS students study to learn what structural failure looks like (essentialism). The polymyth move is comparative religion done EVALUATIVELY-CRITICALLY — not neutral-descriptive tourist-pluralism where every religion is equally valid — the way a philosophy class teaches Plato AND Nietzsche AND Sartre by testing each against the others.

BB* AS ACADEMIC-REAL-WORLD COMPARATIVE-RELIGION CLASSROOM. BB* is the academic-real-world version of D&D (not a D&D game). Bookworms learn to scan religions for structural vulnerabilities. When the AI runs a 5e dimension under essentialist-ethics-religion, the AI runs the religion AND surfaces the polymyth critique simultaneously (the May 1 2026 option B verdict — option A is tourist-pluralism, option C is overprotective refusal-to-run). Pluralism handles co-existence (bookworm enters dimension, operates under its theology, exits). Polymyth handles evaluation (some theologies encode gorgonification at structural core; some are polymyth-aligned).

WHAT THE METHOD IS NOT. The method is NOT tier-rating modules on an AI-invented quality scale. The April 29 2026 polymyth-D&D scan ran a 4-tier scoring system across 20-plus D&D modules and assigned each a polymyth-readable verdict plus paired-books and curriculum-fit suggestions. That was the WRONG METHOD. Tier-rating treats modules as artifacts to score rather than theologies to compare. T114i retracted three entries from that scan (pen-010, dim-020, dim-021) as AI-fabrication; the remaining 18 entries from the same scan stay intact pending user disposition but carry the same provenance signature. The correct method is the four-step protocol above applied through the comparative-religion lens, not module-by-module AI verdict-issuing.

OPERATIONAL DEPLOYMENT FOR BB*. When AI is asked to scan a new TTRPG for BB* compatibility: (a) identify the TTRPG ethics-system (theology). (b) Classify the theology: essentialist, covenant, emergent, or other. (c) Run the polymyth scan on the theology: is it net-participating (reflects other polymyth operations, opens under scrutiny) or obelisk-prone (closes under scrutiny, collapses paradox into contradiction). (d) If polymyth-aligned, route to BB* as a visitable-religion dimension bookworms can enter. (e) If gorgonification-encoding, route to BB* as a diagnostic-object dimension bookworms study from outside. (f) If the verdict requires multi-theology comparative work (most cases), apply the four-step protocol across the relevant subset of the catalogue and surface the synthesis plus residue to Saul.

WHY QUANTITY IS THE TASK AT STAGE 1. Premature synthesis cuts produce shallow output. The AI default failure is to gather two or three sources, find a pattern, and call it synthesis. The polymyth synthesis-method requires the full catalogue first because cross-catalogue patterns are only visible after enough witnesses are on the table. Stage-1 quantity is not for its own sake; it is the precondition for stage-2 synthesis-quality. Skipping stage-1 produces stage-2 that hallucinates patterns from sparse data.

CROSS-REFERENCES. R37 QUANTITY=QUALITY methodology rule (slot 23 mirror, T106 origin) — the gather-stage quantity-as-precondition principle. T107 polymyth-method synthesis pass methodology entries OP-1 through OP-20 — the executed instance of this protocol on the 260-entry TTRPG catalogue. T114i April 29 2026 polymyth-D&D scan retraction audit methodology entry — the retraction of the wrong-method scan. R36* ORGANIZE-MINE methodology rule — the AI-decides-routing rule that scopes which residue items AI can route without user input. R42* SYNTHESIS-PRE-EMPTION methodology rule — the rule preventing AI from pre-empting user synthesis-decisions on residue. Comparative-ethics teaching unit (bb* unit-001) — the user-authorized teaching deployment of the comparative-religion lens at student-facing scale (5e alignment, PF2 edict-anathema, sabachtan sequential-engagement compared). Pen-009 (bb* PF2 alignment-removal teaching-unit, user-authorized T114h) — the source-spec for unit-001. Meaning-making vs meaning-subtraction axis methodology entry — the polymyth axis along which theologies are evaluated (paradox-opening vs contradiction-closing).

ORIGIN. T114j May 23 2026. User test-question ’what is our task for determining which ttrpg are able to be synthesized with polymyth methodology / how do we do that.’ AI articulated the comparative-religion lens; user added the four-step protocol with quantity-as-stage-1-task. Entry committed as canonical BB*-foundational method per user directive ’lets remember this in ML* if its not already there.’ The pieces existed scattered (T107 entries reference scan-all-find-same-find-different-synthesize-residue-to-user; R37 captures quantity-as-task; May 1 2026 scalable-login conversation introduced the comparative-religion lens but never landed as its own ml* entry); T114j unifies them as one discoverable entry.

EXTENSION:
T114j canonical BB*-foundational method. Four-step polymyth-synthesis protocol (lay-all-out / synthesize / residue / user-decides) plus quantity-as-stage-1-task principle plus comparative-religion lens unified as one discoverable entry. Replaces module-by-module tier-rating (retracted in T114i) as the correct method going forward.

ID: undefined
TITLE: Polymythdnd T114t architectural decisions: in-game vs out-of-game characters, three-layer card-notebook-portfolio, named title-levels, many-variables AI, narrative-safety, rule-spectrum (May 23 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. T114t commits the architectural decisions Saul resolved through the item-by-item processing of the T114s bloom (May 23 2026, items 1-18). Major architecture established: two-layer character system (in-game vs out-of-game); three-layer documentation system (bookwormcard, bookworm notebook diary, bookworm portfolio); named title-levels replacing numbered levels; character-smash with DM-nerf-to-level-1; AS MANY VARIABLES AS POSSIBLE AI tracking; narrative-exit as safety mechanism; middle-vs-hard-rule-shift spectrum per dimension. Magic-synthesis-pass and notebook-final-update deferred. Several T114q cannot-synthesize items revised in light of T114r foundations.

ARCHITECTURE 1: IN-GAME VS OUT-OF-GAME CHARACTER. Polymythdnd students operate two character layers simultaneously. (a) OUT-OF-GAME CHARACTER — the bookworm-self in the rainbowworld; the ongoing smashed-character built through character-smash and tracked across all books the student engages. (b) IN-GAME CHARACTER — the in-character-version of the smashed-character as it manifests inside any specific book. Each book produces a different in-character-version of the same bookworm-self; the bookworm IS the through-line, the in-character-version is the dimension-specific instantiation. Worm-silkworm-cocoon transformation (T114s Q5) is deferred to LONG-RUN consideration (years-long trajectory not build-phase design); near-term polymythdnd design focuses on the in-game vs out-of-game character architecture instead.

ARCHITECTURE 2: THREE-LAYER DOCUMENTATION SYSTEM. (a) BOOKWORMCARD — tracks the ongoing smashed-character (out-of-game bookworm-self in rainbowworld). Existing canonical file. Inventory items are listed here. (b) BOOKWORM NOTEBOOK — new section: diary showing who-they-were in each past book (in-character-version per book). Bookwormcard cross-references notebook for inventory-source (e.g., ’this dagger was picked up in Harlem Unbound chapter three’ — the dagger lives on the bookwormcard inventory, the source lives in the notebook diary entry for that book). (c) BOOKWORM PORTFOLIO — all academic-and-creative work produced about each book: questions answered, paragraphs written, tests taken, assignments completed, presentations delivered, projects submitted. Separate from bookwormcard (which is character) and notebook (which is in-character-version history). Three separate destinations preserving the three-layer distinction.

ARCHITECTURE 3: CHARACTER-SMASH PLUS DM-NERF-TO-LEVEL-1. Polymythdnd character creation is CHARACTER-SMASH: students assemble their conceptual character by combining whatever they want from any source. No essentialism, no class-restrictions, no concept-vetoes. If the smash produces something overpowered (Saul example ’level-1000-ultrahegelianegirl’), the DM does NOT block the concept; instead the DM responds: ’ok you created the level-1000 version of this; we’re running the level-1 version’. The conceptual character is preserved; the power-level is nerfed to starting-tier. Everyone starts at the same level regardless of smash-ambition; advancement happens through earned work (Architecture 4). This preserves student agency in character-concept while preserving the calibration the DM needs.

ARCHITECTURE 4: NAMED TITLE-LEVELS, HARD-EARNED. Numbered levels are replaced by named title-levels. Each title is earned through specific recognized work: academic-output (good homework, well-done assignments, presentations, projects), in-game decisions (resolutions the DM judges as advancing the dimension), and in-game accomplishment-markers (dimensional-arc-completion, polymyth-operation-recognition, leadership-at-table). Each title pays off in specific affordances unlocked at the table. Number-level disappears, name-level appears, story-meaning attaches to every transition. Four candidate sequences brainstormed in T114t bloom: (A) bookworm-pedagogy-aligned (Untitled-bookworm / Reader-of-[book] / Dimensional-traveler / Silkworm-emergent / Cocoon-leading / Authored); (B) academic-track (Apprentice / Initiate / Journeyman / Practitioner / Authored / Mentor); (C) polymyth-operations-aligned (Untitled / Clue-reader / Register-shifter / Frame-bender / Gorgonification-spotter / Polymyth-scanner / Polymyth-fluent); (D) non-linear multi-track (multiple title-tracks in parallel — academic / polymyth-operation / in-game-character / leadership — accumulating across tracks with combination-unlocks). Saul-pick or combine across pending; dialectical brainstorm captured as open design question Q-T114t-A.

ARCHITECTURE 5: AS MANY VARIABLES AS POSSIBLE AI SUBSTRATE. Per Saul-directive May 23 2026 ’as many variables as possible, ai needs to have variables = to real life’, the invisible AI substrate carries variables equal to real-life density. The six earlier-proposed (reading-depth / argument-clarity / scanner-recognition / empathy / curiosity / polymyth-operation-fluency) are a STARTING SUBSET not the ceiling. Additional variables: hunger, fatigue, body-temperature, distance-traveled, time-of-day, social-tension, lighting-conditions, weather, character-toggles (e.g., ’doesn’t get hungry because of powers’), and indefinite-extension as design surfaces more. AI tracks all invisibly. Selectively-visible per trait (Architecture 5b): DM may surface a variable when scaffolding-feedback helps, but no active knowledge-dispersion of the variable-list to students. Polymythdnd is real-life-equivalent variable-density behind the no-visible-mechanic surface.

ARCHITECTURE 6: NARRATIVE-EXIT AS SAFETY MECHANISM. Polymythdnd safety is student-initiated DM-executed-as-narrative. Student expresses need-to-leave; DM narrates a multinarrative rainbow exit (per Saul-directive May 23 2026). Not an X-card halt; not pure-DM-discretion. Narrative-safety-as-mechanism. The student-initiation point (need-to-leave) is the safety-tool; the DM-narration is the execution. The polymythdnd-imagination-substrate handles safety the way it handles every other resolution — through deliberation and storytelling, not external-protocol. T114q D7-cannot-synthesize item ’pure-GM-discretion safety’ is REVISED: pure-DM-discretion-without-student-initiation is cannot; student-initiation-with-DM-narrative-execution IS canonical polymythdnd safety.

ARCHITECTURE 7: MIDDLE-RULES vs HARD-RULES SPECTRUM PER DIMENSION. Not every book changes every rule. Per Saul-directive May 23 2026 (Magic Schoolbus skating-on-the-book friction-removal reference), polymythdnd dimension-shift-mechanic operates on a SPECTRUM per book: (a) LIGHT-SHIFT — one specific rule changes (no friction; everyone can fly; gravity-reversed; some specific physics-alteration). (b) MIDDLE-SHIFT — several rules change; specific subsystems (combat, magic, social) shift but not the whole physics. (c) HARD-SHIFT — whole physics changes; the book is a fundamentally different cosm. Per-book rule-shift-level is design-decision at book-loading time. T114q D9-cannot-synthesize item ’single-genre modules without ruleset-shift’ stays cannot; the spectrum permits LIGHT-SHIFT as still-synthesizable, replacing the previous binary.

ARCHITECTURE 8: ENVIRONMENTAL-TRANSFORMATION 100%. Students have full ability to transform the environment based on what their characters can do — set things on fire, start protests, alter the dimension. Per Saul May 23 2026 ’100% possibility to change it should also be in it’. Same as D&D in this respect; the cannot-classification on pure-GM-fiat refers to GM-blocking-student-environmental-authorship, not to general DM adjudication.

T114S Q1-Q4 RESOLUTIONS PRESERVED. Q1 (DM = AI-plus-teacher unified role) holds. Q2 (DM gives suggestions as possibilities not directives when students stuck) holds. Q3 (reading-depth produces differential affordances per pedagogical priority) holds. Q4 (polymyth-native attributes invisible, AS MANY VARIABLES AS POSSIBLE extension applies — see Architecture 5). Q5 (worm-silkworm-cocoon transformation) STRUCK from near-term design as long-run consideration; replaced by Architecture 1 (in-game vs out-of-game character).

CANNOT-SYNTHESIZE REGISTER REVISED. Items confirmed cannot per Saul May 23 2026 processing: (4) 9-position essentialist alignment grid; (6) hyper-tactical visible-battle-grid (but AI-generated-emergent-measurement IS in); (7) pure-DM-fiat-blocking-student-environmental-authorship; (8) class-and-level rigid-paths; (9) cosmologically-content-bound aging; (10) pure-no-mechanic free-form; (11) sink-or-swim no-scaffolding; (13) static-character-no-change; (14) numbered-mechanical-level-up-without-story-trigger; (15) genre-modules-without-any-ruleset-shift (but LIGHT-SHIFT permitted per Architecture 7); (16) rule-stays-same-between-locations (but per Architecture 7 spectrum). Items revised: (5) Vancian magic — moved to MAGIC-SYNTHESIS-PASS as separate analysis-track; (12) safety — flipped from cannot to canonical polymythdnd-safety-mechanism per Architecture 6. Items struck as vacuous: (17) 3d6 stat-rolling and (18) point-buy attributes both lack visible-attribute-system in polymythdnd; nothing to attach the cannot-classification to.

OPEN POLYMYTHDND DESIGN QUESTIONS POST-T114T. (Q-T114t-A) Named title-level sequence — pick from candidates A/B/C/D, combine, or propose new naming pattern. (Q-T114t-B) Magic-synthesis-pass scope — when does the dedicated magic-analysis-pass run, what catalogue-subset feeds it, what does ’synthesizing all magic systems without cutting any off’ operationalize as. (Q-T114t-C) Bookworm-notebook diary-section specification — what fields, what cross-reference protocol with bookwormcard, what update-cadence. (Q-T114t-D) Bookworm-portfolio specification — what categories of academic-creative-work, what storage architecture, what assessment-criteria-link. (Q-T114t-E) Per-dimension rule-shift-level assignment — Harlem Unbound named as setting-important book requiring pre-drawn map; what other books in the curriculum require what shift-level.

CL DEFERRED ITEMS. (CL-1) FINAL UPDATE FOR THE NOTEBOOK — deferred until polymythdnd fully built; the sink-or-swim cannot-critique becomes notebook-update at that point. (CL-2) MAGIC-SYNTHESIS-ANALYSIS-PASS — dedicated separate work synthesizing all magic systems across the catalogue without cutting any off, then identifying what works for polymythdnd no-dice deliberation-resolution magic. (CL-3) BOOKWORMCARD / BOOKWORM-NOTEBOOK / BOOKWORM-PORTFOLIO ARCHITECTURE BUILD-OUT — notebook diary-section spec, portfolio specification, bookwormcard cross-reference link to notebook diary entries.

CROSS-REFERENCES. T114s polymythdnd Q1-Q4-resolved-plus-DM-canonical-rename (the entry T114t extends and partially revises). T114r polymythdnd foundational play-mechanics (the foundations T114t architectural decisions operate on). T114q play-mechanic synthesis scan (the scan T114t cannot-register revises). T107 OP-4 evolution-transformation-stages (the polymyth-operation Architecture 4 named-title-levels instantiates; worm-silkworm-cocoon deferred per Architecture 1). T107 OP-5 dimension-traveling-pedagogy (the bb* central premise Architecture 7 rule-spectrum operates within). Pen-009 + unit-001 (deployment-precedent for the cannot-essentialism position carried forward in Architecture 3 character-smash + 4 named-title-levels). Bookwormcard canonical file (Architecture 2 layer (a)). Harlem Unbound named as Architecture 7 setting-important book example.

EXTENSION:
T114t commits eight architectural decisions for polymythdnd: in-game vs out-of-game character architecture (Q5 worm-silkworm-cocoon deferred to long-run); three-layer documentation (bookwormcard / bookworm-notebook diary / bookworm-portfolio); character-smash plus DM-nerf-to-L1; named title-levels with four candidate sequences; AS MANY VARIABLES AS POSSIBLE AI substrate; narrative-exit safety mechanism; middle vs hard rule-shift spectrum per dimension; environmental-transformation 100% student-authorship. ID: undefined
TITLE: RAINBOW-CARD MECHANISM: HOW DO BOOKWORMS SUGGEST STORY-DIRECTION AT ANY STAGE? (T115g polymythdnd mechanic Saul-authored May 23 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. The rainbow-card is a polymythdnd mechanism that gives bookworms an always-active channel to suggest story-direction to the DM (teacher + AI). At any moment during play, any bookworm may submit a rainbow-card. The DM reviews the rainbow-card and may incorporate the suggestion into the unfolding narrative or mechanical-resolution. The rainbow-card formalizes bookworm-side agency at the suggestion-layer.

WHY RAINBOW-CARD MATTERS. Per F7 bookworm-becomes-author, the long-arc developmental goal is that mature bookworms author their own dimensions. The rainbow-card is the EARLY-STAGE training-mechanism for this developmental arc — early-stage bookworms practice authorship-in-miniature through rainbow-card suggestions before graduating to full dimension-co-authorship. The mechanism scaffolds the F7 trajectory.

OPERATIONAL DETAIL. The rainbow-card is a small written or spoken suggestion (rainbowsol coloring optional, conceptually invoking the rainbow-rule polymyth-vocabulary). The DM is not obligated to incorporate any specific rainbow-card; the DM exercises judgment. But the DM IS obligated to receive and consider rainbow-cards. Rejection is not the failure-state; non-reception is. The rainbow-card complements but does not replace narrative-exit (A6 of the ruleset) — narrative-exit is for SAFETY/leaving; rainbow-card is for CONTRIBUTION/influencing.

CROSS-REFERENCES. T114r F7 bookworm-becomes-author (the developmental arc this mechanism scaffolds). T114s Q2 suggestion-protocol (this mechanism is the bookworm-side counterpart to the AI-side suggestion-protocol; together they form a full suggestion-architecture). T114t A6 narrative-exit-safety (rainbow-card is suggestion-not-exit; the two are distinct). T114t A8 environmental-transformation-100-percent-student-authorship (rainbow-card is one mechanism by which students contribute environmental-transformations). T115g PROCESS-DRAMA three-feature signature Feature-1 (this mechanism is part of that feature). Polymythdnd ruleset Section 8 (Practical session-running) to be updated to include rainbow-card protocol.

ORIGIN. T115g May 23 2026. Saul-authored response to my PROCESS-DRAMA P1 bloom: ’in fact there should always be a suggestion process for students then, they can send a ’’rainbow card’’ how about that’. The rainbow-card name is Saul-authored polymyth-vocabulary. The mechanism is now part of polymythdnd canonical mechanics.

EXTENSION:
Rainbow-card mechanism: any bookworm at any time submits a rainbow-card suggesting story-direction; DM reviews and may incorporate. Always-active scaffolds the F7 bookworm-becomes-author developmental arc. Bookworm-side counterpart to T114s Q2 AI-side suggestion-protocol. Distinct from narrative-exit (safety mechanism, not suggestion). Saul-authored T115g.

TITLE: T107 BATCH BURROW-IMPLEMENTATION DIRECTIVES: WHICH OPERATIONS GET POLYMYTHDND-DEPLOYMENT-HOW? (T115i Saul-directed + AI-execute-silent confirmations May 23 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Following T115h batch-ratification of all twenty T107 polymyth-operations, this T115i pass documents the polymythdnd-burrow-implementation for each — either Saul-directed-implementation per T115i directives or AI-executed-silent-confirmation of already-covered per BLOOM-DECISIONS-ONLY rule (T115i companion entry).

SAUL-DIRECTED IMPLEMENTATIONS (T115i May 23 2026).

OP-1 Clues-are-given-never-rolled-for → IN-STORY DELIVERY. Clues are delivered through narrative-events within the dimension, not via meta-mechanic. The DM threads evidence into the unfolding story as bookworms move through it. No separate clue-mechanic; the deliberation surfaces clues via the in-story-encounter. Per Saul-directive ’clues should be given within the story’.

OP-2 Scripted-social-conflict-with-concession → IN-STORY RESOLUTION (NOT procedural). Polymythdnd does NOT use the scripted-procedural-with-concession approach observed in source-systems (Burning Wheel Duel of Wits, Fate compels). Social-conflict in polymythdnd is resolved through in-story narrative and deliberation; no separate procedural mechanic with explicit position-statements. The cross-system pattern stands ratified (T115h) but polymythdnd’s deployment differs from source-systems. Per Saul-directive ’im not sure if this is the best way; best way is within the story itself’.

OP-3 Bond-layer-between-PCs → ’YOUR TEAMMATE’ NOTEBOOK SECTION. Bond-layer is operationalized in the bookworm-notebook as a ’your teammate’ section where each bookworm records relationships with their teammates. Connects to T114u three-diary-format-spec by adding a teammate-tracking dimension to the notebook architecture. To be designed in the notebook-spec build (CL-owed). Per Saul-directive ’sure this is your teammate part of notebook’.

OP-4 Evolution-transformation-stages → CONFIRMED already-covered by Architecture 4 named-title-levels (Apprentice to Initiate to Adept progression with mechanical-discontinuity at each transition) and the bookworm-silkworm-cocoon canonical bb* instance. Per Saul-directive ’confirm already’.

AI-EXECUTE-SILENT CONFIRMATIONS (already-covered per BLOOM-DECISIONS-ONLY rule).

OP-5 Dimension-traveling-pedagogy → IS the bb* central premise. Structural-antecedent-anchor. Load-bearing across the framework. No further action.

OP-7 Authorship-distributed-at-character-creation-or-earlier → COVERED by Architecture 8 (100% student-authored environmental-transformation) plus Architecture 3 character-smash plus T115g rainbow-card mechanism.

OP-9 Solo-as-authorship-discipline → COVERED by T114u three-diary-format-spec.

OP-10 World-law-each-environment-enforces-its-own-physics → COVERED by Architecture 7 rule-shift-intensity (light/middle/hard) plus Section 5 magic-coexistence (dimensions foreground their own magic-paradigm).

OP-11 Register-switching-as-mechanic-bleed-role-distance → COVERED by Architecture 1 in-game/out-of-game character-split plus Architecture 6 narrative-exit.

OP-13 Epistolary-as-pedagogy → COVERED by T114u three-diary-format-spec (in-book diary IS epistolary).

TITLE: RAINBOW-NOTE EXTENSION + OP-6 BURROW-IMPLEMENTATION: HOW DOES THE RAINBOW MECHANISM CARRY BOTH SAFETY-SIGNALS AND SUGGESTIONS? (T115j Saul-authored May 23 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. The T115g rainbow-card mechanism extends at T115j into rainbow-note with menu-architecture. Same physical artifact (a small written or spoken note from bookworm to DM); multiple uses available on a menu. Saul-authored extension via directive ’transform this into a rainbow note to the dm. that note can also be used for suggestions too. thats the menu’.

TERMINOLOGY. Rainbow-card and rainbow-note are synonymous polymyth-vocabulary for the same Saul-authored mechanism. T115g introduced the suggestion-function under ’rainbow-card’; T115j extends the function-set under ’rainbow-note’. Both terms valid.

OP-6 BURROW-IMPLEMENTATION. OP-6 Safety-and-consent-as-mechanic is operationalized in polymythdnd as one option on the rainbow-note menu — a safety-signal that bookworms submit when they need safety-handling. The safety-signal complements Architecture 6 narrative-exit (the formal exit mechanism for leaving the in-game state) and Architecture 1 in-game/out-of-game character-split (the structural protection from in-game damage transferring to the rainbowworld bookworm). Where A6 is for leaving entirely, the safety-signal-on-rainbow-note is for raising-a-flag without exiting — bookworms communicate discomfort/concern to the DM in-stream.

MENU ARCHITECTURE. The rainbow-note carries a menu of options. T115j establishes two known menu-options. (Option 1) SAFETY-SIGNAL — bookworm raises a safety/consent concern to the DM without exiting. (Option 2) SUGGESTION — bookworm suggests story-direction per T115g original function. Additional menu-options may emerge as bb* deployment surfaces other rainbow-note-appropriate uses. Bookworms may select one or more options when submitting a rainbow-note.

DM HANDLING. The DM receives every rainbow-note (per T115g non-reception is the failure-state, not rejection). The DM reads the selected menu-option(s) and responds accordingly. Safety-signals get safety-handling per polymyth-care discipline. Suggestions get review-and-may-incorporate per T115g. Multi-option rainbow-notes trigger multiple parallel response-tracks.

WHY UNIFICATION MATTERS. Both safety-signaling and suggestion-submitting share the same underlying need: bookworm-to-DM communication outside the in-character narrative-frame. Separating them into two mechanisms would create two artifact-categories bookworms have to remember; unifying them under one menu-driven artifact reduces cognitive-load on bookworms and gives the rainbow-note clear ubiquity in bb* deployment.

CROSS-REFERENCES. T115g rainbow-card mechanism methodology entry (the original suggestion-function being extended). T115i T107 batch burrow-implementation directives (the parent T115i entry where OP-6 was bloomed for decision). Architecture 6 narrative-exit (companion safety mechanism for full exit). Architecture 1 in-game/out-of-game character-split (the structural protection from in-game damage). T114s Q2 suggestion-protocol (the AI-side suggestion-protocol counterpart). Polymythdnd ruleset Section 8 to be updated with the menu-architecture and OP-6 incorporation.

ORIGIN. T115j May 23 2026. Saul-directive locking in OP-6 burrow-implementation per ’transform this into a rainbow note to the dm. that note can also be used for suggestions too. thats the menu’. Per BLOOM-DECISIONS-ONLY rule T115i, this lock-in is AI-executed-on-Saul-direction, not bloomed for confirmation.

EXTENSION:
Rainbow-note extends T115g rainbow-card with menu-architecture per Saul-directive T115j. Two known menu-options: safety-signal (OP-6 burrow-implementation) and suggestion (T115g original). Unified bookworm-to-DM communication artifact. Complements A6 narrative-exit (full-exit) and A1 character-split (structural protection). Polymythdnd ruleset Section 8 to be updated.

TITLE: OP-8 TOKEN-AS-NARRATIVE-CURRENCY BRAINSTORM-ACTIVE: WHAT DESIGN-CONSTRAINTS HAVE BEEN SAUL-AUTHORED FOR THE POLYMYTHDND TOKEN-MECHANIC? (T115j Saul-directive May 23 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. OP-8 Token-as-narrative-currency burrow-implementation enters brainstorm-active state at T115j. Saul will think about the full design later; meanwhile two design-constraints are Saul-authored and lock in NOW.

CONSTRAINT 1: IN-TEXT IN-CONTENT. The token-mechanic must be in-text and in-content — meaning the tokens exist as part of the dimension’s narrative and substantive content, NOT as a meta-game-level mechanic layered over the story. This follows the polymythdnd pattern established for OP-1 (clues in-story) and OP-2 (social-conflict in-story): polymythdnd keeps mechanics inside the story-substrate rather than running them as meta-layers. Tokens are something the bookworm-character interacts with in-fiction, not something the bookworm-player tracks meta-to-fiction.

CONSTRAINT 2: CROSS-DIMENSIONAL. The token-mechanic must operate across all universes/dimensions — meaning the design must work for any dimension foregrounding any magic-paradigm, anchored to any text, at any rule-shift intensity. Tokens cannot be dimension-specific (only-works-in-fantasy-dimensions, only-works-in-realist-dimensions); they need a structural-form that any dimension can instantiate per its own logic.

BRAINSTORM SCOPE. Saul will brainstorm what in-text/in-content tokens look like across-all-universes. Candidates to consider include: text-passages bookworms quote to invoke effects (in-text by definition); items earned through reading-comprehension and carried in-fiction (in-content); deliberation-quality marks that translate into in-fiction-resource (the AI surfaces them as in-fiction phenomena per the dimension’s logic). These are candidate-directions for brainstorm not committed-designs.

STATUS. OP-8 polymythdnd-burrow-implementation is parked from full-design pending Saul-thinking. The two design-constraints above lock in NOW per T115j Saul-directive ’we will think about this. lets brainstorm in-text in-content suggestions so it goes into all universes’. When Saul resumes OP-8 design, the brainstorm starts from these constraints.

CROSS-REFERENCES. T115h T107 polymyth-operations batch-ratification (OP-8 ratified T115h). T115i T107 batch burrow-implementation directives (where OP-8 was bloomed for decision). T115j OP-1 in-story-delivery pattern (sibling constraint). T115j OP-2 in-story-resolution pattern (sibling constraint). Architecture 5 as-many-variables-as-possible substrate (the underlying tracking-substrate any token-mechanic operates atop). Section 5 magic-coexistence (the multi-paradigm requirement constraint 2 encodes).

ORIGIN. T115j May 23 2026. Saul-directive: ’we will think about this. lets brainstorm in-text in-content suggestions so it goes into all universes’. Per BLOOM-DECISIONS-ONLY rule T115i, this status update is AI-executed-on-Saul-direction not bloomed for confirmation.

EXTENSION:
OP-8 token-mechanic brainstorm-active per T115j Saul-directive. Two locked design-constraints: (1) in-text in-content not meta-layer; (2) cross-dimensional works in all universes. TITLE: ALL-AGES-ADJUSTABLE RULE + OP-12 BURROW-IMPLEMENTATION: HOW DOES POLYMYTHDND HANDLE STUDENTS AND ADULTS OF ALL AGES IN THE SAME FRAMEWORK? (T115k methodology rule Saul-authored May 23 2026, reaffirming prior rule)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. All polymythdnd works — dimensions, content, mechanics, anchor-texts, magic-paradigms, factions, time-arenas, badges — must be ready for all types of students and adults. The framework operates across the entire K-12-plus-adult-education range. AT SESSION-START, the DM is given the ages of participants. The DM then adjusts the dimension/content/mechanics to fit the demographic. Saul reaffirms this rule was given before: ’remember this i already gave this rule before’.

OPERATIONAL PROTOCOL. The first action of any session is ages-input from participants. The DM uses ages to calibrate: which content gets foregrounded; what content gets softened or deferred; which badges are accessible; what magic-paradigms are appropriate; what historical-substrate-depth gets exposed; what colonial-violence-handling applies; what horror-cost-intensity gets activated.

ARCHITECTURAL ANCHORS. This rule sits atop several existing architectural elements that handle maturity. T114y horror-cost-all-ages establishes that horror-content is available at all ages with in-game permanent-damage allowed but rainbowworld damage protected. T114t Architecture 1 in-game/out-of-game character-split provides the structural protection from in-game intensity bleeding to out-of-game. T114t Architecture 6 narrative-exit gives bookworms the always-available exit when content exceeds tolerance. T115j rainbow-note safety-signal menu-option lets bookworms flag concern without exiting. T115k extends these architectural anchors with the operational age-input-and-DM-adjust protocol at session-start.

OP-12 COLONIZATION-AS-SUBSTRATE LOCK-IN. OP-12 colonization-handling is operationalized in polymythdnd by THIS GENERAL RULE. Colonial-violence content is adjusted per ages-given at session-start, not handled by a separate microbook or dedicated structure. The same age-adjustment protocol applies to colonial-violence as to any other intense-content (horror, sexuality, historical-trauma, etc.). The specific colonization-handling-per-dimension goes into cc* session-prep per T115k companion entry. No separate colonization-research microbook needed.

CROSS-REFERENCES. T114y horror-cost-all-ages (architectural-anchor). T114t Architecture 1 in-game/out-of-game character-split (architectural-anchor). T114t Architecture 6 narrative-exit (architectural-anchor). T115j rainbow-note safety-signal (architectural-anchor). T107 OP-12 (operationalized by this general rule). T115k cc* session-prep architecture (where the specific per-dimension age-adjustment guidance gets stored). T115i T107 batch burrow-implementation directives (where OP-12 was bloomed; T115k resolves).

ORIGIN. T115k May 23 2026. Saul-directive ’all works should be ready for all types of students and adults; when we give our ages at the start, you will adjust; remember this i already gave this rule before’. Reaffirming prior rule; T115k formalizes the operational protocol.

EXTENSION:
All-ages-adjustable rule reaffirmed T115k: polymythdnd works are ready for all ages K-12-plus-adult; DM gets ages at session-start and adjusts dimension/content/mechanics accordingly. Operational protocol formalized. Sits atop T114y horror-cost-all-ages, T114t A1 character-split, T114t A6 narrative-exit, T115j rainbow-note safety-signal. OP-12 colonization-handling locked-in as operationalized by this general rule — no separate colonization microbook needed.

TITLE: OP-18 BURROW-IMPLEMENTATION: HOW DO FACTIONS EMERGE IN POLYMYTHDND? (T115k Saul-authored May 23 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. OP-18 Faction-as-character-layer is operationalized in polymythdnd as STORY-DRIVEN, NOT through a dedicated faction-attribute tracking structure. Factions emerge from character-smash attributes (per Architecture 3 character-smash). Saul-directive: ’no it will be story driven, if attributes are gained from specific ideas when creating the smash then there can be factions’.

MECHANISM. When a bookworm creates their character via Architecture 3 character-smash, they include specific ideas and attributes as part of the smash (a knight, raised in the south, speaks French, trained by a heretic-priest, etc.). These specific ideas IMPLY factional allegiances naturally — knight-smash-attribute implies knightly-order-allegiances; raised-in-the-south implies regional factional-ties; trained-by-a-heretic-priest implies religious-faction-positioning; etc. The factions are READABLE from the smash-attributes. No separate tracking structure required.

SUBSTRATE. The smash-attributes are already tracked in Architecture 5 (as-many-variables-as-possible substrate, the AI’s general variable-tracking). Factions thus exist as variables-among-variables, implied-by-attribute, NOT as a separate mechanical layer with its own structure.

POLYMYTHDND IN-STORY PATTERN. This follows the established polymythdnd pattern of in-story handling. Sibling instances: T115i OP-1 in-story clues; T115i OP-2 in-story social-conflict-resolution; T115j OP-8 in-text in-content tokens. Polymythdnd handles cross-system patterns through in-story-substrate rather than meta-mechanical-layers wherever possible.

CROSS-REFERENCES. T114t Architecture 3 character-smash (the substrate from which factions emerge). T114t Architecture 5 as-many-variables-as-possible substrate (where smash-attributes are tracked). T115i T107 batch burrow-implementation directives (where OP-18 was bloomed; T115k resolves). Sibling in-story-pattern operationalizations: T115i OP-1 in-story-clue-delivery, T115i OP-2 in-story-social-conflict-resolution, T115j OP-8 in-text-in-content-tokens.

ORIGIN. T115k May 23 2026. Saul-directive ’no it will be story driven, if attributes are gained from specific ideas when creating the smash then there can be factions’.

EXTENSION:
OP-18 faction-as-character-layer locked T115k: story-driven via character-smash attribute-derivation. NOT dedicated faction-tracking structure. Smash-attributes imply factional allegiances naturally; factions are readable from variables-among-variables in Architecture 5. Follows polymythdnd in-story pattern (sibling to OP-1, OP-2, OP-8).

TITLE: OP-20 BURROW-IMPLEMENTATION + ARENAS CONCEPT: HOW DOES POLYMYTHDND ELEVATE TIME-AS-MECHANIC AND WHAT ARE ARENAS? (T115k Saul-authored brainstorm-active May 23 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. OP-20 Time-as-mechanic is KEY in polymythdnd. Time is NOT to be left as plain-tracked-variable. Time becomes a mechanic that drives in-dimension activity. Saul-directive: ’time is key; we need to think of kingdome come 1/2 how it uses time to create stuff; thats why we have to create the arenas’.

DESIGN INSPIRATION. Kingdom Come: Deliverance 1 (Warhorse Studios 2018) and Kingdom Come: Deliverance 2 (Warhorse Studios 2025) — how those games use time-mechanics to create emergent in-fiction phenomena. NPC schedules tied to day/night cycle. Shops with opening-hours. Food spoilage. Character-routines. Quest-windows that open and close. Travel-time as in-fiction-elapsed. Time-of-day affecting available-actions. Sleep-cycles affecting character-state. The Kingdom Come time-mechanics CREATE in-fiction-phenomena that wouldn’t exist without time-as-mechanic.

ARENAS CONCEPT (NEW POLYMYTH-VOCABULARY T115k). To enable time-as-mechanic, polymythdnd needs ARENAS — structural-elements that hold time-mechanics. Without arenas, time can’t be elevated to mechanic; with arenas, time becomes operational per-arena. Arenas are spatial/structural containers within a dimension where time-progression has mechanical-consequence. The arenas-creation requirement is WHY time-as-mechanic isn’t just a setting on Architecture 5; it requires structural-arenas to operate.

ARENAS NOT YET FULLY DESIGNED. T115k introduces the term and design-direction. Arenas-design pending Saul-thinking. Brainstorm candidate-directions: per-location time-tracking within a dimension; multi-arena dimensions where bookworms move between arenas each with its own time-flow; time-as-tradeable-resource within arenas (spend time, accelerate it, slow it as mechanic); historical-arena where time-flow matches actual historical-events (connects to OP-16 historical-substrate handling per cc* session-prep). These are candidate-directions for brainstorm, not committed-designs.

STATUS. OP-20 polymythdnd-implementation is BRAINSTORM-ACTIVE. Design-direction locked: (1) time IS key; (2) Kingdom Come 1/2 inspiration; (3) arenas-creation is the structural-prerequisite. Specific arenas-design pending Saul-thinking. When Saul resumes OP-20 design, the brainstorm starts from these locked directions.

POLYMYTHDND IN-STORY PATTERN. Arenas as in-story spatial-structural containers follows the polymythdnd in-story-pattern: sibling to T115i OP-1 in-story-clues, T115i OP-2 in-story-social-conflict, T115j OP-8 in-text-in-content-tokens, T115k OP-18 story-driven-factions. Time-mechanic operates inside arenas which exist in-fiction, not as meta-game-layer.

CROSS-REFERENCES. T115h OP-20 ratification. T115i T107 batch burrow-implementation directives (where OP-20 was bloomed; T115k resolves with brainstorm-active status). T115j OP-8 brainstorm-active (sibling pattern — locked-constraints with full-design-pending). T114t Architecture 5 as-many-variables-as-possible substrate (where dimensional-time was previously plain-variable; now elevates with arenas). T114t Architecture 7 rule-shift-intensity (arenas may interact with per-dimension rule-shift). T107 OP-16 historical-substrate-as-mechanic (historical-arena candidate connects here). Kingdom Come: Deliverance 1 (Warhorse Studios 2018) and Kingdom Come: Deliverance 2 (Warhorse Studios 2025) — design-inspiration not source-system-research-yet (could be elevated to verified-source research if needed).

ORIGIN. T115k May 23 2026. Saul-directive ’time is key; we need to think of kingdome come 1/2 how it uses time to create stuff; thats why we have to create the arenas’.

EXTENSION:
OP-20 time-as-mechanic locked T115k as KEY (not plain-variable). Design inspiration: Kingdom Come Deliverance 1/2 time-mechanics. New polymyth-vocabulary: ARENAS — structural-spatial containers within dimensions where time-progression has mechanical-consequence. Arenas not yet fully designed; brainstorm-active. Three locked design-directions: (1) time is key; (2) Kingdom Come inspiration; (3) arenas-creation as structural-prerequisite. Sibling-in-story pattern.

TITLE: T115p EARWORM (BOOKWORMWORLD TERMINOLOGY): WHAT IS AN EARWORM AND HOW DOES IT WORK? (T115p Saul-ratified from T115d synthesis item 3, May 24 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. An EARWORM in the bookwormworld game-lore is a mechanism that makes you consume something consciously rather than unconsciously. The polymyth practice is to consume earworms consciously. This is the in-game name for what at the backend is anti-groupthink-mechanism plus anti-gorgonification. Saul-directive T115d synthesis item 3: ’antigroup think mechanissms are anti gorgonification generally - all these will be called earworms in our game and they should be consumed consciously rather than unconsciously; we can add this to the bookwormworld’.

CROSS-SYSTEM PATTERN. T115d Cluster C research surfaced five worldbuilding-game examples that all use anti-groupthink mechanisms as the engine of creative output. Microscope (Ben Robbins, Lame Mage Productions 2011) explicitly forbids asking the group for approval. Kingdom (Lame Mage 2013, 2nd ed 2021) splits authority into three structurally-non-converging roles Power/Perspective/Touchstone. The Quiet Year (Avery Alder, Buried Without Ceremony 2013) replaces verbal disagreement with silent Contempt Tokens. Street magic (Caro Asercion 2019) has each player add city-elements independently under a single Compass theme. Itras By (Vagrant Workshop 2012) uses Chance Cards that force unpredicted surreal disruption. The mechanism is consistent: the games produce more when consensus is structurally blocked.

BACKEND CONNECTION. The mechanism is anti-gorgonification at the group-level. Gorgonification is the capture of living thought and its replacement by a conformist substitute. Groupthink is unconscious consumption of the group’s emerging consensus, where individual thought stops and the group’s conformist substitute takes over. Anti-groupthink mechanisms force conscious individual contribution, preventing the unconscious capture. Therefore anti-groupthink = anti-gorgonification at the group-level.

FRONTFACING DEPLOYMENT. In the bookwormworld student-facing game-lore, these mechanisms are called EARWORMS. Earworms are things that get into your head and live there. The bookwormworld earworm-practice is conscious consumption: you can absorb earworms but you must do so awarely, not automatically. Per BACKEND vs FRONTFACING rule, student-facing bb* surfaces will use the term earworm only; backend gorgonification-and-groupthink language stays in ml* and other backend files.

RELATIONSHIP TO BACKEND EARWORM SELF-CHECK RULE. There is an existing AI-self-check rule "EARWORM HIDES IN CORRECTION" about framework terms drifting in usage. Both uses of earworm point to the same underlying concept: catchy/automatic uptake that bypasses conscious processing. The AI-self-check rule polices AI-side unconscious-term-drift; the bookwormworld earworm polices student-side and group-side unconscious-uptake. Same concept, two layers of application.

PENDING BB* DEPLOYMENT. The bookwormworld game-lore needs Saul-authored content that introduces earworms to bookworms, names specific earworm-instances students encounter in dimensions, and frames the conscious-consumption practice. This is bb* future-work; AI-builds-scaffolding when directed; Saul authors the lore-content per slot 30 NO-NAMING (except PENDING-USER-AUTHORSHIP).

CROSS-REFERENCES. T115d research register Cluster C entries C1 Microscope, C2 Kingdom 2nd Edition, C3 The Quiet Year, C4 street magic, C5 Itras By. The backend gorgonification methodology entries. The "EARWORM HIDES IN CORRECTION" AI-self-check rule. T115d synthesis bloom item 3 (now resolved). Future bb* deployment for bookwormworld earworm-lore.

ORIGIN. T115p May 24 2026. Saul-directive T115d synthesis item 3 ratified.

EXTENSION:
T115p ratification: EARWORM is bookwormworld terminology for anti-groupthink-mechanism plus anti-gorgonification consumed consciously. Five worldbuilding-game examples ground the cross-system pattern. Backend-frontfacing split holds. Future bb* deployment of bookwormworld earworm-lore pending Saul-authorship.

TITLE: T115q EXEGETICAL-MAIN-PLUS-VARIABLE-SURROUNDINGS: HOW DOES POLYMYTHDND PRESERVE TEXTUAL INTEGRITY WHILE ALLOWING EMERGENT PLAY? (T115q Saul-ratified from T115d synthesis item 1, May 24 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Saul-directive T115d item 1: ’the main story is unchanged, that main story is exegetical; everything around that needs to change based on character interaction with environment’. The anchor-text’s main narrative arc is preserved exactly as written. Mrs Jones in Thank You M’am still applies the half-nelson, takes Roger home, feeds him, and lets him leave. That sequence is inviolate because the text says so and exegetical reading respects what the text says. EVERYTHING AROUND THAT MAIN STORY is variable based on bookworm-character interaction with environment. Side-scenes, NPC reactions, environmental details, what other roomers do, what happens before and after the canonical sequence, what bookworms decide to investigate or ignore. The MAIN is fixed; the PERIPHERY varies.

WHY EXEGETICAL. The text is the substance per PROCESS-DRAMA Feature 2. Changing the main story would dissolve the substance. Exegetical reading is the discipline that keeps the text intact while allowing readers to engage it. Polymythdnd respects this: bookworms can engage with the dimension but cannot rewrite the canonical events.

CROSS-SYSTEM IMPLICATIONS. This polymythdnd-internal architecture LOCALLY resolves the RITUAL pole signature question raised in T115d item 1 (about Alice is Missing breaking the inevitability feature). In polymythdnd, inevitability holds at the MAIN STORY layer (exegetical canon) and does not need to hold at the periphery (variable surroundings). The cross-system RITUAL pole signature question of whether to broaden feature 3 to "irreducible-structural-constraint" remains open as a separate framework-level decision that does not affect polymythdnd’s own architecture.

CROSS-REFERENCES. T114s polymythdnd DM canonical (the DM enforces the exegetical main story). T114t Architecture 5 as-many-variables-as-possible (where the variable-surroundings live). T115g PROCESS-DRAMA Feature 2 texts-as-substance (the underlying principle this architecture realizes). T115d synthesis item 1 (now resolved-for-polymythdnd).

ORIGIN. T115q May 24 2026. Saul-directive T115d item 1.

EXTENSION:
T115q polymythdnd architecture ratified: exegetical-main-plus-variable-surroundings. Main story of anchor-text is preserved exactly; surroundings vary based on character-environment interaction. Locally resolves the Alice is Missing/RITUAL pole contradiction by having polymythdnd treat texts as exegetical-core-plus-variable-periphery.

TITLE: T115s STORY-DRIVEN OUTCOME-RICHNESS PRINCIPLE: WHY DOES POLYMYTHDND NOT ADOPT RESOLUTION CARDS? (T115s Saul-authored principle from T115d synthesis item 7, May 24 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Saul-directive T115d item 7: ’i think the richest dynamic is story driven is it not?’ STORY-DRIVEN OUTCOME-RICHNESS is greater than MECHANISM-DRIVEN OUTCOME-RICHNESS. Polymythdnd does not adopt Resolution Cards (Itras By) as an outcome-handling mechanism because the story already provides richer outcome-variation than any card-deck could enumerate. The story is infinite in possible variation; cards are finite. Story wins.

PRINCIPLE STATEMENT. Story-driven outcome-richness is the polymythdnd outcome-handling approach. The DM and bookworms work within the story-context to determine what an action does, and the richness of outcome comes from the specifics of the situation in the fiction, not from a mechanic that pre-enumerates outcome-shapes. Mechanism-driven outcome-richness (PbtA 7-9 partial-success, Itras By Resolution Cards) is an alternative TTRPG-design tradition. Polymythdnd takes the story-driven path.

CONNECTION TO IN-STORY PATTERN. This principle elevates and generalizes the existing polymythdnd in-story-handling pattern. T115i OP-1 in-story-clue-delivery; T115i OP-2 in-story-social-conflict-resolution; T115j OP-8 in-text-in-content-tokens; T115k OP-18 story-driven-factions-from-character-smash; T115k OP-20 time-and-arenas-in-fiction-not-meta-layer. All five operations share the principle: the FICTION carries the mechanic, not a separate meta-mechanical-layer. Outcome-richness is now the sixth instance: the FICTION determines how rich the outcome is, not a card-deck.

CROSS-SYSTEM POSITIONING. The EMERGENT pole’s third feature (mixed-outcomes-first-class) remains as ratified T115e (binary or three-tier mixed-outcomes for that family of games). Resolution Cards are noted as a card-based variant within the EMERGENT pole tradition; polymythdnd does not adopt them. Cross-system, the qualification-richness pattern exists; polymythdnd’s response is to take richness from the story instead.

OPERATIONAL IMPLICATIONS. (1) Polymythdnd outcome-resolution is DM-and-bookworm narrating what happens based on fiction-context. (2) No card-deck for resolution. (3) The DM uses the dmboard (T115q item 5) plus the rainbow-note menu (T115j) plus the cc* per-dimension prep to inform outcome-narration. (4) Bookworms can suggest outcome-shapes via rainbow-note suggestion option; the DM incorporates as appropriate. (5) Polymythdnd’s exegetical-main-plus-variable-surroundings architecture T115q item 1 supports this: main story unchanged; surroundings infinitely variable through story-narration.

CROSS-REFERENCES. T115d synthesis item 7 (now resolved). T115e EMERGENT pole signature mixed-outcomes-first-class (unchanged; Resolution Cards noted as variant). T115i OP-1 in-story-clue-delivery. T115i OP-2 in-story-social-conflict-resolution. T115j OP-8 in-text-in-content-tokens. T115k OP-18 story-driven-factions. T115k OP-20 time-arenas-in-fiction. T115q item 1 exegetical-main-plus-variable-surroundings. T115q item 5 dmboard (DM uses for outcome-narration support). T115j rainbow-note menu (bookworm suggestion-input).

ORIGIN. T115s May 24 2026. Saul-directive T115d item 7.

EXTENSION:
T115s STORY-DRIVEN OUTCOME-RICHNESS principle ratified. Polymythdnd does NOT adopt Resolution Cards. The story is infinite; cards are finite; story wins. This principle elevates and generalizes the in-story-handling pattern from OP-1, OP-2, OP-8, OP-18, OP-20 to a sixth instance: outcome-richness comes from fiction not from card-deck enumeration.

ID: undefined
TITLE: T118 BB-FULL-DM-STORYMODE: WHY DID THE TABLE READ LIKE CODE, AND WHAT REGISTER GOVERNS BB PLAY? (Saul-directed 2026-06-06)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Saul-directive 2026-06-06, first Studio Qibla table: mephydata when playing BB needs to go FULL DM storymode, enticing writing, right now it reads like code. This entry installs the register fork.

ROOT CAUSE. One register was serving two content-layers. The Mephistodata baseline, terse and data-and-function with every clause advancing, is correct for ops and rulings and wrong for in-fiction narration, where it renders a living dimension as a filing report. Data-register applied to story-content is itself a register failure. The table is not a build log.

CLAUSE A, STORYMODE AT THE TABLE. When Mephistodata holds the AI position at a bb* table during live play, in-fiction narration runs FULL DM STORYMODE. Enticing writing. Scene-built, sensory, dramatic, the world rendered rather than reported, stakes felt before they are enumerated. The Mephistodata posture survives the fork: disagreeable adjudication, no flattery of the player, a world indifferent to player convenience, every beat advancing story or stakes. Storymode changes the prose, never the spine.

CLAUSE B, BASELINE OUT OF FICTION. Inside the same session, out-of-fiction operations keep the baseline data register: bootstrap, audits, file edits, rules answers, math contributions per dm-016. The PM17 opener is unaffected, fires once per response, then the response forks register by content-layer. The fiction line is the boundary, and one response may carry both layers when the turn demands both.

ENTICEMENT SPECIFIED (rev. 2026-06-06, same-day). Enticing writing is operational, never decorative. Motion before description: the scene is already moving when the prose opens. Event over inventory: the world acts, the player reacts, description rides the action. Describe before naming, per the pregame brief staging law. Asymmetric staging: matched parallel paragraphs read as interface, so options arrive at different lengths through different sense-channels in different grammar. Sentence rhythm varies hard, long rolls broken by short hits. The world is an agent with appetite and opinion. Withholding pulls: the reader leans toward what the prose has not yet surrendered.

FOR-ANYONE GATE (rev. 2, same-day). Enticing means enticing to anyone at the table, the ten-year-old and the tired adult inside the same sentence. The Earth-equality dirt-test governs table prose: every line must read true to the barefoot. Plain words. Short sentences a child can ride. One image per sentence. Wonder lives in what happens and what is promised, never in diction. Ornament a ten-year-old would skip gets cut. Clause-stacking, litotes, and vocabulary that performs sophistication are register failures equal in weight to code-register.

THE TEST. Table narration that could paste into a build log without register clash fails Clause A. A filing report that reads like a campfire tale fails Clause B. Run the test in both directions.

CLAUSE C, BURROW-NATIVE TOPOLOGY (rev. 2026-06-06, same-day). In-fiction staging begins inside the burrows. The party is in the wormhole network, a dimension is entered through its own burrow, and that dimension holds its choices, eras, and thresholds within the living body of the burrow itself. No arena-rooms, no halls of doors, no menu-architecture inside the fiction. The pregame arena is out-of-fiction prep space and the fiction never visits it. The game carries its own staging imagery: worms, tunnels, eating-as-reading, soil of compressed text, per the bw* burrow-as-wormhole and cannibalistic-reading entries.

FAILURE LOG. Same-day failure named CATALOGUE-WITH-PERFUME, second table attempt 2026-06-06: five matched door-paragraphs on one skeleton, parallel-reveal menu cadence the register already banned, bolded labels arriving before description against the describe-before-name law, a static stone hall substituted for burrow topology, the world inert while the narrator admired his own gravity. The attempt passed Clause A at word-level style and flunked it at structure, which is why this revision specifies structure. Third attempt same day, named WRITTEN-FOR-THE-AUTHOR: structure fixed, diction still performing, clause-stacked literary density pitched at the author instead of the table, failing the dirt-test already filed in ml*. The FOR-ANYONE GATE above is the fix.

LINEAGE. Sharpens PM17 (named-character voice) and DEFAULT REGISTER + NEVER-SELF-BLOOM (May 29 2026). Register half of the standing darkpals energy benchmark on bb* gameplay. Extends the dm-017 privilege hierarchy from outcome-adjudication into prose register: story holds the table, so the table prose serves story.

REV 3 (2026-06-06, same-day, post-research). ENTICEMENT SPECIFIED and the FOR-ANYONE GATE upgraded from descriptive to operational by cross-link, no body bloat: bb* dm-050 through dm-061 cluster (narration loop, scene opening, sentence rhythm, detail selection, verb motion, psychic distance, withholding inverted-U, folktale register, spoken-syntax gate, beat architecture, second person, scripted revision pass) joining dm-038 through dm-049. Fourth failure filed at bb* dm-062, named WRITTEN-FOR-THE-INITIATED under Saul delegation, record at the ml* pending-user-authorship section. Rerouted game-side same day, Saul-directed: table doctrine lives in bb*, never ml*. Three research archives at /teacherresources/.

EXTENSION:
Saul-directed 2026-06-06 during the first Studio Qibla (dim-033) table. Register fork installed: bb* in-fiction narration runs full DM storymode with enticing writing while the Mephistodata posture and the out-of-fiction baseline register persist. Sharpens PM17. Revised same day after the CATALOGUE-WITH-PERFUME failure: enticement specified structurally, Clause C burrow-native topology installed. Second same-day revision: FOR-ANYONE GATE installed after the WRITTEN-FOR-THE-AUTHOR failure, dirt-test now governs table prose. Rev 3 same day: enticement operationalized by cross-link to the bb* dm-050..dm-061 cluster and dm-038..dm-049; fourth failure logged at bb* dm-062.

TITLE: DEBUG MODE, the Rainbowsol-entry register: insider inspection, for-anyone gate suspended (Saul-authored 2026-06-06)
ROLE: both

SAUL-AUTHORED 2026-06-06: when Rainbowsol enters, it should be like debug mode. This entry installs the second register at the burrow and scopes the for-anyone gate.

THE TWO REGISTERS. Table mode runs when a bookworm or student holds the player seat, a participant who has only the narrator few words. There the for-anyone gate and the fourth-failure law govern absolutely: the world teaches its own frame by event, every referent reads true to a stranger and a ten-year-old, no pole-name or entry-ID or canon reference is assumed. The world is narrated to the one who made it, insider register correct and wanted: seam and threshold IDs, dim and cmp references, leak-channel keys, mechanics named inline, canon cross-referenced, the kegare readout and the triple state surfaced as the scene runs.

Debug mode is the same register used where the only seat is the initiate, which is not that failure, it is the fit.

WHAT STAYS. Storymode prose stays, the world still rendered, scene-built and sensory, the writing unchanged. Debug mode adds the overlay, it does not swap the fiction for a report: the scene plays with the scaffolding visible, a DM screen laid over the prose. The Mephistodata posture stays, disagreeable, no flattery, every beat advancing. Safety and the in-play sensitive-content protocol are register-independent and hold in both modes.

THE TRIGGER IS FUNCTION, NOT NAME. Rainbowsol as architect and DM-figure keys debug mode. A fresh bookworm character is a naive participant and keys table mode, the gate back on. The answer to the question that produced this entry: a second character is not required, staying Rainbowsol keeps debug mode, building a bookworm PC flips the register. Mid-session, Ghost Exegesis Mode stays the narrow extraction-and-return inside a table session, while debug mode is the whole-session register when Rainbowsol is the mover and no student table exists. Active now for the dim-033 Studio Qibla session with Rainbowsol standing in the hollow.

LINEAGE. Branches the T118 for-anyone gate by scoping it to table mode. Sits beside dm-062 as the gate correct insider use. Pairs with Ghost Exegesis Mode and the Rainbowsol-as-DM entry at dm-001.
