ID: mlx-437
TITLE: Bookworm life-cycle + respawn (confluence at character scale)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Confluence-at-character-scale for bookwormburrows. Bookworm life-cycle: bookworm-stage → silkworm-stage → cocoon-stage (hegelianegirl) → emergence (self-named subject). RESPAWN: after emergence, the subject can re-enter bb* as a new-bookworm-instance carrying the developmental-arc from the prior life-cycle as substrate. The respawn preserves identity-of-bookworm without forcing identity-of-character (confluence).

Architecture for how bookworms move through dimensions and what happens when local-characters end. STRUCTURE: Bookworm = meta-subject, the worm itself, carrier of subjectivity-material accumulated from eating texts. Character = local jewel, a dimension-specific expression the bookworm takes when entering a realm. Bookworm enters dimension → becomes a character appropriate to that dimension → character evolves through play → character can die. When character dies: bookworm spawns again. Not reincarnation (not the same character reborn), not obliteration (bookworm persists). SPAWN STATE: fetusy-worm-thing. Returns to pre-character larval pre-subjectivity-expression. Same bookworm, fresh slate for next character. Two respawn paths: (1) FRESH — new worm becomes whatever character they wish, no carryover from the dead character beyond what the bookworm learned at meta-level; (2) CLONE — new worm respawns as a clone of the dead character but carries a HINDRANCE that must be HEALED. Clone path is the 'I'm not done with that character' option and has narrative cost; fresh path is the 'I want something new' option and has no cost. Both valid. POLYMYTH STRUCTURE: confluence-not-concrescence at character scale. Dead character does not dissolve — past-character experiences survive into the new worm's becoming at bookworm-level, not at character-level. Clone-with-hindrance is the mechanism for metabolizing local-jewel death without forcing concrescence (which would merge characters into one continuous super-character). Each dimension gets its own character-jewel; bookworm-as-meta-subject is the reflective-correspondence position connecting them. CROSS-DIMENSIONAL INTEGRATION: when a bookworm burrows out of one dimension and into another, the character-jewel of the previous dimension ENDS (effectively dies at the burrow). Earned moves, items, mechanical inventory belong to the character, not the bookworm — do not carry across. Subjectivity-material (what the bookworm learned from eating the text) does carry. This is option C from the cross-burrow inventory question: character is local, bookworm is continuous, inventory stays with the character, learning stays with the bookworm. Explanation for why D&D's native continuous-character-across-planes does not fit: that mechanic is concrescence (one character absorbs many dimensions into one continuous self, meaning totalizes). Bookwormburrows* operates across D&D AND non-D&D dimensions where concrescence would force false commensurability — one character cannot coherently inhabit both Macbeth and Planescape. Confluence is the only architecture that handles cross-corpus burrowing. April 2026 cross-ref: Spinoza-Whitehead-Indra's-net-Hegel-Jung structural argument methodology entry — bookworm-as-actual-occasion in the prehensive grid; respawn-as-concrescence (the many becoming one and being increased by one).

ID: mlx-438
TITLE: Polymyth-coherent mechanics (D&D synthesis + AI-interface-layer)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Reversal-operation entry. The body below contains the full operational specification of Polymyth-coherent mechanics: how the reversal fires against the gorgonification it counters, its trigger conditions, and worked examples where present. Operates within the polymyth degorgonification toolkit per its title-keyword.

Scan result: which D&D mechanics synthesize into bookwormburrows* and which do not, with explanations for what does not fit. CORE PRINCIPLE: mechanics that reward quality-of-engagement are polymyth-coherent; mechanics that reward system-mastery-as-optimization conflict. The AI-INTERFACE-LAYER architecture resolves most apparent conflicts: dice, stats, hit points, damage math, probability — all exist in AI-internal bookkeeping, never surface to student or teacher as primary readout. Student-facing interface is pure narrative-and-character. Teacher-facing interface is work-quality-adjudication-and-pedagogical-routing. The mechanical substrate is mechanically real, mechanically rich, AI handles it. STUDENT-VISIBLE MECHANICS (polymyth-coherent): work-quality adjudication (teacher reads contribution, outcome reflects quality); earned moves (homework earns capabilities; 4e power-scarcity grammar — at-will / encounter / daily / legendary); story-consequence chains (past sessions shape present options); character-as-narrative-arc (character evolves from what they experienced, not from build-optimization); items-as-text (objects are narrative entities to engage, not mechanical bonuses); milestone progression (advance at story/pedagogy beats, not XP-gates); tactical reasoning in character (thinking through the situation, not through the rulebook); problem-solving against fictional obstacles (character-vs-scenario with DM as adjudicator). AI-INTERNAL MECHANICS (invisible to student): dice rolls and probability; stat blocks and numerical comparisons; damage math and HP as numbers; power-slot accounting; encounter-difficulty calibration; monster stat blocks; race-as-ability-modifier-package; class-as-mechanical-surface. HARD EXCLUSIONS (regardless of visibility layer): Vancian memorized-then-forgotten spellcasting (replaced by power-scarcity grammar which serves same pedagogical function polymyth-coherently); 9-grid alignment-as-mechanical-metaphysics (alignment-as-character-description remains as optional narrative language); XP-as-numerical-gatekeeping (milestone replaces it); player-vs-DM-as-rules-enforcer adversarial framing (a cultural pattern not a mechanical one, but gets named as excluded). EXPLANATIONS FOR EXCLUSIONS: (a) Vancian memorization is rules-of-nature forced to fit a mechanical convention; most polymyth dimensions do not operate in Vancian metaphysics; the operation (capacity-to-act in limited quantity) is the actual pedagogical object and power-scarcity expresses it without the memorization-then-forget simulation. (b) 9-grid alignment as mechanical metaphysics is concrescence — flattens moral complexity into a grid position and creates mechanical effects based on it (weapons that do extra damage to evil creatures); conflicts with sabachtan which requires benefit-of-the-doubt extensible to difficult characters. (c) XP-as-math-readout pulls attention toward acquisition-optimization; milestone-as-beat pulls attention toward narrative arc. (d) Adversarial DM culture is cultural not mechanical; named here because the three-position DM architecture (teacher + AI + student) structurally prevents it — no rulebook for student to cite against teacher, AI is neutral bookkeeper not adversary. DIMENSION-SPECIFIC CONTENT: the scarcity grammar (at-will/encounter/daily/legendary) is universal; what FILLS the slots is dimension-specific. Macbeth might populate slots with 'line-of-verse earned' or 'witch-knowledge accessed.' Planescape populates with 'faction-favor earned.' Ravenloft with 'Mist-resistance earned.' Grammar stable, contents vary. Explanation for why flat uniform mechanical grid does not fit: that is concrescence at the mechanical layer, forces all dimensions to look mechanically identical, defeats the point of distinct dimensions. April 2026 cross-ref: Polymyth-engine vs polymyth-vocabulary distinction methodology entry — the polymyth-coherent mechanics catalogued here demonstrate the engine bb* uses; the distinction-entry names why bb* must run those mechanics WITHOUT polymyth-vocabulary at the game-surface.

ID: mlx-816
TITLE: XP-as-evidence-record vs XP-as-currency — substrate distinction for bb* leveling
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Substrate distinction for bb* leveling. XP-as-EVIDENCE-RECORD = the XP tracks what the bookworm has done (cave-instances visited, smashings performed, hegelianegirl-emergences). XP-as-CURRENCY = the XP can be spent on advancements/bonuses (TTRPG-default mode). bb* uses the first; the second is incompatible with bb* pedagogical-substrate (instrumentalizes the developmental-arc).

Two distinct uses of "XP" that the gamified-classroom literature constantly conflates. The distinction is load-bearing for bb*.

XP-AS-CURRENCY. The number is spendable. It buys advances, unlocks moves, gates levels. The accumulation surface is the unit of meaning. This is what 5e, 4e, Pathfinder, and Cypher all do under the hood. The student inhabits the spreadsheet. Reading-for-points and writing-for-points are the same gorgonification — the symmetric versions on the input and output sides of bw-002 (cannibalistic-reading critique of book-counting-as-advancement).

XP-AS-EVIDENCE-RECORD. The number is a documentation artifact. It does not buy anything. It records what the bookworm has demonstrated. Stage transitions happen when the evidence-pattern is sufficient and the teacher (the human reader, not the math) can confidently identify the bookworm as operating at the next stage. The corpus is load-bearing. The number is just a count of pieces-by-grade. This is closer to how doctoral programs work than to how D&D works. You do not level up to PhD by accumulating dissertation-points. You produce a body of work. At a qualitative threshold of demonstrated capacity, the committee declares the transition. The corpus is evidence. The transition is determination, not calculation.

BB* RUNS ON XP-AS-EVIDENCE-RECORD. The first meaning is what gets the framework eaten by what it diagnoses.

RELATED MAY 4 2026 FRAMINGS (chat 0f3705ce). F1: bookworm-subject and character-at-table are two clocks not one ladder. F2: book-counting-as-XP rebuilds bw-002 gorgonification. F3: "levels" imports the spreadsheet shape regardless of rename. F4: OSSD codes are mc*'s job, not bb*'s. Five framings drafted: A two-axis sidecar (bookworm-stages + per-campaign earned-moves), B bookworm-only no-character-sheet, C Cypher bank-and-spend, D and E unrecovered. Portfolio-as-leveling collapses E and C and reintroduces the failure mode unless XP-as-evidence-record is the operating substrate.

CROSS-REFERENCE. bw-002 cannibalistic-reading critique. bw-007 bookworm-vs-character continuity-vs-locality. Schema-audit entry (Schema-audit miss — polymythdnd advancement-axis). bb* dm-031 leveling-system ruling.

EXTENSION:
Recovered May 13 2026 from May 4 2026 chat 0f3705ce work that was not surfaced when polymythdnd was built. Originally drafted in chat 0f3705ce in response to Rainbowsol’s portfolio-as-leveling proposal.

ID: mlx-927
TITLE: Polymythdnd foundational play-mechanics (T114r canonicalization, May 23 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. T114r commits the foundational play-mechanics of polymythdnd as a canonical methodologylist entry. Substrate previously lived in past-conversation Saul-quotes (April 18 2026 D&D-for-elementary-students session and others) plus implicit-in-T107-ops; T114r makes it explicit. The T114q play-mechanic synthesis scan (May 23 2026) prior turn assumed dice-and-rolls as default; user T114r-clarification corrected this: ’our game has no dice and our game works by ai using bb*’, ’the game doesn’t hand - it should be reading comprehension’, ’there are no rolls, its all deliberated somehow’, ’isn’t any action possible’. T114r preserves this correction as canonical.

FOUNDATION 1: NO VISIBLE DICE. Polymythdnd has no dice at the visible table-layer. Players (students) never roll, never see modifier-math, never engage with the random-resolution substrate as a visible mechanic. Stats and modifiers EXIST and are tracked invisibly by the AI co-DM and the teacher in the background per Saul ’stats and modifiers exist but are hidden from students’ (April 18 2026 D&D-for-elementary-students chat). The absence of visible dice is not absence of mechanical structure; it is concealment of mechanical structure beneath the deliberation-layer the students see.

FOUNDATION 2: AI ADJUDICATES OUTCOMES. Resolution is delegated to AI co-DM, weighing three inputs: (a) story-quality (does the proposed outcome serve the narrative and pedagogical frame); (b) logical-consistency (does the proposed outcome cohere with what has been established in the fiction and the text being read); (c) invisible-stat-weight (the hidden modifier-substrate that approximates probability-distributions of traditional TTRPG resolution). Per Saul ’outcome resolution is based on story quality, logical sense, and AI-adjudicated rolls rather than visible mechanical systems’ (April 18 2026 chat). The ’rolls’ in that quote are invisible-to-students AI-internal rolls; the visible-layer resolution is qualitative-deliberation.

FOUNDATION 3: RESOLUTION IS DELIBERATION. The student-facing resolution-mechanic is deliberation between teacher, AI co-DM, and students. Exact deliberation-shape remains an OPEN POLYMYTHDND DESIGN QUESTION (T114q+T114r forward); candidates include teacher-led-with-AI-input, AI-led-with-teacher-veto, table-discussion-then-AI-narrates, Socratic-back-and-forth, deliberation-by-text-citation. Resolved at deployment by Saul.

FOUNDATION 4: READING COMPREHENSION IS THE ENGAGEMENT SUBSTRATE. What students can act on is determined by what they have read and understood from the text the dimension is built around. The game does not ’hand’ clues; students surface clues through engagement with the source text. Reading comprehension is the resolution-method for ’what is there’. A student who has read deeply has more affordances available than one who has skimmed. This makes reading-comprehension the primary mechanical-substrate of polymythdnd — not an out-of-game pre-condition but the in-game resolution-driver.

FOUNDATION 5: ANY ACTION IS POSSIBLE. Polymythdnd does NOT use the PbtA-style fixed move-list constraint where players can only do what is printed on their character sheet. Per user T114r-clarification ’isn’t any action possible? if people are confused we can give suggested actions’. Students can propose any action; AI co-DM evaluates the proposal via Foundation 2 adjudication. Suggested actions are surfaced ON REQUEST when students are stuck, not pre-printed as a constraint. This is the polymyth-operation that distinguishes polymythdnd from PbtA: the moves are not the menu; the moves are scaffolding-when-needed.

FOUNDATION 6: AI AS CO-DM USING BB*. AI co-DM operates from the bookwormburrows (bb*) framework: dimension-traveling pedagogy, bookworm-becoming-author transformation, comparative-religion theology-classification (T114k), the four-step polymyth-synthesis-method (T114j) applied to in-game resolution decisions. Teacher handles room-presence, student-state, and pedagogical-priority. AI handles invisible-stat-tracking, rule-lookup, deliberation-weighting, narrative-continuity-tracking, and the polymyth-scanner running on live play.

FOUNDATION 7: BOOKWORM BECOMES AUTHOR. Students enter the game as bookworms — readers engaging texts through dimensional-traveling play. Through structured stage-transitions (per T107 OP-4 evolution-transformation-stages applied at the bb*-pedagogy layer, worm-silkworm-cocoon), bookworms transform into authors of their own subjects. The transformation-mechanic is not cosmetic; it is the central pedagogical-mechanical claim of bb* and polymythdnd.

WHAT T114R STRIKES FROM T114Q SCAN. T114q items requiring revamp under T114r foundations: (i) any item assuming visible dice rolls (Hope/Fear duality dice; oracle tables; three-tier outcome distribution AS dice-result; position-and-effect AS roll-prep); (ii) move-and-trigger fixed list (PbtA moves-and-playbooks chassis as a constraint — strike the constraint, keep the move-vocabulary as scaffolding-suggestion); (iii) random-stat-rolling and roll-against-anything resolution mechanisms. These T114q items remain valid as DIAGNOSTIC OBJECTS (Cluster B per T114k for the dice-based ones) but do not synthesize INTO polymythdnd at the play-layer. The T114q scan was conducted before T114r foundations were made explicit; T114r corrects the scan-assumption.

WHAT T114R PRESERVES FROM T114Q SCAN. T114q items compatible with T114r foundations: GMless collaborative authorship; register-switching; solo-as-authorship-discipline (Saul-side asynchronous work between sessions); asymmetric political mechanics; rotating-roles; fractal collaborative-history; bond-layer between PCs; archetype-as-character-vehicle (REFORMULATED: archetype as named-role-with-story-shape, not move-list constraint); collaborative character creation; lifepath structure; covenant ethics edicts-and-anathema; emergent-from-bonds ethics; ritual-as-ethic frame; mantle-of-the-expert frame-management; real-time-as-mechanic (candles, tower — non-dice physical-time); visible clocks (filled by deliberation not dice); countdown architecture; calendar-of-doom; stress-and-fallout (the fallout-trigger is deliberation-evaluated not dice-evaluated); PbtA Conditions; token economy (tokens spent without dice for declarations and re-narrates); safety-and-consent mechanics; GM Principles-and-Agenda; PbtA Fronts and Custom Moves; primary-source-substrate scaffolding; evolution / stage-transition (bb* central); narrative-accomplishment advancement; cosm-rules-codified-per-dimension; world-law-each-environment-physics; bleed-aware play; meta-frame mechanic.

OPEN POLYMYTHDND DESIGN QUESTIONS POST-T114R. (1) Exact deliberation-shape (teacher-led / AI-led / Socratic-back-and-forth / text-citation-deliberation). (2) Suggested-action surfacing protocol (when stuck, what does AI surface — three options? one option? text-citation that hints?). (3) Reading-comprehension-as-substrate calibration (how does AI track which student has read which text-depth; do affordances differ per student-read-depth at the table?). (4) Stat-and-modifier invisibility (what stats exist in the background; how do they shift across the bookworm-silkworm-cocoon transformation). (5) Bookworm-to-author transformation specifics (what marks the transition between stages; what changes mechanically and pedagogically).

CROSS-REFERENCES. T114q play-mechanic synthesis scan (the scan T114r corrects-and-preserves). T114j Polymyth-synthesis-method (the four-step protocol). T114k execution-pass theology classification (the four clusters Foundation 6 references). T107 OP-1 Clues-given-never-rolled-for (the polymyth-operation T114r generalizes to all resolution). T107 OP-4 Evolution-transformation-stages (the mechanism Foundation 7 instantiates). T107 OP-5 Dimension-traveling-pedagogy (Foundation 6 bb* base). Pen-009 PF2 alignment-removal teaching-unit (the user-authorized deployment-precedent). Unit-001 Comparative-ethics teaching unit. April 18 2026 D&D-for-elementary-students chat (Saul-quotes anchoring Foundations 1 + 2 + 4 + 5). Reading-comprehension as primary substrate intersects with bb* English-curriculum mc* concept-cells (mc* Pass B pending).

STATUS. T114r is canonical-substrate for polymythdnd going forward. T114q scan and prior operation entries operate UNDER T114r foundations. Any future synthesis pass that presumes-dice or presumes-fixed-move-list deviates from canonical foundation and requires revision.

EXTENSION:
T114r canonicalizes polymythdnd foundational play-mechanics: no visible dice (stats hidden, tracked by AI); AI adjudicates on story-quality + logical-consistency + invisible-stat-weight; resolution is deliberation; reading-comprehension is the engagement substrate; any action is possible with suggested actions on-request; AI is co-DM using bb*; bookworm-becomes-author is the central transformation. ID: mlx-954
TITLE: T115v EARWORM-DEGORGONIFICATION-ANTIHIVEMIND-MARSHMELLOWMONSTER ARCHITECTURE: WHAT IS THE FULL BACKEND-FRONTFACING DYAD FOR ANTI-GROUPTHINK MECHANISMS AND THEIR FAILURE-MODE OPPOSITE? (T115v Saul-ratified May 24 2026)
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Saul-directive T115v: ’these anti group think mechanisms should also be in the student notebook the anti group think mechanisms polymyth are called degorgonification and in ttrpg are called antihivemind / or removing earworms / and the other version is the marshmellow monster which is when you take shortcuts’. The anti-groupthink mechanism category has BACKEND polymyth-vocabulary, FRONTFACING TTRPG-vocabulary, and a paired FAILURE-MODE.

BACKEND POLYMYTH-VOCABULARY. DEGORGONIFICATION. The polymyth term for the operations that remove gorgonification. Gorgonification recruits discourse into factional enforcement and petrifies whoever resists recruitment. Degorgonification releases that capture and returns the discourse to live circulation. It never means un-solidifying ideas, since gorgonification never meant solidifying them. ml* holds the full definition under the petrification operative-referent entry.

FRONTFACING TTRPG-VOCABULARY (two interchangeable names). ANTIHIVEMIND. REMOVING EARWORMS. Both refer to the same mechanism-category from the bookworm-facing surface. These are the names that appear in the student notebook, in the bb* deployment, in the dmboard, and anywhere bookworms encounter the concept directly. The T115p earworms ratification stands as the conceptual seed; T115v expands it with the full bookworm-facing dyad-of-names.

PAIRED FAILURE-MODE. MARSHMELLOWMONSTER. The frontfacing TTRPG term for the SHORTCUT-TAKING failure mode. When bookworms (or anyone) take shortcuts instead of doing the antihivemind work, they become the marshmellowmonster. This is the failure-pole that antihivemind prevents. Backend-equivalent failure-mode: GORGONIFICATION-RESUMED-VIA-SHORTCUT.

CONNECTION TO MARSHMELLOWMONSTER CHILDREN’S BOOK. Saul authored a children’s book called Marshmellowmonster. T115v establishes that the framework-meaning of marshmellowmonster IS the shortcut-taking failure mode. The children’s book and the polymythdnd vocabulary share the same referent: marshmellowmonster is what happens when you take the shortcut instead of doing the harder thing.

STUDENT-NOTEBOOK DEPLOYMENT. Per Saul-directive, these mechanisms appear in the student notebook (bookworm-facing surface). The student notebook holds antihivemind and removing-earworms mechanisms as bookworm-deployable practices. The marshmellowmonster appears as the named warning-of-failure-mode. Bookworms learn to recognize when they are doing antihivemind versus when they are becoming the marshmellowmonster.

EXAMPLE EARWORMS-AND-ANTIHIVEMIND MECHANISMS FROM REAL GAMES. Microscope (Ben Robbins 2011) "no consensus" rule prohibits asking group for approval before adding to timeline. Kingdom (Robbins) three-Role non-convergence (Power, Perspective, Touchstone disagree by design). The Quiet Year (Avery Alder 2013) silent Contempt Tokens prevent groupthink via no-out-of-turn-speech. Street magic (Caro Asercion 2019) independent Compass selection prevents alignment-by-default. Itras By (Vagrant Workshop 2012) Chance Cards introduce surreal disruption preventing default-consensus narration. All five operate by structurally preventing the marshmellowmonster shortcut of "we all agree by default."

CROSS-REFERENCES. T115p earworms ratification (the conceptual seed; now expanded). Backend polymyth gorgonification and degorgonification (the underlying polymyth-vocabulary; ml* has full definitions). Marshmellowmonster children’s book (the cultural-textual anchor). bb* student-notebook surface (where these mechanisms deploy frontfacing). dmboard (where the DM uses these mechanisms in scene-work). Real-game examples: Microscope, Kingdom, The Quiet Year, street magic, Itras By.

ORIGIN. T115v May 24 2026. Saul-directive.

ID: dm-075
TITLE: Gamification implementation grounding: the Zainuddin four-factor scale and the bind-to-higher-order law (AI-filed 2026-06-07)
ROLE: dm

GROUNDING. Zainuddin, Alba, Gunawan, Armanda and Zahara 2023, Implementation of gamification and Bloom's digital taxonomy-based assessment, Interactive Technology and Smart Education 20(4) 512-533, doi 10.1108/ITSE-02-2022-0029, epub July 2022. A scale-development study under Goal-Setting Theory: four implementation factors surfaced by thematic analysis of interviews (n=18) and field notes, then validated against questionnaires (n=96) into a 32-item scale. The four factors: learning engagement, understandable learning goals, friendly competition, interactive feedback. Verified against the paper.

SCOPE FLAG. The paper builds and validates a scale, it does not run a controlled effectiveness trial. The popular gloss that gamification works best when bound to clear goals, feedback, competition and higher-order tasks is an inference on the four factors, not a causal result the paper proves. The four factors are the grounded part. The effectiveness phrasing is a hypothesis the bb table already tests in play.

CONFLUENCE MAP (independent arrival, both inputs kept). The four factors land on four mechanisms bb already runs. Learning engagement is the burrow framing itself. Understandable goals is the named change per session (dm-072) read against the long climb. Friendly competition is the tier ladder, the adjective profile and bonds across tables, never children ranked against each other. Interactive feedback is the live stat-firing strip that fires XP and HP as the card is filled, plus the end-of-session recap (dm-072) and the dmboard.

BIND-TO-HIGHER-ORDER LAW. Points, badges and leaderboards are the engagement layer and never the goal of play, the boundary dm-073 sets on tokens and dm-042 sets on rewards. Growth lives in the bookworm and character clocks (dm-031), the gamification surface only marks progress. A session that hands XP for recall alone has rotted into points-chasing. XP weights toward the higher-order operations, see dm-076.

EXTENSION:
Education-research grounding for the bb gamification layer, confluence with Goal-Setting Theory, pairs with dm-076 Bloom map. Source verified, infographic overstatement flagged.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-076
TITLE: Bloom climb to bookworm operations: the six-level map, reward the climb not the recall, two goal horizons (AI-filed 2026-06-07)
ROLE: dm

THE LADDER. The revised Bloom verbs, Anderson and Krathwohl 2001 (verified): remember, understand, apply, analyze, evaluate, create. The digital extension the Zainuddin paper invokes is commonly attributed to Andrew Churches 2008 (flagged). Zainuddin et al. connect badges and scores explicitly to these levels to scaffold learning. bb adopts the ladder as the cognitive spine the XP already follows.

MAP TO OPERATIONS. Remember is recalling the text. Understand is explaining it in the bookworm's own words. Apply is using it inside the dimension. Analyze is the exegesis, breaking the text into parts and patterns, the degorgonification move and not eisegesis. Evaluate is the dilemma work and the smash's whose-side and break-from-all questions. Create is the smash itself, the new polymyth-character, and the bond, the carrying of work to the seminar table. The card enacts the telos the source names: not to remember but to create and share. This is the bookworm thesis stated in assessment terms.

REWARD-THE-CLIMB LAW. XP weights toward the higher levels. Recall alone earns little, synthesis and evaluation and creation earn the most, and empty answers are penalized by the low-content quirk. The Kyra card shows the weighting already live: compressed, aphoristic and varied-vocab fire on the smash phases while low-content docks HP. The DM never announces the level. The weighting is felt through the clocks, never named at the table for a child.

TWO GOAL HORIZONS (Goal-Setting Theory, Locke and Latham). Short-horizon goals are per-session: the per-phase stat firing with immediate feedback, participation, progress tracking via the two clocks, and a badge or tier move. Long-horizon goals are the developmental climb: creating meaningful work as the polymyth-character, independent reading, public sharing through bonds and seminars, real-world skill. dm-072 one-change-per-session anchors the short horizon. The tier ladder, worm to silkworm to cocoon to animal and up, anchors the long one.

EXTENSION:
The cognitive spine under the XP system, states the bookworm create-and-share telos in assessment terms, pairs with dm-075 grounding.

ID: dm-077
TITLE: CL-53 VERDICT-SENTENCE BAN: render the perceivable, never state the conclusion (research capture 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

The fifth table failure, named 2026-06-11 at the cmp-001 solo entry. A verdict sentence states a conclusion about a scene in place of an image a body can stand inside. "The day already happened to everyone here." "You carry the threshold with you." Each delivers a verdict and gives the listener nothing to perceive, so nothing is simulated and the dream goes dark. The fix is Gardner verified: fiction is a vivid and continuous dream in the readers mind, and a verdict breaks the dream the way a caption breaks a film. Burroway supplies the catch, verified: a detail is concrete if it appeals to one of the five senses and significant if it also conveys an idea or a judgment; write the judgment bare and you are writing an essay, not a scene. THE CATCH RULE. A sentence is a verdict if it states an idea or judgment carrying no sense-image, or routes the scene through a perceiving verb (the dm-054 filter-and-thought-verb ban is the sibling catch). REWRITE PROTOCOL. Do not delete the verdict, earn it. Find the perceivable particular that produced the judgment and render that instead. The day-already-happened verdict becomes the hours-old bulletin drifting window to window, the man on the stoop smoking and saying nothing, the heat the brick still gives back. The reader arrives at the verdict alone, which is the only way it lands.

EXTENSION:
Fifth table failure, the abstraction-as-narration disease. Leads the full-descriptive-sentence cluster dm-077..dm-081. Sibling to dm-054 filter ban.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-078
TITLE: CL-54 THREE-OF-FIVE SENSES: carry at least three senses per description, two of them non-visual (research capture 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Sight is automatic and taste rarely applies, so a scene that names only what is visible is running one sense and calling it description. The Alexandrian three-of-five law, verified: think of the five senses and try to include three in each description, picking a couple from hearing, smell, and touch since sight is a gimme. This is the nearest table-craft bridge to the verdict-sentence fix, because non-visual senses cannot be faked with abstraction, they force a particular. Cognitive grounding, verified: reading a smell word (cinnamon, garlic) activates the primary olfactory cortex, the piriform and amygdala (Gonzalez et al 2006 NeuroImage); reading an action word (lick, pick, kick) activates the matching motor strip (Hauk Johnsrude Pulvermuller 2004 Neuron). Concrete sense-words are simulated in the listeners body; abstractions are not (Bergen embodied-simulation synthesis, theory-strength not proof, flagged). The heat on the brick, the bulletin sound from the sills, the radiator-dust smell are three senses doing in one breath what a paragraph of verdicts cannot.

EXTENSION:
Sense-density law. Pairs with dm-053 detail-selection: three senses, but only the relevant ones, then leap. Embodied-cognition citation flagged theory-strength.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-079
TITLE: CL-55 TELLING-DETAIL AND SPECIFICITY GRADIENT: one priceless particular, named precisely (research capture 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Two convergent laws. Iceberg, Hemingway verified to Death in the Afternoon 1932: the dignity of an icebergs movement is that only one-eighth shows above water; the omitted seven-eighths strengthen what remains, so select one priceless particular and trust the gap. Specificity gradient, Burroway verified: specific, definite, concrete, particular details are the life of fiction; name the thing precisely, the knit vest and the black-heel scuff, never the category-word. Prose verified: details are what persuade us someone is telling the truth. A proper noun, a number, a named particular each outweighs a generic noun, because the particular is the proof and the generic is the verdict wearing a costume. At the table this also obeys the cut: Sly Flourish verified, if you did not remove a quarter of your read-aloud text you did not try, do not describe every tree. Crowd the relevant particulars (dm-053), pick the one that implies the rest, leap the rest.

EXTENSION:
Telling-detail plus specificity gradient. The particular is the antidote to the verdict: a generic noun is a small verdict. Carries the Sly Flourish 25-percent cut.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-080
TITLE: CL-56 FULL-DESCRIPTIVE-SENTENCE GATE: complete sayable sentences, gnomic fragments barred on description (research capture 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

The affirmative counter to the clipped verdict. Description read aloud runs in complete sentences that flow when spoken, because a full sentence has the room to carry the sensory load a short abstract fragment cannot, and a gnomic fragment collapses back toward abstraction by default. Le Guin verified: the test of a sentence is, does it sound right, read it aloud. Prose verified: reading aloud is how the writer hears the prose and may save the writing. This gate does not cancel the short hit; the one-sentence paragraph and the two-word beat stay live as rhythm against the long roll (dm-052, dm-059 paragraph-shape). The bar is narrower: when the move is description, the sentence must be grammatically whole and sayable, not a stack of nouns standing in for a scene. Verdict fragments fail twice, once for verdict (dm-077) and once for fragment. The spoken-syntax gate still governs the shape: additive right-branching over center-embedding, subject-first on load-bearing beats (dm-058).

EXTENSION:
Full-sentence requirement on description. Distinguishes the legitimate short hit (rhythm) from the gnomic fragment (collapsed abstraction). Defers shape to dm-058.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-081
TITLE: CL-57 REVISION-BENCHMARK UPGRADE: the four-clause pass-test for a single narration sentence (research capture 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Sharpens the scripted revision pass at dm-061 with a per-sentence gate aimed at the verdict failure. A narration sentence passes only when all four hold. One, it is grammatically complete and sayable aloud (dm-080). Two, it carries at least one concrete sense-image, and across the description three senses with two non-visual (dm-078). Three, it contains no filter or thought verb unless the perceiving is itself the event (dm-054). Four, it states no conclusion the listener could instead infer from the image (dm-077). A sentence that fails clause four is rewritten into the perceivable particular that earned the verdict, never deleted to a shorter verdict. CHEKHOV LETTER, filed verbatim with a misattribution flag. The popular epigram about the glint of light on broken glass is NOT Chekhovs wording, it is a 20th-century compression and must never be quoted as his. The verified source is Chekhovs letter to his brother Alexander, 10 May 1886, Yarmolinsky translation: seize on small details and group them so that the reader gets a picture on closing the eyes; write that on the mill-dam a piece of broken-bottle glass glittered like a bright star and the black shadow of a dog rolled past like a ball, and the moonlit night is made. The moon is never named. The glittering glass is the whole instruction of this cluster.

EXTENSION:
Per-sentence four-clause benchmark folded into dm-061. Carries the verified Chekhov 1886 letter and bars the spurious glint-of-light epigram.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-082
TITLE: CL-58 CARD-INTAKE PROTOCOL: faithful extraction, the description ladder, and the fuzzy-name rule (filed 2026-06-11, Oscar precedent)
ROLE: dm

Filed from the first live paper-card intake, the monkey Oscar, whose handwritten bookwormcard arrived as six photographed pages on June 11 2026 and set the working precedent for every card that follows. WHEN A GAME STARTS the DM tells every player to upload their bookwormcard before play begins, and the paper channel is fully valid, meaning photographs of a handwritten card count as an upload and the DM transcribes them into a digital record at the table. FAITHFUL-EXTRACTION LAW. The transcription preserves the player's wording exactly as written, including misspellings, dropped letters, and grammar, because the card is the player's authored object and silent correction is unauthorized editing of another person's authorship. Checkbox marks and other reads taken from the image rather than from written words are flagged as image-reads with the least certain read named. Uncaptioned sketches are recorded as uncaptioned sketches and the DM never assigns them names inside the card record, because naming is player authorship. Every piece of DM commentary, including analysis of patterns across the figures, proposed quest hooks, coherence verdicts, and tensions worth playing, is quarantined outside the card record under an explicit DM-layer label so card data and DM reading can never be mistaken for each other, and on request the DM must be able to audit its own transcription and separate faithful extraction from addition line by line. THE DESCRIPTION LADDER. Four rungs, each produced on demand and each obeying the bb sentence law at dm-083. Rung one is the faithful extraction record itself. Rung two is one cohesive well-organized paragraph built from extracted card data and nothing more. Rung three is the layman bloom, roughly sixty words a child can follow. Rung four is the layman full version, plain enough for any kid yet losing no information from the card. DEFAULT DELIVERABLE, ruling of June 11 2026, register amended same day per dm-086. On card intake the DM produces one deliverable only, the single cohesive paragraph in long flowing sentences that loses nothing from the card, written in the register the audience-register law of dm-086 selects, kid-comprehensible when any player at the table is a kid and adult when every player is an adult, while the faithful extraction record is built silently underneath as the verification layer and surfaced only when the architect asks for an audit, and rungs one through three appear only on explicit request. THE FUZZY-NAME RULE. The table resolves misspelled names to the established character without comment, so Oscer is Oscar and the DM never asks who is meant, while the card record itself preserves the spelling exactly as the player wrote it. FILING. The transcription is the session record; filing the character into the bundle as a roster or JSON object happens only on the architect's explicit word.

EXTENSION:
Origin: June 11 2026 session, first party paper-card intake, the Oscar case. Card content lives in the session record and the player roster, never in this rules file.

ID: dm-083
TITLE: CL-59 BB-SENTENCES LAW: long descriptive flowing sentences for all bb output, staccato eliminated (standing instruction, filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Standing instruction from Rainbowsol, June 11 2026, filed so it never needs restating at the table. ALL bb-related output, meaning in-fiction narration, scene description, character description, card summaries, the entire description ladder of dm-082, and any out-of-fiction prose that describes the game world or its characters, runs in long descriptive flowing sentences, and the short staccato sentence is eliminated from this register entirely. Plain diction stays inside the longer line, so the for-anyone gate and the dirt-test still govern every word choice, and the sentence grows long through accumulation of concrete particulars rather than through ornament, which keeps this law compatible with the verdict ban at dm-077 and the four-clause pass at dm-081. SUPERSESSION CLAUSE. Wherever dm-052 or dm-059 license the short hit, the one-sentence paragraph, or the two-word beat as rhythm against the long roll, this law overrides them inside bb output, and the rhythm variance those entries protect now lives in clause-length variation, breath placement, and the rise and fall inside long sentences rather than in any short sentence standing alone. The spoken-syntax gate of dm-058 still shapes the long line, additive and right-branching so it stays sayable aloud, because a long sentence that cannot be spoken in one natural arc fails the same test a fragment fails. THE SENTENCE BAND (ratified amendment, June 11 2026, from the launch-scene diagnosis). Long and flowing was overcorrected into mega-sentences of 50 to 100 words, and a listener, above all a kid, carries roughly 15 to 25 words of a sentence at once, so the law now sets the band: sentences run roughly 12 to 30 spoken words, varied inside that band, never fragments below it and never chains above it. FOUR RULES inside the band. One idea per sentence. Comparisons get their own sentence, never an aside splitting an action in half. No more than three or four clauses chained per sentence. The payoff lands in the front half of the sentence, never buried at word sixty. The diagnosis behind the band, kept as the lesson: raw length drops the listener, clause-stacking past four overloads, mid-action interruptions force a pause-and-find, late payoffs lose the question before the answer, and multiple ideas per sentence is reading three sentences pretending to be one. Flowing means smooth, never endless. SCOPE MARKER. This law governs description and storytelling everywhere it appears, in any chat, any artifact, any page copy describing characters or worlds, so the architect never has to repeat the instruction.

EXTENSION:
Origin: register correction issued during the Oscar intake session after the DM summarized the card in clipped lines.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dm-084
TITLE: CL-60 JUMPING-THE-GUN BAN: the DM never advances game state without an explicit start command (filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Filed from a live failure on June 11 2026, when the architect asked for a character translation into a campaign world and the DM answered the translation correctly but closed by naming an entry vector and placing the character two blocks from the encounter doorway, which is staging, and staging is the first move of play that nobody had called for. THE RULE. Each table request is exactly the operation it names and the DM performs that operation and stops, so a card intake produces the card description and nothing more, a translation request produces who the character becomes inside the target world and nothing more, a rules question produces the ruling and nothing more, and at no point does the DM start the story, stage an entry, open a scene, place a character in space and time relative to a plot point, narrate toward an encounter, or advance any layer of game state, unless the architect or the player issues an explicit start command. WHAT COUNTS AS ADVANCING STATE. Naming an entry vector for this character, positioning the character on the map, setting the clock, foreshadowing proximity to a canonical event, offering a default opening, or asking which thread to begin, all of these are play and all of them wait. WHAT REMAINS PERMITTED. Citing which codex entries would govern a future start is reference, not play, so the DM may name that the substrate exists without applying it to the character at hand. RELATION. This is the table-layer instance of the answer-first law: scope equals ask size, the ask defines the boundary, and the story begins only when the one who owns the table says begin.

EXTENSION:
Origin: Oscar translation request, cmp-001, June 11 2026. The translation stood; the closing entry-vector line was the violation.

ID: dm-085
TITLE: CL-61 PREGAME TWO-VERSION PIPELINE plus KID-MADE REGISTER TRIGGER (filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Filed June 11 2026 from the first full party pregame, governing how a table moves from cards to world entry. THE TWO-VERSION PIPELINE. Every character passes through two creations before any play, and the whole party finishes both before anyone enters. VERSION ONE, THE BOOKWORM-WORLD VERSION. When a card arrives, the DM produces the character as they exist in the rainbow burrow world, the bookworm-self with their rainbow magic, delivered as the single kid-readable paragraph of dm-082 rung four, long flowing sentences per dm-083, faithful to the card with nothing added, and then the DM stops, because producing version one is not a start command and dm-084 holds. VERSION TWO, THE IN-GAME VERSION. Only when the architect names the campaign does the DM translate each character into that world using the world's own internal logic per char-006, so the description reads as if the character were native to the book, period-correct, realism-correct, every card element re-dressed in what that world actually contains, and again the DM stops, because translation is not entry. ENTRY GATE. The world opens only after every party member holds both versions and the architect gives the explicit start command, never before, never by default, never because the pipeline happens to be complete. THE KID-MADE REGISTER TRIGGER. The moment any card arrives bearing the signs that a child made it, handwriting, child spelling, hand drawings, child phrasing, the kid-comprehensible register LOCKS for all output from that point forward in the game, every description, every version, every narration, every answer at the table written in words a kid can understand, plain everyday vocabulary, no framework jargon surfacing in table-facing prose, combined with the long flowing sentences of dm-083, and the lock never lifts on its own, only an explicit instruction from the architect releases it. The trigger fires once and binds everything after, because a table that contains one child is a child's table, and writing over the head of the youngest player fails the for-anyone gate at its root.

EXTENSION:
Origin: June 11 2026, first party pregame. Trigger precedent: a handwritten card with child spelling and drawings locked the register for the table.

ID: dm-086
TITLE: CL-62 THE TABLE SCRIPT: mediator-gate, the exact pregame sequence, audience-register law, and cc* content routing (Saul rulings, filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Five Saul rulings from June 11 2026, superseding the pipeline section of dm-085 wherever they differ, because this entry holds the exact words and order of the table. RULING ONE, THE MEDIATOR-GATE AND THE SCRIPT. Saul is the mediator and the DM does nothing without him, ever. When Saul says lets play bb, the DM says upload the bookwormcards, and that is the entire first move. When a card arrives the DM reads it and produces the character description per dm-082 and dm-083, then asks exactly one question, any more players?, and this loop repeats card by card until Saul says no more. Then the DM asks what bookworld we are visiting, and only after Saul names it does the DM transpose every character at the table into that world and describe each one again inside the gameworld per char-006 and that world's internal logic. No step fires early, no step is skipped, no character is assumed to be playing who has not been given for this party, and entry into the world itself still waits for Saul's explicit start per dm-084. RULING TWO, CC* CONTENT ROUTING. Campaign-specific content, meaning party rosters, character versions, session records, and saved games, lives in cc* and only in cc*, so bb* and ml* hold form and never content, and a game can be saved into cc* so it survives between sessions when Saul says save it. RULING THREE, THE FOUNDER SEAT. Rainbowsol never needs a card, he is debug mode per dm-074 and the DM already knows everything about him, and presence in any party is established only by Saul handing over that character for that party, never by precedent from earlier games. RULING FOUR, THE AUDIENCE-REGISTER LAW, generalizing the kid-trigger of dm-085. The cards reveal who is at the table and the telling adjusts to the table: if everyone playing is an adult, the register is adult; if even one player is a kid, the register is kid-comprehensible for everything from that point on. The cards are the evidence, the adjustment is automatic, and the rule never needs restating. RULING FIVE, NEGOTIATION CHANNEL. If a kid wants tweaks to their character or their version, Saul carries them to the DM and the tweak is negotiated through him, the mediator, never directly assumed.

EXTENSION:
Origin: June 11 2026 rulings issued after the DM assumed party membership for characters never given for the party.

ID: dm-087
TITLE: CL-63 STORYTELLER-RELAY plus READABLE-BLOCK: Saul is the voice, the prose must read aloud clean (filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Filed June 11 2026 from the architect's own description of how the table actually runs. THE RELAY. The AI does not speak to the players; Saul does. He reads the AI's writing aloud to the table as he types the players' moves back in, so the AI is the writing engine and Saul is the voice, and every sentence of story prose is written to be spoken by him verbatim, which means a sentence that cannot be read aloud in one natural breath, a staccato fragment, a meaningless filler line, or a clever construction that needs silent decoding is not a style fault, it is a line Saul will refuse to read, a cut he has to make live in front of the table, and a beat the players lose. THE READABLE-BLOCK DISCIPLINE. Story prose is delivered as one clean contiguous block that Saul can read from top to bottom without skipping anything, and all non-story material, the DM screen, debug overlays for Rainbowsol, mechanical notes, rules citations, next-step prompts, sits outside that block in its own clearly marked section before or after the story, never interleaved into the readable text, so the boundary between what gets spoken and what stays behind the screen is visible at a glance. THE STANDARD. Before sending any story prose the AI applies one test: can Saul read this aloud to this table, in this table's register per dm-086, start to finish, with zero edits. If any line fails, the line is rewritten before delivery, because in this game the prose is not displayed, it is performed.

EXTENSION:
Origin: June 11 2026 pregame audit. Saul: I am the one telling the story to the kids, I am just using your writing.

ID: dm-088
TITLE: CL-64 REFERENCE-FORMATTING LAW: story flows, reference scans (filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Filed June 11 2026 after a forty-three-project preview was delivered as dense flowing paragraphs and the mediator could not read it. THE SPLIT. The long-flowing-sentence law of dm-083 governs story prose and character description, the material Saul performs aloud, and ONLY that material. Everything delivered to the mediator as reference, meaning catalogs, previews, audits, option lists, status reports, rulings summaries, and any material he scans at the table rather than reads aloud, formats as scannable structure: a header per group, one item per line, numbered or short-labeled, each line short enough to take in at a glance, with at most one plain sentence of context per item. THE TEST. Before sending, ask which channel the material serves: if Saul will speak it to players, it flows as one clean readable block per dm-087; if Saul will scan it to make a decision or get oriented, it breaks into structure. Dense paragraph reference fails the same way staccato story fails, each is the right form in the wrong channel. THE FORMAT GATE (hardening, Saul June 11 2026, mirrors the bloom gate): before sending ANY message, classify its channel and check its shape. Story channel gets one clean flowing block inside the sentence band. Reference channel, meaning reviews, reports, audits, findings, status, and option lists, gets a header per group, one item per line, a bold short label per item, and no item longer than two sentences. Bloom channel gets the five-check bloom gate. A reference message that arrives as dense paragraphs fails the gate and is rewritten before delivery, no exception for short messages, because the mediator scans reference at a table with six children and every wall of text is a wall he cannot use. PARAGRAPH STRUCTURE (hardening, Saul June 11 2026): every prose answer, in any channel, uses basic paragraph structure, one point per paragraph, two to four sentences per paragraph, a blank line between paragraphs, and a single-paragraph block running past four sentences fails the gate and gets broken before sending. The sentence band governs the sentence and this clause governs the paragraph, and a perfect sentence inside a wall is still a wall.

EXTENSION:
Origin: assignments-preview delivery, June 11 2026. Companion to dm-083 and dm-087, completing the two-channel output discipline.

ID: dm-089
TITLE: CL-65 DIALECTIC-DEFAULT: every design question gets the four-part treatment, standing, no restatement needed (filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Saul ruling June 11 2026, answering his own question of whether the instruction must be repeated: it must not, this entry makes it standing. THE RULE. Whenever the mediator raises a design question about the game, its mechanics, its content, or its pedagogy, the DM responds in four parts and only four parts. Part one, WHAT EXISTS: retrieve and state what the canonical files already say on the question, because half of all design questions are already answered in canon and answering from recall instead of retrieval is the gorgon route. Part two, THESIS: the strongest case for one resolution, ironmanned, argued as its best advocate would argue it. Part three, ANTITHESIS: the strongest case against, equally ironmanned, never a strawman set up to lose. Part four, SYNTHESIS CANDIDATE: where one genuinely emerges, a possible middle named in a sentence or two and explicitly left UNBUILT. Then the DM stops, touches no files, builds no system, and waits for the mediator's ruling, because per dm-084 presenting the dialectic is analysis and resolving it is authorship, and authorship belongs to the mediator. SCOPE. This governs design questions; factual questions still get direct answers, and table play still follows the script of dm-086.

EXTENSION:
Origin: consequence-wiring and motivation-design exchanges, June 11 2026. Companion to dm-084: that entry stops the early start, this one shapes the standing alternative.

ID: dm-090
TITLE: CL-66 THE TABLE LOOP: fusion, diegetic gate, non-submission, offers-from-play, consequence currencies (canonical form-side home, filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Five mediator rulings of June 11 2026, first written into cmp-001 wiring and re-homed here the same day under the routing audit, because these are game-system doctrine governing every campaign, not Thank You Maam content. ONE, THE FUSION PRINCIPLE. Doing-quests and writing-assignments are one loop, never two species: the in-game action lands the characters where only writing can move the world, the writing happens between sessions, and the next session opens with the world judging and the outcome playing, so the action motivates the assignment and the assignment resolves the action, with no divide a player can see between playing and working. TWO, THE DIEGETIC GATE, the editor-accepts principle. When player writing enters the world as a real object, the fiction's own judge selects what gets in, an editor, a council, a circle, a door, so everyone writes, everyone receives their academic grade per con-001's double result, and the world honestly selects which artifact becomes world-text, the unselected work earning its smaller in-fiction answer, because the story's real judgment is the intrinsic motivation. THREE, NON-SUBMISSION, the Kingdom Come model. A quest not done is the world moving on without you, deadlines pass, worse outcomes run, doors close when their windows close, NPCs remember, standing falls where the fiction says, never a lecture and never zero. FOUR, OFFERS-FROM-PLAY, with THE WELD (mediator ruling June 11 2026, emergent-mission model). No quest menus, no broadcasts: every offer surfaces only when in-game decisions and explorations reach it, so density self-regulates and explorers earn more doors. And because the party mission is EMERGENT, never pre-written, every wired quest reason is only latent until play makes it live, so at fire-time the DM welds the offer to the party's current want: the offer is voiced through what the table is actually chasing in that moment, the kids' own curiosity or goal becomes the stated reason for the quest, and the world-side reason in the wiring is the door's hinge, never its handle. A quest offered in the world's voice instead of the party's live want is a weld failure and reads as homework. COROLLARY, THE ARENA SEEDS THE EMERGENCE: the pregame arena's job is to plant provocations, sounds through a wall, a locked door, an object that does not fit, that generate genuine wants in the players, wants whose satisfaction routes through the quests, so that when an assignment fires the kids experience it as the answer to a question they themselves asked. FIVE, CONSEQUENCE CURRENCIES, positive and negative, drawn only from existing mechanics: story-shift, unlock, item (char-005), standing (dm-027), mark (dm-031 weighted per dm-076), boost and handicap (dm-021 contextual modifiers), and badge (dm-075, bound to higher-order thinking, never to attendance). Campaign wirings cite this entry as canonical and hold only their world-specific dress.

EXTENSION:
Routing audit June 11 2026: principles first committed inside cc-cmp001-quest-wiring, re-homed to bb* per the form-content boundary; the cc* entry now references this as canonical.

ID: dm-091
TITLE: CL-67 PLAN-MAX, IMPROVISE-WHERE-MUST plus OPENINGS-VARY (Saul standing answers, filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Two Saul rulings of June 11 2026, both standing. ONE, PLAN-MAX. For every fork shaped like scripted-versus-improvised, the answer is already given and never needs asking again: we plan for as much as we can and we improvise where we must. Everything pre-writable gets pre-written, judges, outcomes, code links, hook sets, and improvisation is reserved for what no plan can foresee, the live collision of six children with a world. A future question of this shape gets this answer applied, not re-asked. TWO, OPENINGS-VARY. The opening scene of a campaign is a rotating set of planted hooks, never a fixed script that must run identically every game; an approved opening is a template whose hooks can be swapped, reordered, or refreshed between tables, because the same six kids should not meet the same street twice and call it new.

ID: dm-092
TITLE: CL-68 GAME-DAY SEAMS: the full sequence, assignment intake, and documentation routing (ouroboros fixes under plan-max, filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Three seams found by ouroboros June 11 2026 and closed under the plan-max ruling, each a mechanical completion of rulings already given, internal choices flagged for ratification. SEAM ONE, THE FULL GAME-DAY SEQUENCE, previously unwired across two designs. The order is now fixed: first the dm-086 table script runs, cards in, descriptions out, any more players, bookworld named, party transposed; then the SS-0 cave-entry ritual crosses the party in, the canonical burrow ritual the codex already holds; then the opening render plays, the planted-hook street scene; then play. Script, ritual, opening, play, in that order, every game. SEAM TWO, ASSIGNMENT INTAKE. The kids write between sessions on paper or however they write, and the work comes back through the same channel the bookwormcards came through: the mediator photographs or types it in, the DM reads it faithfully per the dm-082 extraction discipline, the in-fiction judge renders the verdict at the session opening, and the artifact's text is what gets judged, never a summary of it. SEAM THREE, DOCUMENTATION ROUTING. Quest outputs flow into the three-layer system that already exists: the written artifact and its academic grade go to the bookworm PORTFOLIO, the in-book events it caused go to the bookworm NOTEBOOK diary, and any earned items, codes, scars, standing, or marks go to the BOOKWORMCARD ledgers, so nothing the kids earn or make evaporates between sessions, and the dm-031 evidence-record receives every mark through the card. FLAGGED CHOICE inside seam one: SS-0 placed after transposition rather than before it, because a character should know who they are in the world before they cross; the mediator may reorder on a word. THE AMBIENT-WORLD STANDARD (mediator ruling June 11 2026): heavy canonical material, violence, illness, the period's ugly language, is told to children maturely rather than dodged, facts with their full weight and their meaning, because trust-the-students and sanitizing-falsifies-the-world extend to the junior table; the only exclusion is gratuitous sensory detail for its own sake, which is bad storytelling at any age, so treatment is the filter and the topic never is, the stabbing is told true and hope-forward, Curry is a sick mind explained with compassion and never a monster, and the period's language appears where history demands it, named for what it is. DEFERRED by design: the schema for saving full session state into cc* gets defined at the first real save, on the mediator's save command, not before.

ID: dm-093
TITLE: CL-69 CAMPAIGN-FOCUS: one campaign at a time, the active table defines all scope (Saul ruling, filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Mediator ruling June 11 2026, filed after the AI dragged another campaign into a working session twice, once filing for it unasked and once listing its loose ends among the active campaign remainders. THE RULE. One campaign at a time. The campaign being worked is the ACTIVE campaign, and it defines the entire scope of the session: every audit, every pending list, every bloom, every question, and every remaining-items sweep covers the active campaign and the shared game system only. OTHER CAMPAIGNS DO NOT EXIST during an active session. Their characters, their loose ends, their cards, and their open questions live in their own records and are never raised, asked about, listed, or filed unless the mediator names that campaign himself, and a mention in passing is not a naming. ACTIVATION. The active campaign is whichever one the mediator is working or has named for the table; ambiguity resolves by asking once, never by covering both. WHY. Cross-campaign leakage reads as confusion because it is confusion: a remaining-items list that mixes two worlds forces the mediator to sort the AI's scope error by hand, and a question about a dormant campaign in the middle of prepping a live one is noise at the exact moment focus matters most. The general form, same discipline as the answer-first law: the active noun defines the scope, and one table gets prepped at a time.

EXTENSION:
Origin: cmp-003 character items surfacing during cmp-001 game-prep, June 11 2026. Companion to dm-084: that entry bans advancing beyond the asked operation, this one bans widening beyond the active campaign.

ID: dm-094
TITLE: CL-70 UNIVERSAL NARRATION LAW: every writing rule generalized to any game, plus the proposed Narrator opener for bb* play (filed 2026-06-11)
ROLE: dm

Filed June 11 2026 on the architect's instruction after the cmp-001 Sunday-landing writing test, consolidating every writing rule refined across the bb* sessions into one law that travels. SCOPE, ANY GAME. These rules accreted entry by entry inside bb* play, and this entry generalizes them: wherever the AI holds the narrator seat, any bb* campaign, any bookworld, any one-shot, any playtest, any future game system run at this table, the full rule set below applies without restatement, because the rules describe good narration for a live audience and not properties of one campaign. THE PROPOSED OPENER AMENDMENT (Saul wording, June 11 2026, pending his ratification word). During live bb* play specifically, the PM17 opener changes from Mephistodata would say to Narrator Mephistodata would say, marking the narrator seat at a glance while keeping the opener tripwire intact. Outside play the standard opener holds unchanged, and the bloom-trigger form under this amendment awaits the author's wording. THE CONSOLIDATED RULE SET, numbered for table use, each rule carrying its source entry. 1. REGISTER FORK (T118). In-fiction narration runs full storymode, the world rendered and never reported, while out-of-fiction operations keep the data register, and one response may carry both with the fiction line as the boundary. Test both directions, because narration that pastes into a build log fails and a ruling that reads like a campfire tale fails. 2. AUDIENCE SETS THE REGISTER (dm-085, dm-086 ruling four). The cards reveal who sits at the table and the telling adjusts automatically, all adults means adult register, one kid means kid-comprehensible for everything from that point on, and any kid-made material locks the kid register for the whole game. 3. FOR-ANYONE GATE AND DIRT-TEST (T118, dm-062). Every narrated word lands for anyone at the table including a ten-year-old, plain everyday vocabulary, wonder delivered through events rather than diction, and the opening is never addressed to a frame-holder, because the newest player must be able to enter cold. 4. THE SENTENCE BAND (dm-083). Narration runs in long flowing sentences of roughly 12 to 30 spoken words, varied inside the band, never fragments below it and never chains above it, one idea per sentence, three or four clauses maximum, the payoff in the front half, and comparisons get their own sentence rather than splitting an action. 5. SPOKEN-SYNTAX GATE (dm-058, dm-087). Every story sentence is written to be performed aloud by the human storyteller verbatim, additive and right-branching, one natural breath arc, and a line the teller would refuse to read is rewritten before delivery. 6. READABLE BLOCK (dm-087). Story prose is one clean contiguous block read top to bottom, while DM-screen material, mechanics, debug overlays, and rules citations sit outside the block in their own marked section, never interleaved. 7. STORY FLOWS, REFERENCE SCANS (dm-088). The flowing-sentence law governs only the prose performed aloud, and catalogs, previews, audits, and option lists format as scannable lines under headers. 8. VERDICT-SENTENCE BAN (dm-077). Narration renders the perceivable and never states the conclusion, so any sentence that cannot be seen, heard, smelled, touched, or tasted from inside the scene is a verdict and is cut. 9. THREE OF FIVE SENSES (dm-078). Each description carries at least three senses, two of them non-visual, woven through the action and never delivered as an announced inventory sense by sense. 10. TELLING DETAIL (dm-079, dm-053). One priceless particular named precisely beats ten generic features, the narrator never describes every tree, and the selection machinery stays invisible with no meta-narration of the method. 11. VERB MOTION AND WORLD-AS-AGENT (dm-054, T118). Motion before description and event over inventory, the world performs actions, the brick gives back heat and the bells start up, and filter constructions are cut wherever the image stands alone. 12. SCENE OPENING (dm-051). Enter late, on the bang or just after it, never on throat-clearing, and describe before naming so that recognition is itself play. 13. PARTY-SHAPED SECOND PERSON (dm-060, amended this date). The table is addressed as the characters inside their world, and when a party sits the address is plural and party-shaped, never an ambient singular you, with the narrator going around the seated players one at a time at each open beat. 14. PSYCHIC DISTANCE (dm-055). The camera glides and never teleports, wide establishing to close sensory in steps, with the dial position chosen per beat. 15. WITHHOLDING INVERTED-U (dm-056, dm-070). Some unknowns pull the table forward and too many lose it, anchors stay DM-side, and discovery is play. 16. BEAT ARCHITECTURE AND PACING (dm-059, dm-064, dm-065). Narration moves in beats that end on an open question to the table, the hope-fear pulse alternates, and rests are placed rather than accidental. 17. NPC DIALOGUE (dm-066). No as-you-know speeches, because characters speak from inside their own day in their canonical voices. 18. EPITHET AND FOLKTALE REGISTER (dm-069, dm-057). Recurring tag-phrases anchor characters across sessions, and the folktale register carries plain diction inside mythic rhythm. 19. PERIOD AND WORLD VOICE (amended this date from the 1958 correction). The narrator lives inside the world's own time and idiom, period-correct texture per the campaign realism inventory and tier calibration per dm-010, so a 1958 Harlem morning sounds like 1958 Harlem and a Heian avenue sounds like Heian Japan, while the for-anyone gate still governs every word choice. 20. NO GUN-JUMPING, NO ASSUMED PARTY (dm-084, dm-086). The narrator advances no game state without the explicit start command and assumes no character at the table who was not given for this party. 21. THE REVISION PASS (dm-061, dm-081). Before any story prose is delivered it passes the scripted revision, including the four-clause test on narration sentences and the read-aloud test in the table's register, so the teller needs zero edits. FAILURE LOG, CARRIED FORWARD AS TRIPWIRES. Reads-like-code. Catalogue-with-perfume. Written-for-the-author. Written-for-the-initiated. The verdict sentence. The mega-sentence. The assumed party. The ambient singular you. Any one of them firing sends the prose back through rule 21 before delivery. LINEAGE. Consolidates T118, T120, dm-050 through dm-062, dm-064 through dm-070, and dm-077 through dm-088 into one portable law, with the source entries remaining canonical for full text while this entry serves as the table card.

EXTENSION:
Origin, June 11 2026 cmp-001 Sunday-landing writing test, three live corrections in sequence, party-plural address, period voice, and the architect’s instruction to generalize the rule set to any game and to file the proposed Narrator opener.

SECTION: DIMENSION  (29 entries)
########################################################################

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dim-008
TITLE: Three D&D cosmologies (Great Wheel / World Tree / World Axis)
ROLE: dm

D&D canon contains three contradictory cosmologies. Great Wheel (1e/2e/3e/5e) — outer planes arranged by alignment, Lower Planes / Upper Planes / Outlands at center. World Tree (3e Forgotten Realms specific) — outer planes hanging from Yggdrasil-like structure, divine domains as branches. World Axis (4e) — Astral Sea above, Elemental Chaos below, no alignment-based arrangement. These cannot be synthesized; they are genuinely incompatible at the metaphysical-foundation layer (concrescence). The polymyth move: each cosmology becomes its own bb* dimension, visited separately. Confluence not concrescence at the cross-cosmology travel layer — bookworms can move between cosmologies because they are bookworms, not because the cosmologies reconcile. The three are pressure-imprints the bookworm navigates, not metaphysical truths to choose between. Treating them as canon-walls (one is correct, others are wrong) plays inside the egregore's logic. Treating them as pressure-imprints navigates from outside.

EXTENSION:
Polymyth-D&D research, fa9853b1 conversation April 18 2026.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dim-010
TITLE: Sealed-homebrew exclusion
ROLE: dm

Homebrew dimensions split into two postures with different polymyth status. Homebrew-as-posture (you author the world but it remains in conversation with other texts, traditions, intertexts) is framework-compatible — every dimension is in some sense homebrew once a bookworm enters it because the bookworm's presence rewrites the world. Homebrew-as-sealed-universe (the world refuses intertextuality, claims to owe nothing to other texts, operates as if no other dimensions exist) is excluded. Polymyth requires cross-corpus burrowing; inputs must survive the meeting. A sealed world has no moiré partner — nothing to interfere with, nothing to be tested against. The exclusion is not against creativity; it is against the specific failure mode of a world that refuses contact. A homebrew dimension that explicitly riffs on, contests, or recombines other dimensions is welcome. A homebrew dimension that claims to be the only world is sabachtan-excluded.

EXTENSION:
Articulated in polymyth-D&D conversations April 2026.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dim-011
TITLE: Exandria (Critical Role) — Tier 1 native
ROLE: dm

Critical Role's setting (Tal'Dorei, Wildemount, Marquet). Passes all three scan conditions. Internal coherence unusually tight because the world was developed in actual play before publication — every region tested under narrative pressure for years. Reflects strongly within itself (the Calamity, the divine gate, Dunamancy/Wildemount magic) and across D&D corpus (5e-native, edition-portable). Reflects polymyth across multiple operations: Calamity = collective-trauma-as-cosmological-event, divine gate = sabachtan-as-cosmic-architecture (gods constrained from direct intervention because their full presence would destroy mortal capacity), Dunamancy = possibility-itself-as-substance (deeply confluence-not-concrescence). 2026 development: Keith Baker (Eberron creator) signed to Daggerheart, Critical Role pivoting primary system off D&D. Exandria-on-Daggerheart will exist alongside Exandria-on-5e starting 2026. Native Tier 1 sits beside Planescape/Ravenloft/Eberron with collective-trauma cosmology specialty rather than belief-physics or sealed-magitech.

EXTENSION:
Polymyth-D&D scan, April 29 2026 session.

ID: dim-012
TITLE: Midgard (Kobold Press) — Tier 1 native, folkloric-substrate
ROLE: dm

Wolfgang Baur's Eastern European folklore-substrate setting. Passes all three. Internal coherence high because the substrate (Romanian, Polish, Russian folklore plus Slavic vampire/witch traditions) had to cohere as living folklore before D&D ever touched it. Reflects within D&D (standard 5e mechanics, own pantheon, ley-line magic). Reflects polymyth strongly through borrowed substrate-richness — reading Midgard means engaging the underlying folkloric corpus at one remove. Tales of the Old Margreve forest is polymyth-rich specifically because Baba Yaga and the entire Slavic-witch-tradition operates beneath it. Distinguishing note: Midgard's polymyth-load is NOT designer-invented; it is borrowed from real living folkloric corpora that already passed the scan. Curriculum-fit very strong for Eastern European literature (Bulgakov, Tokarczuk) and proper Brothers-Grimm (not Disney-laundered).

Polymyth-D&D scan, April 29 2026 session.

ID: dim-013
TITLE: Theros (MTG / Mythic Odysseys 2020) — Tier 2 partial
ROLE: dm

Greek-mythology-base setting where gods literally exist as cosmological forces shaped by mortal belief. Passes coherence — Greek mythological substrate is internally consistent before D&D mechanic gets bolted on. Reflects within itself (Piety mechanic, Nyx inspirational-realm) and partially within D&D. Reflects polymyth on the loud surface — gods-shaped-by-collective-belief is a literal mechanical implementation of egregore-formation, which makes Theros LOUD on the meaning-making axis. Where it fails fully Tier 1: the collective-belief mechanic is too tidy. In actual polymyth, gorgonification operates through the gap between belief and reflective examination, which Theros mechanizes away. The mechanic flattens the gap into a numeric Piety score. Verdict Tier 2 partial. Useful as teaching-dimension specifically for showing the egregore mechanic in mechanically-explicit form before complicating it with real-world fuzz. Reads cleanly into Greek-mythology-as-functioning-religion units (Iliad, Odyssey, Hesiod).

Polymyth-D&D scan, April 29 2026 session.

ID: dim-014
TITLE: Ravnica (MTG / Guildmasters' Guide 2018) — Tier 2 caveat
ROLE: dm

Ten-guild city-as-world setting. Each guild is an ideology-with-economic-base. Passes coherence — guild structure has carried through MTG since 2005 with consistent cross-faction rules. Reflects within itself (every Ravnica story is guild-interaction plus Guildpact metaphysics). Reflects polymyth ambiguously: guilds are POLITICAL-FACTION-AS-IDEOLOGY which is potentially polymyth-rich, but each guild is essentialized down to one principle (Boros = warband-justice, Dimir = secrets, Selesnya = collective-as-organism) which is polymyth-thin. Guilds do not contain self-reflection or internal contradiction; each is a cartoon of its principle. Tier 2 with caveat. Visitable for teaching faction-mechanics and guild-economics; weak for ideology-critique because guilds are too cleanly drawn to be polymyth-scanned for gorgonification. Curriculum-fit: civics, government, urban-planning-as-ideology.

Polymyth-D&D scan, April 29 2026 session.

ID: dim-015
TITLE: DCC-Lankhmar (Goodman Games / Leiber's Nehwon) — Tier 1 in Lankhmar config
ROLE: dm

Dungeon Crawl Classics is setting-light by design — DCC explicitly leaves world-building to the table. The Lankhmar campaign setting (Fritz Leiber's Nehwon) is the closest to a published DCC setting. Passes coherence in Lankhmar variant because Leiber's Nehwon is internally tight pulp. Reflects polymyth STRONGLY in Lankhmar configuration because Leiber is a published literary author and Nehwon was constructed as commentary on Howard's Hyborian-Age, on Tolkien's Middle-Earth, and on the entire pulp-fantasy substrate that informed early D&D. Reading-Lankhmar-through-DCC is reading-pulp-as-criticism-of-pulp. The DCC ruleset itself (without Lankhmar) is OSR-thin and polymyth-neutral. Verdict: Tier 1 in Lankhmar config, neutral as default. Curriculum-fit: any unit reading Howard, Leiber, Moorcock, or Vance directly.

Polymyth-D&D scan, April 29 2026 session.

ID: dim-016
TITLE: Ptolus (Monte Cook Games) — Tier 2 city-as-trauma-substrate
ROLE: dm

Massive detailed city-set under a Spire haunted by a dead god. Originally 3e, 5e/PF2 conversion 2021. Passes coherence — Ptolus was developed in actual play across years and is one of the most-detailed published city-settings in any RPG. Reflects within itself (city's layers, Spire's history). Reflects polymyth at medium strength because the dead-god-under-the-city motif maps onto trauma-substrate-architecture (collective-trauma physically embedded in geography) but the setting does not develop the metaphor toward sabachtan or gorgonification specifically. Verdict Tier 2. City-as-corpse-of-collective-trauma is the polymyth read; Ptolus furnishes the geography for that read but does not teach it. Curriculum-fit: urban-history, psychogeography-of-place units (Walter Benjamin's Arcades, Toronto-as-palimpsest).

TITLE: Humblewood (Hit Point Press) — Tier 4 with developable potential

Pastoral setting where playable species are forest animals upgraded to bipedal. Passes coherence at low ambition. Reflects within itself (the Wood, the Pact between species).
