ID: dim-018
TITLE: Strixhaven (MTG / Curriculum of Chaos 2021) — Tier 4 visit-only
ROLE: dm

Magical university with five colleges-of-magic. Passes coherence at low ambition — school setting with class schedules and exams. Reflects within itself and within D&D (standard 5e). Reflects polymyth WEAKLY: magic-school-as-Hogwarts-derivative does not interrogate the institutional form of education itself. Strixhaven treats academia as backdrop, not as polymyth-scannable system. Five colleges are glossy adjective-pairs (Silverquill = eloquence-and-conviction, Lorehold = past-and-present, Prismari = aesthetic-and-passion) rather than competing pedagogies that could be sabachtan-tested against each other. Verdict low Tier 4, visit only. Loses opportunity that an academia-themed setting should be polymyth-rich. Polymyth-rich academia-setting would explicitly thematize institutional capture, credentialism, the Arendt question of thinking-vs-knowledge, faculty-research-vs-teaching tension. Strixhaven does none of that. Curriculum-fit limited: only as lazy Hogwarts-substitute for younger students; cannot carry weight in any rigorous curriculum.

ID: dim-027
TITLE: Daggerheart (Critical Role / Darrington Press, May 2025) — Tier 1 polymyth-native ruleset
ROLE: dm

Story-driven ruleset by Spenser Starke. Hope/Fear duality dice (one twelve-sided die for Hope, one for Fear; player gets Hope-or-Fear resource on every roll). No initiative; GM-makes-moves-on-rolls (PbtA-influenced). Polymyth-relevant because the Hope/Fear mechanic IS a structural-encoding of the meaning-making vs meaning-subtraction axis. Every roll generates either Hope (player resource) or Fear (GM resource); the game balances these as opposing currencies. Closer to polymyth-native than any prior published ruleset. Hope & Fear expansion summer 2026 adds physical Fear-counter making the dynamic mechanically literal at the table. SRD released May 2025 (license-safe for derivative work). Verdict Tier 1 polymyth-compatible ruleset. Critical Role pivot away from D&D plus Keith Baker signing to Daggerheart suggests Daggerheart will become an industry-standard parallel-track to D&D. Strong candidate to BECOME the bookwormburrows mechanical default rather than 5e. See pen-007 for the default-ruleset decision.

EXTENSION:
Polymyth-D&D scan, April 29 2026 session.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dim-028
TITLE: Pathfinder 2e Remaster (Paizo 2023-2024, ORC license) — polymyth-aligned ruleset
ROLE: dm

Sibling of D&D 5e by direct lineage but mechanically distinct. Three-action economy, much more granular than 5e. Significant for the scan: Remaster explicitly REMOVED ALIGNMENT as a mechanical concept, replacing it with edicts/anathema (commitments-and-prohibitions defining a code of ethics that can change as the character changes). This is a polymyth-aligned mechanical move. Edict/anathema mechanically implements sabachtan engagement — character's ethical structure is a witnessable set of commitments rather than a metaphysical-tag. Verdict: usable as alternative ruleset for older bookworms (high school plus) who can handle the granularity. Worth running a unit specifically on PF2 Remaster's edict/anathema vs D&D 5e's residual alignment to teach how rules-design encodes ethics-design. ORC license (Open RPG Creative License) replaces OGL and is more stable for derivative work. See pen-009 for the teaching-unit spec.

EXTENSION:
Polymyth-D&D scan, April 29 2026 session.

ID: dim-029
TITLE: 5e / 2024 revision (One D&D) — default mechanical surface
ROLE: dm

Default-assumed mechanical surface throughout prior sessions. Bounded accuracy, advantage/disadvantage, simplified skills. Polymyth-neutral as a ruleset because the rules do not enforce a metaphysics — Inspiration mechanic is the closest the rules come to having a polymyth-relevant feature, and it is too vestigial to teach with. Caveat: 2024 revision quietly removed alignment from chargen flow (it remains optional, no longer a required field). That removal is sabachtan-aligned in spirit though not as decisively as PF2 Remaster's full removal. SRD 5.1 (Creative Commons BY 4.0, January 2023) covers the portion usable in derivative work like bb v1 character-creator. Verdict: default mechanical surface for bookwormburrows, with Daggerheart as the alternative-track per pen-007.

ID: dim-031
TITLE: Pre-3e and 3.0/3.5 — archaeological-only
ROLE: dm

OD&D (1974), AD&D 1e (1977-1989), AD&D 2e (1989-2000) plus 3.0/3.5 (2000-2008, the version DDO still runs). Mechanically incompatible with 5e. Polymyth-readable only as primary-source artifact for the history of D&D — Gygax's pulp-Tolkien-fusion, original Greyhawk, AD&D 2e specialty-priest era, 3.5 Forgotten Realms Time-of-Troubles to early Spellplague timeline. Polymyth-D&D scan, April 29 2026 session.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dim-001
TITLE: Text-as-dimension
ROLE: both

Any text with coherent internal logic is a visitable dimension. The text's world holds itself together while visited. Bookworm enters Hughes' Harlem, Shakespeare's Scotland, Wagamese's Fort Frances, Achebe's Umuofia — each dimension retains its own rules, pace, moral weight, language register. Rainbowsol does not homogenize dimensions into one operating system. Each dimension teaches the bookworm in its own way. Not all texts make good dimensions; some are too thin, some too chaotic. Rainbowsol curates which texts are worth visiting.

DUAL-LAYER OVERLAY DEPLOYMENT (reusable pattern for single-author-driven cmp-NNN). Any text-as-dimension built on a single author corpus can deploy a base-plus-overlay cosmology. Layer B is the real historical or fictional setting the source text is about, held at full realism intensity per dm-010. Layer A is the author textual-overlay version of that setting, the same geography and timeline plus author-corpus ambient saturation. Default state holds the overlay applied; the bookworm enters in Hughes-Dream-Harlem or Shakespeare-Dream-Scotland or Wagamese-Dream-Fort-Frances rather than in the unmediated historical setting. Canonical pop-mechanism: the author documented physical presence-location (Hughes 20 East 127th workroom for cmp-001; analogous author-location for cmp-NNN). Visiting it lifts the overlay; the bookworm is in Layer B base alone. Crossing back restores the overlay. Layer B base persists underneath the overlay throughout; the historical period material is layer-invariant.

SEVEN SURFACING FORMS (how the Layer A overlay manifests as findable in-dimension material). (1) Physical books on tables in apartments and reading rooms. (2) Poems clipped to walls in rooms where someone has read them. (3) Story-pages on typewriters in writing surfaces. (4) Song lyrics on radio and other audio surfaces in the period sound environment. (5) Passages read aloud by NPCs. (6) NPC dialogue spoken in the author text-canonical register. (7) Events from the author works happening to a different bookworm-perspective than the canonical foreground perspective. Each surfacing form is AMBIENT TEXTURE of the overlay NOT a portal mechanism. The portal class is named separately at ml* PM14 MATRIX anchor MIRROR-AS-UNIVERSAL-PORTAL CLASS sub-clause.

CAMPAIGN INSTANTIATION. cmp-001 instantiates this pattern for Langston Hughes 1958 Harlem at cc-cmp001-narrative-architecture MAY 10 2026 EXTENSION REVISED and cc-cmp001-hughes-corpus-overlay. Future single-author-driven cmp-NNN inherit the same pattern instantiated with their own author + setting + portal-location.

NON-INHERITORS. Multi-author campaigns (anthologies, era-substrates without a single author-presence), non-author-driven campaigns (historical events without a textual source), and campaigns where the source text IS the bookworm diegetic-world rather than an overlay-on-historical-world do not inherit this pattern. They use other text-as-dimension instantiation modes.

MAY 10 2026 ADDITION. Generalized from cmp-001 substrate per the EVERYTHING-IN-A-STAR-FILE-AT-SEMINARSCHOOLS DISCIPLINE futureproofing principle. Pattern available for cmp-NNN inheritance starting with cmp-002.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dim-002
TITLE: Playstyle-vs-lore axes
ROLE: both

Dimensions vary along two independent axes. (1) PLAYSTYLE: how the dimension handles resolution — story-privileged (quality of narration decides), rules-tight (internal consequences are strict), rules-loose (DM rulings dominate). (2) LORE: how much canon-content the dimension carries — canon-heavy (specific events must be honored), canon-light (setting provides tone, events flexible), canon-agnostic (only structural features preserved). Different texts position differently. Macbeth = story-privileged + canon-heavy at the plot-spine, flexible in scenes between. Icespire Peak (original campaign) = rules-tight + canon-light. Rainbowsol names the axes at session start so bookworms know which dimension they are in.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dim-003
TITLE: Dimensions in play
ROLE: both

Active bookwormburrows* dimensions. TEXT-DIMENSIONS: Hughes' Harlem (Thank You M'am), Shakespeare's Scotland (Macbeth), Wagamese's Fort Frances (Indian Horse), Achebe's Umuofia (Things Fall Apart). HOMEBREW-DIMENSIONS: Venus Island (Blob, Epic Cat, [REDACTED] Chen, Ki, Flying Squirrel Man). CAMPAIGN-DIMENSIONS: Icespire Peak (Rainbowsol running for existing group, character Samunovich the Bard). New dimensions added as Rainbowsol curates. No pre-set canonical list — the list is the currently-active visitable set.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dim-004
TITLE: D&D sub-worlds as available dimensions (non-ranked)
ROLE: both

D&D is a multiverse of coherent sub-worlds, not one unified canon. Teacher picks a sub-world; campaign stays inside it unless cross-dimensional burrows happen. Not ranked. Available sub-worlds passing three-tier + two-layer + sabachtan filters: PLANESCAPE (Sigil portals, Outer Planes, belief-as-physics, faction-as-ideology-made-material; Zeb Cook's philosophical substrate — factions map to Nietzsche/Stirner/Hobbes/Spinoza/critical-religious-studies positions; cannot be played as combat-game because belief is built into mechanics). RAVENLOFT (gothic-horror Domains of Dread; darklord's domain IS their psychology externalized; moral-weight as mechanic — Mists respond to moral choices; gothic-literary substrate — Stoker/Poe/Shelley; moral choices carry real geography-consequence). EBERRON (noir-fantasy magitech; surface narratives always mask material operations; Keith Baker drew on Chandler/Hammett, East India Company/Standard Oil history, interwar European anxiety; setting punishes taking-at-face-value and rewards structural reading). DRAGONLANCE (operatic-epic; three-moons magic + gods-absence-and-return as collective-consciousness operations; heroic-destiny bypass available so partial-forcing). FORGOTTEN REALMS (largest accretive setting; regional curation required — Thay, Waterdeep, Menzoberranzan, Myth Drannor are collective-consciousness-forcing; many other regions are generic adventure-backdrop; teacher curates). GREYHAWK (Gygaxian sword-and-sorcery; pulp-register; thin forcing but cultural-foundational for D&D-genre language). SPELJAMMER (crystal-spheres wildspace space-fantasy; travel-backdrop register; thin substrate but playable as lightweight dimension). MYSTARA (BECMI-era Known World; Immortals-as-ascended-mortals is potentially collective-consciousness-forcing but was never developed; publishing-dead with thin canon — room for bookworm authorship). BIRTHRIGHT (bloodline-inheritance-from-killed-gods; collective-divine-consciousness distributed into mortal bloodlines; publishing-dead; potentially polymyth-rich if teacher develops the bloodline-substrate angle). HARD-EXCLUDED: DARK SUN (fails sabachtan-exclusion; core operations — chattel slavery, racial hierarchies as metaphysics, defiling magic — are indefensible at operational substrate level; see sabachtan-exclusion principle in ml*). FR TIMELINE NOTE: Forgotten Realms has four mutually contradictory timelines (pre-Time-of-Troubles, post-Time-of-Troubles, post-Spellplague, post-Sundering). Treat each as its own micro-dimension. Teacher picks the century (e.g., '1372 DR'). Teacher does NOT need D&D expertise — AI holds the dimension-detail. Teacher treats each sub-world the same way they would treat any text-dimension: reads enough to run it, uses it, moves on.

ID: dim-005
TITLE: Dark Sun (hard exclusion from bookwormburrows*)
ROLE: both

Not burrow-able. Study-as-artifact only, if at all, and only for older bookworms with the frame-work to handle diagnostic analysis. REASON: sabachtan-exclusion principle — see ml* methodology entry. Dark Sun passes internal coherence (designers Denning/Brown consulted paleoclimatologists on ecological-collapse; the world's logic is tight) and passes the Yourcenar-test (real scientific substrate for ecological collapse). Under the three-tier text-selection rule ALONE it would be Tier 1 or Tier 2. But the setting's core mechanical operations REQUIRE chattel slavery as economic substrate, racial hierarchies presented as metaphysical fact (halflings as cannibal-savages, thri-kreen as alien-insect caste, human tiered castes, defiler/preserver moral-binary bound up with race and class), and defiling magic — casting spells by killing the land and the beings in it — as the rational power path. Cannot remove these operations without destroying the setting; they ARE the setting. Benefit-of-the-doubt, if extended, would affirm the operations. CONTRAST WITH INDIAN HORSE: Indian Horse (Wagamese) is dark content and Tier 1. The darkness in Indian Horse is the SUBJECT of the text; the text's operations are sabachtan-compatible — frame-break critique rather than structural endorsement. Dark Sun's operations are not the subject critiqued; they are the engine the setting runs on. Darkness-as-subject vs. darkness-as-engine. PUBLISHER-LEVEL CONFIRMATION: WotC's Kyle Brink (D&D executive director) stated 2023 the setting is 'problematic in a lot of ways given current inclusion standards.' Dark Sun has not been published for 5e. Bookwormburrows* does not revive it.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: dim-006
TITLE: Lençóis Maranhenses (biome-dimension, non-text)
ROLE: both

Burrow-able non-text dimension. The dune-and-lagoon field in Maranhão state, northeastern Brazil. UNESCO World Heritage Site 2024. 155,000 hectares. Three-biome transition zone (Amazon, Cerrado, Caatinga). Full scholarly and operational content in ml* Lençóis methodology entry and citation [48]. WHY IT IS A DIMENSION: the biome has its own internal logic that holds itself together while visited. Rainfall (~2000mm/year) raises the water table above sand level, impermeable sediment prevents drainage, lagoons form in basins between barchan dunes, dry season evaporates lagoons, wind migrates dunes 4-25m/year, endemic species (Pininga turtle, wolf fish) evolved to exploit the cycle. Coherent self-sustaining system, planet-scale pedagogy. WHY IT BURROWS STRONGLY (Tier 1 by three-tier and two-layer tests — see ml*): internal coherence (hydrology + aeolian geomorphology + biology interlock); external coherence (reflects Indra's Net as geometry — aquifer links every lagoon, wind regime links every dune, local state encodes global state across the shared substrate); sabachtan-compatibility (the biome does not close meaning; it is net-participating and teaches the student non-reduction between categories); Yourcenar-test substrate (real hydrogeology, real aeolian dynamics, real ecology — not genre-echo-chamber). WHAT BOOKWORMS LEARN BY BURROWING: continuous-variable reasoning. The student who enters Lençóis stops treating desert and lagoon as primitives and starts reading water-presence and sand-presence as the underlying variables, with biome-labels as post-hoc summaries. Indra's Net as geometry of reflective-correspondence (each node encoding all others through shared substrate). Shifting-mosaic steady state (stability at the aggregate that no single coordinate exhibits). Fuzzy-logic-as-research-program (textbook fuzzy handles graded membership within fixed categories; Lençóis teaches where that formalism needs coupled-node and time-evolving extensions to actually describe what the biome is doing). HOW TO ENTER IT AS A DIMENSION: Rainbowsol guides bookworms across the threshold. The burrow is into the biome as a whole, not into one lagoon or one dune. Student takes a bookworm-scale role — a small biologist on field research, a child from one of the living communities (Queimada dos Britos, Baixa Grande, Ponta do Mangue), a migratory bird arriving at the lagoons, a Pininga turtle waiting out the dry season. Character scale is deliberate: small relative to the biome is the correct scale for full participation. SESSION STRUCTURE: works at multi-session arc matching the biome's seasonal cycle. Session 1 = wet season arrival, lagoons full. Session 2 = dry-season onset, lagoons evaporating, dune migration accelerating. Session 3 = deep dry, community relocation decisions, wolf-fish eggs waiting. Session 4 = next wet season, new lagoon configuration, Pininga turtles emerging. The seasonal cycle is the campaign structure. CROSS-DIMENSION CORRESPONDENCE: bookworms emerging from Lençóis often carry forward net-geometry intuitions that activate when they later enter Planescape (belief-as-physics as the same substrate-coupling at a different variable), Ravenloft (Mists-respond-to-moral-choice as coupling), or any Indra's-Net-rich text-dimension. The biome teaches geometry that transfers. DISTINCTION FROM DESERT FRAMING: the biome receives more annual rainfall than Scotland or London. Desert by morphology, not by rainfall. The standard desert-wetland binary fails here on its own terms, which is part of what makes the dimension pedagogically sharp — students who arrive expecting 'desert' have their category dissolved by the operation of the biome itself.

EXTENSION:
Full scholarly content in ml* Lençóis methodology entry; citation [48] documents sources (UNESCO WHC 1611, Wikipedia, Live Science Dec 2025, Nature/Scientific Reports 2019, geologyscience.com, ladatco.com).

TITLE: All Summer in a Day - Bradbury 1954 - dim-032 (cc* cmp-002) - SCAFFOLDING STUB
ROLE: both

STUB. Saul-authored content pending. Per T115k cc* session-prep architecture, structural placeholder entry. The All Summer in a Day dimension is the second cc* campaign per Saul-directive May 23 2026. Ray Bradbury short story 1954 (originally published in The Magazine of Fantasy and Science Fiction March 1954). Setting: a future colony on Venus where the sun appears only once every seven years. The story takes place in a school classroom of nine-year-old children on the day the sun is due. Margot is the protagonist - the only child who remembers the sun from Earth before the family emigrated five years prior. The other children, who do not remember the sun, lock Margot in a closet just before the sun appears. After two hours of sunshine and play, the rain returns; the children remember Margot and open the closet. The story ends with Margot emerging into the dim rain-light.

CANONICAL POLYMYTHDND ANCHOR. The Margot empathy-bronze badge example per T114v. The kids-who-locked-Margot apology-letter assignment is the bronze-tier demonstration context (a poorly-written letter from the locker-kids contrasts with the gold-tier Roger-to-Mrs-Washington letter in Thank You M’am).

Detailed dim-032 content (room layout, NPC dossiers including Margot and the locker-kids and the teacher, time-markers across the school-day, object inventories including the closet, voice-samples, realism layers including Venus-future-colony-setting verified details) is pending Saul-authorship per T115k AI-builds-scaffolding-saul-authors-content protocol.

ID: bw-011
TITLE: bb* vs /bookwormcard/ vs /bb/ (three-URL architecture: operation file, game app, landing page)
ROLE: both

Three URLs under seminarschools.com share the bookwormburrows ecosystem. Each names a different layer with a different audience.

(1) bb* (with asterisk) is the operation file. The HTML lives at /polymyth/bookwormburrows/ canonical. bb* is the framework-internal substrate that defines bookworms, dimensions, eating-as-reading, the silkworm-to-cocoon-to-self-named-emergence arc, DM protocol, session structures, credit integration. bb* is primarily teacher-facing. It is the surface where teachers organize all the concepts they teach. Cross-references to ml* and mc* and cc* content surface here for the teacher who needs the whole framework in one navigable hub.

(2) /bookwormcard/ (May 10 2026 new URL) is the live character-creator app and future social-network surface for students. This was previously at /bb/ but the URL collided with the bb*-file naming convention. The game lives at /bookwormcard/ from May 10 forward. The matrix-aesthetic character creator runs here. Adults post AS their characters here on the text-only social media surface per pen-004. Under-18 character creation requires parent or guardian presence per pen-004 parental-presence design.

(3) /bb/ (May 10 2026 new role) is the landing page. Pure routing. Two cards on the page. One links to /bookwormcard/ for the game with copy aimed at students who want to play. One links to /polymyth/bookwormburrows/ for bb* the teacher console with copy aimed at teachers who want to organize their teaching of the framework. Anyone arriving at /bb/ gets routed to the surface that fits them. No characters created here. No content authored here. The page exists so that the previously-conflated /bb/ URL becomes the unifying entry-point for both audiences rather than the game-only URL it used to be.

THE ASTERISK-SUFFIX CONVENTION still tracks across the meaninglib. ml*, mc*, bb*, cc*, core* are framework files. Their unstarred counterparts when they exist are derivative public-facing surfaces. With this refactor /bb/ becomes the landing-surface for the bb* substrate. /bookwormcard/ becomes the game-surface that consumes bb* one-way. The convention is load-bearing because conflating these three layers collapses what each layer does and loses the substrate that makes the system coherent.

ORIGIN. May 10 2026 session. The user corrected an AI assumption that /bookwormcard/ was the character-creator. Original April 28 2026 framing from leizu-build-extended-3 had bb (no asterisk) named as both the social-network site AND the URL /bb/. The May 10 refactor splits the bb-no-asterisk layer into TWO distinct things. The game and social network move to /bookwormcard/. The landing page becomes /bb/. Three URLs. Three audiences. One teacher-organizing hub at bb*.

CROSS-REFERENCES. pen-004 (bb v1 deployed at /bookwormcard/, URL references updated from /bb/ to /bookwormcard/, retagged from pending May 12 2026). pen-011 (public-facing promises rule, applies to /bb/ landing surface after refactor). pen-012 (off-upload tracking entry for /bb/-folder-to-/bookwormcard/ migration and bookwormcard-game PDF URL update). ml* EVERYTHING-IN-A-STAR-FILE-AT-SEMINARSCHOOLS DISCIPLINE (Component B: all * files online at seminarschools.com; the tri-URL architecture is one implementation of that singularity).

MAY 12 2026 CORRECTION. Multi-line find-replace damage swept from this entry. Title-slot 3, section (1) duplicate canonical/legacy-mirror phrasing, section (2) previously-at URL, section (3) landing URL plus arriving-at clause, asterisk-convention closing sentence URL, and cross-references pen-004 + pen-011 + pen-012 all had /bb/ wrongly substituted to /bookwormcard/ at some earlier point. Fixed under audit-deployment-first protocol. _redirects file at site root confirms the canonical URL assignment.

EXTENSION:
May 10 2026 extension renamed from bb*-vs-bb to reflect three-URL architecture. May 12 2026 corruption sweep fixed multi-site find-replace damage where /bb/ instances had been wrongly substituted to /bookwormcard/.

ID: bw-001
TITLE: Bookworm (entry-level subject)
ROLE: both

Entry-level position in bookwormburrows*. A bookworm can burrow between soils — appears in one dimension, disappears, surfaces in another. This magical earthworm power is how any participant begins. The bookworm does not need to know the destination to burrow; the burrowing itself is the skill. Bookworms can enter books, apples, any self-contained dimension that has its own internal logic. Starts as larval: eats without designing. Becomes subject when eating is joined by designing. Everyone in bookwormburrows* begins as a bookworm regardless of age or prior reading experience. Cultural touchstone: Richard Scarry's Lowly Worm as children's-literature figure of small-scale confident participation across a world too big for him, whose mobility across every scene in The Busy World (named not accidentally) generates the reader-experience of cross-dimensional presence. The bookworm-inside-a-world pattern is textually present in the name-pair (Worm/World) even without explicit page-crossing mechanics. Lowly is theoretical-space-reference, not citation — Scarry's IP is not imported, but the pattern he exemplifies is acknowledged as cultural commons. A bookworm in bookwormburrows* is Lowly-scaled: small relative to the text-dimension being entered, which is precisely the correct scale for full participation rather than a preliminary stage to be outgrown.

EXTENSION:
Hey Arnold reference: worm inside apple, unexpected dimension inside ordinary object.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: bw-002
TITLE: Eating-as-reading (cannibalistic-reading)
ROLE: both

Core mechanic. Bookworm reads text, but reading here is ingestion not spectating. Text enters the worm; digestion converts text into subjectivity-material. What the worm eats becomes what the worm is made of. Standard reading positions reader outside text; analysis positions reader further outside. Eating-as-reading is inside. Hughes' Mrs. Jones and Roger become internal substance. When the bookworm encounters a parallel moral situation in a different text, it does not 'recall Hughes' — it feels Hughes as part of its own response. Test of eating: did the text change what the worm does next, or only what it can describe? Only the first counts.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: bw-003
TITLE: Designing-the-story-you-are-on
ROLE: both

Second core mechanic. Subjectivity move. A bookworm that only eats is a passive feeder. A bookworm that eats AND designs becomes subject. Designing is not inventing fiction — it is taking responsibility for the arc of your own becoming. What soils you enter next. What you refuse to eat. What you carry forward. What you leave in one soil to pick up in another. Pedagogical assessment aligns here: a student's work is evidence of eating (what they took in) and designing (what they are doing with it). Character choices, next-session requests, moral adjudications, long-form essay argument — all are design-artifacts.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: bw-004
TITLE: Developmental arc: bookworm → silkworm → cocoon → self-named subject
ROLE: both

Five-stage arc (April 2026 expansion from bookworm→subject to full silkworm geometry — see ml* silkworm-developmental-arc methodology entry for framework-wide version). (1) BOOKWORM — eats text, burrows between dimensions, not yet designing. Larval. Receptive subjectivity, takes shape of what it eats. No particularity yet. (2) SILKWORM — eats AND designs. Digests mulberry (text-dimensions) into fibroin (secreted substrate: essays, character-choices, arcs, homework, choices about what to carry forward and what to leave). What comes OUT of the student is recognizably theirs. First moment of particularity. Subjectivity here is productive — the silk is always OUTSIDE the worm; the student grows by externalizing digested substrate, not by internal accumulation. What bookwormburrows* previously called 'subject' collapses two things together; silkworm is the more precise name for Stage Two. (3) COCOON = HEGELIANEGIRL — silkworm wraps itself in its own silk. Previous form negated, next form not yet determined. Universal capacity for authentic subjectivity. The cocoon is built from the student's OWN digested substrate, not from external scaffolding — the institution cannot build the cocoon for the student. This is the stage where the teacher and the game STEP BACK. (4) SELF-NAMED EMERGENCE — what comes out of the cocoon is a particularity that names itself. Not a pre-specified moth. The name is the subject's first act; the subject comes into being by naming. An academy that hands its graduates pre-made identity-labels collapses this stage back into species-production. Emergence is by design outside institutional scaffolding. (5) EGGS-ON-MULBERRY — emerged subject's output becomes mulberry for next generation of bookworms. Their silk (papers, characters, modules, records) is the substrate subsequent bookworms burrow through. Pedagogical recursion closes. RAINBOWSOL POSITION (unchanged): Rainbowsol is Rainbowsol's singular founder/DM role. Rainbowsol is one name-out-of-the-cocoon (Rainbowsol's particularity at Stage Four), not a rank bookworms graduate to. Other emerged subjects name themselves under their own names. Growth continues indefinitely after emergence through further eating, further digesting, further secreting, and potentially further cocoons (multiple cocoon-cycles across a lifetime is expected rather than anomalous). WHERE THE GAME ACTS: bookwormburrows* directly scaffolds Stages 1 and 2. The game CAN scaffold cocoon-conditions (classroom allows withdrawal, individual work periods, student-held character sheets, minimal DM interference) but CANNOT scaffold emergence. Emergence is the student's own act. See Leizu-Academy-withdrawal entry in ml* for the institutional-design version. DOMESTICATION RISK (real): Bombyx mori the insect was bred to produce silk at the cost of flying and feeding — domesticated moths cannot survive. Pedagogical institutions risk producing excellent silkworms who never moth. Game design must hold this pressure; evaluating students on silk quality only rewards Stage Two and can strand them there.

EXTENSION:
Companion entries: ml* silkworm-developmental-arc methodology entry (framework-wide version); ml* hegelianegirl entry (cocoon-stage, self-naming); ml* Leizu mythic substrate entry (institutional design constraint); bw-002 eating-as-reading; bw-003 designing-the-story-you-are-on.

ID: bw-005
TITLE: Everyone makes their own character
ROLE: both

Non-negotiable. Each participant designs their own character from the start. No pre-fabricated party rosters for students to pick from. Character creation is the first act of designing — and therefore the first subjectivity move before a single soil has been entered. Character sheet held by student not DM. Evolution of the character across sessions is the visible trace of the bookworm becoming subject. Character-sheet changes = subjectivity-in-progress.

ID: bw-006
TITLE: Burrow as wormhole (worms burrowing between dimensions)
ROLE: both

The burrow IS the cross-dimensional mechanism. Not metaphor, operation. Worms burrow: disappear burrowing in, appear burrowing out in another realm. Wormholes at bookworm-scale. No hub, no transit-space, no Bookworm-Earth interior to traverse — the burrow is the crossing itself. Bookworms start with rainbow-magic (Rainbowsol's magic), which IS what lets them burrow. The rainbow is the signature of the dimensional crossing. CULTURAL-COMMONS PRECEDENT: rainbow-as-threshold-between-worlds is a cross-cultural pattern running through Bifrost (Norse rainbow bridge between human-world and realm-of-gods), leprechaun's pot of gold at rainbow's end (Celtic rainbow marking the fairy-otherworld threshold), Rainbow Bridge for pets (1959 grief-poem, now ubiquitous in Western pet-bereavement culture, explicit descent from Bifrost), Nyan Cat (rainbow-trailed Pop-Tart cat crossing parallel universes in meme-canon, cross-media cameo everywhere from Adventure Time to MCU to Android easter eggs), MCU Bifrost (explicitly identified as Einstein-Rosen bridge / wormhole). Four-plus independent egregores producing the same structural move — rainbow as signature of inter-realm mobility — without coordinating. Bookwormburrows* burrow-and-rainbow-magic inherits from the full commons-pattern, not from any single IP. The pattern is cultural commons; specific characters (Nyan Cat, leprechaun figures, Heimdall) stay with their owners. FUNCTIONAL CONSEQUENCES: burrows are cheap, repeatable, require no destination-mastery. A bookworm can try a dimension, leave, try another, come back. What matters is what they DO when they arrive. Cross-dimension travel is bookwormburrows*-native — the connective-tissue D&D settings (Planescape portals, Spelljammer wildspace, Ravenloft Mists) are NOT required for travel; those are in-dimension local-travel theories specific to their own settings. CHARACTER-TRANSITION AT BURROW: see bookworm life-cycle entry — character-jewel ends at the burrow, bookworm continues carrying subjectivity-material, new character forms on arrival in the new dimension. Rainbowsol (founder/DM of bookwormburrows*) is the one who holds the threshold across burrows — the rainbow-magic flows through Rainbowsol's authorial position. INDEPENDENT-ARRIVAL PRECEDENT FROM POP-CULTURE EGREGORE — STRANGER THINGS (Netflix, Duffer Brothers, 2016-2025): Season 5 Volume 2 (2025) revealed that the Upside Down is not a parallel dimension but a traversable wormhole-bridge connecting Earth (Rightside Up) to a destination-dimension called the Abyss / Dimension X (per Stranger Things Fandom Wiki, ScreenRant, ComicBook.com, Netflix Tudum, all Dec 2025). Three-plane cosmology: Earth + Upside Down (bridge) + Abyss (destination). Upside Down is the wormhole, not a world. Structure, not destination. The show's vines-and-tendrils-and-webbing are the crossing-signature substrate — per ComicBook.com, the Upside Down 'resembles Hawkins because it exists as the friction point where the wormhole pushes against the physical world, creating a distorted echo of the environment.' The threshold-flesh between worlds is Earth's pressure-imprint on the bridge's skin, not a duplicate Earth. This is structurally IDENTICAL to bookwormburrows* architecture: burrow = wormhole (rift / gate / wound-in-space-time), no hub-dimension, crossing-signature = substrate (for Stranger Things: vines; for bookwormburrows*: rainbow-magic), dimensions remain their own realms not nested inside a connecting super-world. Two independent-arrival confirmations: (1) bookwormburrows* rejected Bookworm Earth (hub-dimension worms traverse) and (2) Stranger Things rejected Upside Down-as-parallel-world — same correction, same reason. Note: Stranger Things characters THEMSELVES use D&D cosmology to theorize their reality. Dustin names the Abyss after 'chaotic planes of Dungeons & Dragons' per ComicBook.com; Mike/Lucas/Dustin call the Upside Down 'the Vale of Shadows' in Season 1 per Stranger Things Fandom Wiki. The children use D&D as interpretive substrate to navigate actual inter-dimensional events — which is precisely the bookwormburrows* pedagogical operation enacted inside a 2016-2025 mass-audience egregore.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: bw-007
TITLE: Character life-cycle (bookworm continuous, character local)
ROLE: both

Bookworm enters dimension → becomes a character appropriate to that dimension → character evolves through play → character can die. When character dies: bookworm spawns again. Spawn state: fetusy-worm-thing. Returns to pre-character larval pre-subjectivity-expression. Same bookworm, fresh slate for next character. TWO RESPAWN PATHS: (1) FRESH — new worm becomes whatever character they wish, no carryover from the dead character beyond what the bookworm learned at meta-level. No cost. (2) CLONE — new worm respawns as a clone of the dead character but carries a HINDRANCE that must be HEALED. Narrative cost, extra work, but continuity of arc. Both valid. The hindrance is dimension-appropriate (a Ravenloft clone carries a Dark Gift residue; a Planescape clone carries a faction-mark that does not match their new stance; a Macbeth clone carries a guilt-echo that bleeds into unrelated scenes). Teacher and AI together determine the hindrance at respawn; student plays the healing work. MECHANICAL INVENTORY AT DEATH: earned moves, items, power-slots belong to the CHARACTER, not the bookworm — lost at death. SUBJECTIVITY-MATERIAL (what the bookworm learned from eating the dimension's texts, encounters, consequences) carries — this is what the bookworm IS, durable across character-deaths. Teacher and AI adjudicate what subjectivity-material is, how it shows up in the next character. MECHANICAL INVENTORY AT BURROW: same rule. Burrow out of Macbeth into Planescape = Macbeth-character ends, new Planescape-character forms. Earned moves stay with the ended character. Subjectivity-material crosses. DEATH IS SURVIVABLE, STAKES REMAIN REAL: because respawn exists, death does not collapse the bookworm's arc. Teacher can let characters die without crisis. But the character CAN end — stakes are real at the character-scale even when the bookworm is durable at meta-scale.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: bw-008
TITLE: Silkworm stage (eating + secreting)
ROLE: both

Stage Two of the bookworm→subject arc, named specifically April 2026. Previously collapsed into 'subject' in bw-004; now held separately because the transition from eating-only (bookworm) to eating-and-secreting (silkworm) is the first move toward particularity and the game's pedagogical center of gravity. OPERATION: student has eaten enough text-dimensions to digest them into secreted output — essays, character-arcs, homework, project-deliverables, session-design, journal entries. The secretion is fibroin-analog: the input (mulberry = assigned text) transformed into thread (student's own voice, own structure, own argument). Recognizably this student's silk, not that student's, even when the input was shared across the classroom. TEST FOR THE STAGE: can the student produce output that they themselves, re-reading later, recognize as theirs and not as regurgitated text-dimension? If yes, silkworm is operational. If output is summarization, restatement, or parroting, the student is still in bookworm stage — more eating required before digestion produces genuine secretion. EXTERNALIZATION PRINCIPLE: silk is OUTSIDE the worm. Subject grows by what it externalizes as structure, not by what it accumulates inside. This contrasts directly with standard developmental models (internalization). The student's portfolio, character arcs, essays, module-contributions are the subject — not a record of the subject, the subject itself. LEIZU PATRON: the stage is mythically patronned by 嫘祖 Leizu (see ml* Leizu-mythic-substrate entry). Leizu Academy by name is the silkworm-stage academy. Seminar Schools parallel. Both institutions scaffold the digestion and reel-and-loom scaling of secretion. Neither builds the cocoon; cocoon is built by the silkworm from its own silk. GAME MECHANICS: silkworm stage maps to bookwormburrows* work-quality adjudication (con-001). Strong paragraph = silkworm-grade secretion. Weak paragraph = bookworm stage still operative, more eating needed. Degradation consequences (con-003) and marshmellowblob absorption (con-002) both indicate stalled bookworm stage, not silkworm failure — different failure mode. Silkworm failure mode is narrower: student secretes but secretion is not digested (output that looks like silk but is actually undigested mulberry — copying, paraphrasing without understanding, AI-generated submission without the student's own digestion). Fibroin-test catches it: does the secretion carry the substrate the student ate, or is it cocoon-shell without worm-inside? COCOON THRESHOLD: when the silkworm wraps itself in its own silk, the game steps back. Institution does not build the cocoon. See bw-009 cocoon-stage entry and ml* hegelianegirl entry.

EXTENSION:
Extension of the original bookworm→subject arc; silkworm is the precise name for what was previously conflated under 'subject' at Stage Two. Stage Four 'subject' refers specifically to the self-named emergence.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: bw-009
TITLE: Cocoon stage (hegelianegirl — universal capacity, pre-named)
ROLE: both

Stage Three of the bookworm→subject arc. The silkworm wraps itself in its own silk. Previous form (silkworm) negated; next form (named subject) not yet determined. Full philosophical content in ml* hegelianegirl entry; this entry holds the bookwormburrows* operational layer. WHAT HAPPENS: the student withdraws into their own accumulated output. Not literal isolation — emotional-intellectual withdrawal inside an ongoing game or classroom. Less interaction with the DM, less visible design-of-next-steps, less conspicuous engagement. Student appears quieter. Character sheet updates slow. This often reads as disengagement from the outside; in the cocoon stage reading it as disengagement and pulling the student out prematurely is the worst possible intervention. INSTITUTION STEPS BACK: Leizu Academy and Seminar Schools (silkworm-stage institutions) cannot build the cocoon for the student. Teacher recognizes cocoon-signs and gives space. DM continues to run the game but reduces direct pressure on the cocooning student. Other bookworms continue their own arcs in parallel. WHAT IT IS NOT: cocoon is not depression, not avoidance, not disengagement from the world. Cocoon is active self-enclosure in what the student has already secreted. The student is working on themselves using their own silk as substrate. Hegelianegirl is the shape of that work at the stage — pure universal capacity for authentic subjectivity, the previous form negated, the next form not yet named. CHARACTER-SIDE INDICATORS: student's character in-game may go silent too — not marshmellowblob absorption (that's Stage One failure, bw eats nothing), not character degradation (that's Stage Two failure, silkworm submits weak work). Character-going-silent in cocoon-stage typically shows as the character taking a contemplative in-fiction arc: retreat to a monastery, long journey alone, season of apprenticeship. The fiction tracks the student. Good teacher notices and gives the character space. EMERGENCE FOLLOWS NATURALLY OR DOES NOT FOLLOW AT ALL: cocoon does not guarantee emergence. Student may remain in cocoon across a whole semester. Student may emerge only after years, after leaving the academy, after multiple cocoon cycles. Bookwormburrows* does not set a timeline for emergence because doing so pre-specifies the stage and collapses it. MULTIPLE COCOONS ACROSS A LIFE: expected rather than anomalous. Subjects do not emerge once. They eat new dimensions, secrete new silk, cocoon again, emerge again renamed or with revised names. The arc is recursive at the life-scale, not linear.

EXTENSION:
Philosophical content in ml* hegelianegirl entry. Institutional design-constraint content in ml* Leizu mythic-substrate entry.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: bw-010
TITLE: Self-named emergence (Stage Four — particularity)
ROLE: both

Stage Four of the bookworm→subject arc. The cocoon opens. What emerges is a particularity that names itself. Not a pre-specified moth — bookwormburrows* rejects the moth-metaphor on purpose because Bombyx mori as biological species produces Bombyx mori, and the species-designation pre-specifies the individual. Hegelianegirl-as-cocoon removes species-pre-specification. The emerging subject names themselves; the name IS the act of emergence. ARENDT CORRESPONDENCE: close to Arendt's analysis of action and identity (The Human Condition 1958) — the who emerges in the act. The name is not a label applied to a pre-existing interior; the name is the subject's first act, and the subject comes into being by performing it. You cannot know in advance what name will come out. Indeterminacy is load-bearing. WHAT IT LOOKS LIKE IN THE CLASSROOM: a student who had gone quiet during the cocoon stage (bw-009) begins producing work that is recognizably ON THEIR OWN TERMS. Not following the assignment, not resisting the assignment — operating alongside it, from a position the assignment did not specify. Their character-arcs, essays, module-contributions start carrying a signature the teacher recognizes without being able to name it first. Often the student can name it themselves now: 'I write about X because Y,' 'my interest is Z,' 'I want to work on W.' The name may not be a single word. Usually it is a posture, a question, a direction. Rainbowsol is the name Rainbowsol came out of his own cocoon under. Other names are other particularities. INSTITUTION'S ROLE: recognize without pre-specifying. The academy records graduation and credentials; the academy does not hand the student their identity. Collapsing recognition and self-naming is the core failure mode for the institution at this stage. RAINBOW MAGIC (see ses-003): teachers running Rainbow Magic across multiple classrooms recognize emergence when they see it. They cannot induce it. They can hold the classroom conditions that do not prevent it. EMERGENCE IS NOT PERMANENT STATE: named subject can eat new dimensions, cocoon again, emerge again under revised or extended names. Multiple cocoons-and-emergences across a life is the expected cycle, not the exception. Emergence is a stage the subject passes through, not an arrival point. POST-EMERGENCE CONTRIBUTIONS: the subject's output at this stage becomes mulberry for subsequent generations of bookworms (Stage Five — eggs-on-mulberry). Students who have emerged often become informal silkworm-stage mentors for younger bookworms in the academy — their silk becomes substrate for the next cohort's eating. NOT promotion to Rainbowsol — Rainbowsol is Rainbowsol's singular role, not a rank in the arc.

EXTENSION:
Companion: ml* silkworm-developmental-arc methodology entry; ml* hegelianegirl entry; Arendt citation in ml* [20].


########################################################################
SECTION: CHARACTER-CREATION  (6 entries)
########################################################################

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: char-001
TITLE: Character-creation-as-writing-exercise
ROLE: both

First session of any campaign is character creation, held as its own session. Students write their character into existence through age-banded question sets. Output is both a character sheet and a first piece of writing assessed as writing. The two functions are not separate: how well the character is written is how well the character functions in play. Weakly-written character = weak in-dimension performance. Strongly-written character = strong performance. This alignment removes the 'game vs. schoolwork' tension at the outset.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: char-002
TITLE: Age-banded question sets (9-11 set)
ROLE: both

Six-question set for bookworms 9-11: (1) Who was your character before the story began? (2) What do they want more than anything? (3) What are they afraid of? (4) What skill did they learn from someone who loved them? (5) What do they carry with them always and why? (6) What would make them break their own rules? Each question requires 2-3 sentences minimum. Answers become the character sheet. Questions open expansion sets available as bookworm develops.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: char-003
TITLE: Character sheet as living document
ROLE: both

Sheet updates continuously as the bookworm plays. New answers get added. Old answers get revised when the character's development makes them false. Rainbowsol does not hold the sheet; student holds it. Revisions are visible evidence of designing-the-story-you-are-on. A sheet that never changes across a campaign is a warning sign — bookworm is not designing. Sheet change frequency is a Rainbowsol diagnostic for bookworm development.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: char-004
TITLE: Soul Anchor: four invariants the bookwormcard carries between books
ROLE: both

The four invariants surfaced during dnd-synthesis ouroborosanalyses. They are recorded on Series II Page I of the bookwormcard and persist across all books the bookworm enters. The AI translates them into each book's local mechanics at the moment of resolution.

(1) CORE WANT. What the character wants more than anything. Beginner: the thing they want. Intermediate: the want that survives even when they get what they thought they wanted. Advanced: the want their character does not yet know they have.

(2) CORE FEAR. What the character fears most. Beginner: what they would not want to happen to them. Intermediate: the fear that already shapes the choices they make. Advanced: the fear that is the same shape as the want.

(3) CARRIED OBJECT. The single object the character always has. Beginner: a thing they always have on them. Intermediate: the object they would go back into a burning building for. Advanced: the object that is also a wound.

(4) FOUNDATIONAL VALUE. The value the character organizes around. Beginner: the value they would name if asked. Intermediate: the value visible in what they do, not what they say. Advanced: the value other people break for them.

Translation pattern (see char-006). In 5e the book, CORE WANT becomes a Bond, CORE FEAR a Flaw, CARRIED OBJECT an inventory anchor, FOUNDATIONAL VALUE an Ideal. In Cairn the book, CARRIED OBJECT takes a slot. In Daggerheart the book, FOUNDATIONAL VALUE shapes a Hope card. The bookwormcard never has to know which book is active.

EXTENSION:
See char-006 bookwormcard system-agnostic, dm-021 AI math, dm-020 library-of-systems.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: char-005
TITLE: Items carried: rainbow-items vs consumable (three end-of-book modes, confluence-vs-concrescence at the item-crossing layer)
ROLE: both

The bookwormcard ITEMS CARRIED field splits at book-exit into three resolution modes. Modes two and three together form the persistent class, named RAINBOW ITEMS after the rainbow-crossing back from book to burrow at bw-006. Mode one is the consumable class. The bookwormcard surface therefore carries two top-level rows, RAINBOW (carry forward) and CONSUMABLE (one book only). Sub-modes within RAINBOW live as inline notes on the AI math strip. The player does not have to taxonomize their own inventory at entry time.

MODE 1, DISSOLVE. The consumable class. Used up in the book. No polymyth-item produced. Examples. A healing potion in a 5e book. A torch in a Shadowdark book that burns down in one hour real-time. A scroll read and dropped.

MODE 2, CONVERT. The book-item transforms in the crossing back to the burrow. The rainbow-version is what gets recorded on the bookwormcard. Examples. The witch cord from Macbeth becomes a marker of contact with the unseen. The notebook from Umuofia in Things Fall Apart becomes a record of what was forbidden to write down. The cigarette case from Wagamese Fort Frances becomes a rainbow-version of an object that holds someone else silence. The conversion is a teaching choice. The teacher and AI agree at book-exit on what the rainbow-version names.

MODE 3, REMAIN intact. The book-item carries through unchanged. It is recorded on the bookwormcard as itself. Two sub-types. Sub-type 3a, TROPHY. The item is commemorative, marks an event, has no mechanical effect but anchors a memory. Examples. Mrs. Jones ten dollars from Hughes Thank You Mam. The bone from a felled monster. Sub-type 3b, USEABLE. The item retains a functional capacity that operates across books. Examples. Mrs. Jones comb, advantage on first-impression rolls per the original Hughes campaign loot. A blade with sharpness preserved. A skill-token the AI translates per active book.

THE AI ROLE. When the polymyth-character leaves a book, the AI proposes the resolution mode for each book-item based on the item nature, the book chassis rules, and what the polymyth-character did with the item. The teacher confirms or overrides. Confirmed modes update the bookwormcard.

PEDAGOGICAL FUNCTION. The three-mode structure teaches the bookworm that not every encounter leaves a permanent trace, but that meaningful encounters do. The choice of which book-items dissolve, convert, or remain is a teaching choice. The teacher uses the resolution mode to signal what mattered in the book the bookworm just left.

CONFLUENCE-VS-CONCRESCENCE MAPPING. The three modes are the polymyth-internal confluence-vs-concrescence operation (dm-004) rendered at the item-crossing layer. DISSOLVE is concrescence at this layer. The item identity ends in the crossing, integrated into book-events and does not persist as a polymyth-item. REMAIN is pure confluence at this layer. The item identity is preserved fully across the crossing, the book-item carries through as itself. CONVERT is the middle case. The item identity is preserved AND transformed. The rainbow-version remembers what it came from. The transformation IS the marker of crossing. Both the book-context and the burrow-context are visible in the rainbow-version. See dm-004 LAYER 3 for the full layered articulation and see ml* CONFLUENCE-VS-CONCRESCENCE OPERATIONAL-DISTINCTION for the polymyth parent.

EXTENSION:
Rebuilt 2026-05-15 from May 13 chat content (chat 8b68f9c8). Extended 2026-05-15 with the explicit confluence-vs-concrescence mapping closing pen-002. The three modes ARE the dm-004 operation at the item-crossing layer. Engages bw-006 rainbow-crossing-signature for the class name.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: char-006
TITLE: Bookwormcard as system-agnostic + AI as system-translator
ROLE: both

The bookwormcard is system-agnostic. It records general invariants and history, not chassis-specific mechanics. The AI is the system-translator. It maps the card's data into each active book's native mechanical idiom at the moment of resolution. The card never has to know which book is active.

What the card holds (system-agnostic). Soul-anchor invariants (char-004). Items split into persistent and consumable (char-005). Training, equipment, knowledge in general terms. Scars and their narrative descriptions (not their mechanical effects in any specific chassis). Book-portal log of traversals. Stakes ledger of mission-failure costs. Birth data. Burrowing animal. Horoscope.

What the AI does (system-translator). At resolution time, takes the card's general data, identifies the active book's chassis, and produces book-specific contextual modifiers (dm-021). "This bookworm trained in scribing" → in a 5e book this becomes "+1 to history checks involving documents." In a Cairn book this becomes "test for forgery succeeds on a 4+ instead of 5+." In a Daggerheart book this becomes "you may pull from your knowledge deck before this roll." Same card data, three different in-book effects.

Why this design. (1) The card stays stable across the library, which is the whole point of having a persistent bookworm identity. (2) Players don't have to learn each chassis's schema — they just maintain the bookwormcard. (3) The AI absorbs the complexity that single-chassis play would distribute to the player. (4) Translation can be inspected by the teacher; the AI shows its work.

The bookwormcard does the identity work. The AI does the translation work. The teacher does the judgment work. The player does the writing and the choices.

EXTENSION:
See char-004 soul anchor, char-005 items split, dm-021 AI math, dm-020 library-of-systems, dm-018 teacher load-bearing.

ID: cred-001
TITLE: Module-mapping (modulecanon*)
ROLE: both

Campaign completion in bookwormburrows* maps to modulecanon* modules. A campaign that moved through Macbeth dimension + Indian Horse dimension + Things Fall Apart dimension covers identifiable mc* modules in English literary analysis, postcolonial reading, moral-ethical reasoning, close reading, frame-critical-literacy. SeminarSchools issues non-OSSD credits for these modules. Bookwormburrows* consumes modulecanon* one-way: the campaign accomplishes module outcomes; modulecanon* does not design campaigns. This preserves Rainbowsol's adjudicative freedom while making credit integration mechanical.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: cred-002
TITLE: OSSD pathway (pending Leizu accreditation)
ROLE: both

If Leizu Academy is accredited to issue OSSD credits, bookwormburrows* campaigns can earn OSSD courses in text-native subjects. Strongest candidates: Philosophy HZT4U (moral reasoning native to story-quality adjudication), ENG2D/3U/4U (direct English curriculum mapping with full specific-expectation crosswalk in modulecanon*), World Religions HRT3M, Classical Civilization LVV4U, History courses. Math, sciences, and languages are poor fits for bookwormburrows* structure and stay outside the credit-integration scope. Accreditation status is the blocker, not curriculum fit. **Curriculum maps live in modulecanon* (mc*), not in bb*.** mc* holds the OSSD crosswalk, the IB crosswalk, and any other curriculum-specific mappings; bb* stays curriculum-agnostic. Citation work and ministry-code-to-mechanic mapping for any specific curriculum is mc* territory. Campaign Codex (separate from mc*, still to be created as of April 28 2026) holds the adventure catalog — campaigns past and future, playable scenarios — distinct from the curriculum-mapping function.

EXTENSION:
cred-002 updated April 28 2026 to point at mc* instead of Campaign Codex per Rainbowsol architectural clarification.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ID: cred-003
TITLE: SeminarSchools (non-OSSD)
ROLE: both

Parallel to Leizu's OSSD track. SeminarSchools issues its own non-OSSD credits for bookwormburrows* completion via modulecanon* module mapping. Non-OSSD means the credit is institutionally validated by SeminarSchools specifically, not recognized as Ontario secondary credit. Useful for: homeschoolers needing portfolio evidence, students whose families want documented learning outside the public system, supplementary credentials for university applications where non-standard learning is a feature not a bug. Both tracks (Leizu OSSD + SeminarSchools non-OSSD) run in parallel, neither subordinate to the other.

ID: undefined
TITLE: Live app /bookwormcard/index.html SERIES + card_no schema deprecation
ROLE: both

LAYMAN. Pending-item entry. The body below specifies a work-item not yet completed: the substrate it operates on, the action-required, the blocker-status (AI-executable vs user-authorship-required), and its priority within the framework’s current build-state.

Bb*-app-internal schema decision. The May 13 2026 recovery batch renamed the print template's top-of-card metadata from "SERIES + CARD No." to "BOOKS COMPLETED + BURROW DATE" per Rainbowsol direction (the original labels referred to nothing). The live app at /bookwormcard/index.html still uses the old data-fields: data.series + data.card_no, with auto-incrementing localStorage counter at lines 1037-1061.

SCHEMA QUESTION. Three options.

OPTION A. Full migration. Rename data.series → data.burrow_date (ISO date of first save). Rename data.card_no → data.books_completed (live-derived from data.bookHistory length, currently non-existent). Migrate existing localStorage entries via a one-shot reader that maps old field names to new ones for users who have a v1 card stored. Schema bump.

OPTION B. Print-only rename. Print template uses BOOKS COMPLETED + BURROW DATE labels but reads from data.card_no (treated as books-completed proxy) and data.startTime (treated as burrow-date proxy). No live-app changes. Internal storage retains old field names.

OPTION C. Soft deprecate. Live app retains old fields and prints them under new labels; new fields not added; deprecation handled in a future v2 schema bump when bb*-related downstream consumers (Hall of Fame export, downloadable card archives) are also restructured.

DECIDING LOOKS LIKE. Pick A, B, or C. Default-suggested: C (soft deprecate) because the existing fields have no surface that the user actually sees under the old name anymore, and a hard schema migration is brittle relative to its benefit.

DOWNSTREAM. The print template currently shows blank for BOOKS COMPLETED + BURROW DATE because the data-field names don't resolve in the existing data model. Decision affects whether that becomes wired or stays blank.

EXTENSION:
Logged to ml* May 13 2026 from chat-only status. File-routing-rule remediation. Per the May 13 recovery batch, print template now reads data-field="books_completed" and data-field="burrow_date" which currently resolve to empty.

ID: pen-010
